# astro-ph.IM [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [OmegaNeuron: Applying GravitySpy Similarity Methods to the Search for LIGO Glitch Witnesses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23460)
*Bri Aleman,Derek Davis*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: OmegaNeuron是一个机器学习工具，通过整合GravitySpy的图像相似性方法和Omega Scan的瞬态分析，自动识别引力波探测器中的辅助通道噪声（glitch witness channels），从而提高引力波观测的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波（gravitational-wave）探测器的极高灵敏度使其易受短时瞬态噪声（glitches）干扰，现有工具如Omega Scan和GravitySpy存在手动检查或依赖大规模训练集的限制，需要更高效的自动化解决方案。

Method: OmegaNeuron整合了GravitySpy的图像相似性（image similarity）方法和Omega Scan的瞬态分析（transient analysis），通过机器学习自动识别辅助通道中的噪声见证（witness channels），并提供定量相似性度量（quantitative similarity metric）进行清晰排序。

Result: 应用于多个噪声示例时，OmegaNeuron始终突出显示合理的见证通道，与现有相关性工具（correlation tools）表现出高度一致性，并通过定量相似性度量提供更清晰的排序。

Conclusion: OmegaNeuron已集成到gwdetchar软件包中，能够实现更快速的分析，改善噪声见证识别，从而增强探测器灵敏度（detector sensitivity）和引力波观测的可靠性。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave (GW) astronomy has advanced our understanding of compact mergers through instruments like the Laser Interferometer Gravitational-Wave Observatory (LIGO). However, the extreme sensitivity required for these detections makes the instruments susceptible to short-duration transient noise, or glitches, which obscure GW data. Current tools such as Omega Scan and GravitySpy assist in identifying and classifying such noise, but are limited by manual inspection or dependence on large training sets. To address these challenges, we present \textit{OmegaNeuron}, a machine-learning tool that integrates GravitySpy's image similarity methods with Omega Scan's transient analysis to automate the identification of auxiliary channels that witness glitches. Applied to multiple glitch examples, OmegaNeuron consistently highlighted plausible witness channels and showed strong agreement with existing correlation tools, while providing clearer ranking through a quantitative similarity metric. Integrated into the \texttt{gwdetchar} package, OmegaNeuron enables faster analysis that improves glitch witness identification, enhancing both detector sensitivity and the reliability of gravitational-wave observations.

</details>


<div id='physics.app-ph'></div>

# physics.app-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Polyvinylpyrrolidone planarized liquid crystalline 1T-WS2/rGO hybrid nanocomposites-based humidity sensing platform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23385)
*A. Vasilev,M. Zhezhu,S. Gyozalyan,L. Avanesyan,Y. Grigoryan,A. A. Kuzanyan,A. A. Hovhannisyan,Mohamed Aly Saad Aly,D. A. Ghazaryan,H. Gharagulyan*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 该研究首次报道了通过水热法合成并利用聚乙烯吡咯烷酮（PVP）稳定的1T相二硫化钨/还原氧化石墨烯（1T-WS2/PVP/rGO）杂化纳米复合材料，及其液晶相形成和在湿度传感中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维杂化纳米复合材料结合石墨烯类材料和过渡金属二硫属化物（TMDCs），因其组分的协同效应在环境传感中至关重要。这些材料能解决单一材料的局限性，提供增强的灵敏度、选择性、表面体积比、可调电子特性、与分析物的强相互作用以及快速检测能力。

Method: 采用水热合成法（hydrothermally synthesized）制备了聚乙烯吡咯烷酮（PVP）稳定的1T相二硫化钨/还原氧化石墨烯（1T-WS2/PVP/rGO）杂化纳米复合材料。利用该复合材料固有的液晶行为（liquid crystalline behavior）形成高度均匀的薄膜用于湿度传感。

Result: 全面分析研究了1T-WS2/PVP/rGO杂化纳米复合材料的结构光学特性（optostructural characterization）和关键性能参数，包括响应时间和恢复时间。该传感平台结合了1T-WS2的金属优势、PVP的稳定作用和rGO的导电框架，形成排列的液晶结构，实现了增强的灵敏度、快速响应和环境鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 这是首次报道1T-WS2/PVP/rGO杂化纳米复合材料的合成、其液晶相形成以及在湿度传感中的应用。该研究为湿度传感引入了一种新颖的方法，利用1T-WS2/PVP/rGO液晶薄膜实现了性能提升。

Abstract: Two-dimensional hybrid nanocomposites combining graphene-like materials and transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDCs) are created using various synthesis methods and are vital for environmental sensing due to the synergistic effects of their components. These hybrid materials offer enhanced sensitivity, selectivity, surface-to-volume ratio, tunable electronic properties, strong interaction with analytes, and fast detection capabilities, which address the limitations of individual materials. This is due to their outstanding surface-to-volume ratio, tunable electronic properties, strong interactions with analytes, as well as their high sensitivity, selectivity, and fast detection capabilities, which are crucial for environmental sensing. Herein, a hydrothermally synthesized and polyvinylpyrrolidone (PVP)-stabilized 1T phase tungsten disulfide/reduced graphene oxide, 1T-WS2/PVP/rGO, hybrid nanocomposite is reported. The intrinsic liquid crystalline behavior of the synthesized composite enables the formation of highly uniform films for effective humidity sensing. The optostructural characterization and key performance parameters, including response and recovery times, of the 1T-WS2/PVP/rGO hybrid nanocomposite-based structure are comprehensively analyzed and studied. This is the first to report on the synthesis of a 1T-WS2/PVP/rGO hybrid nanocomposite, its liquid crystalline phase formation, and application in humidity sensing. The proposed sensing platform introduces a novel approach to humidity sensing using 1T-WS2/PVP/rGO liquid crystalline films, which combine the metallic advantages of 1T-WS2, the stabilizing role of PVP and the conductive framework of rGO into aligned LC structures for enhanced sensitivity, rapid response and environmental robustness.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.mtrl-sci'></div>

# cond-mat.mtrl-sci [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [A high-performance cobalt-free cathode for proton-conducting solid oxide fuel cells via multi-element doping in Sr2Fe2O6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23399)
*Le Zhou,Yanru Yin,Dilshod Nematov,Hailu Dai,Yuyuan Gu,Shoufu Yu,Lei Bi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究提出并验证了一种多元素掺杂策略，用于提升Sr2Fe2O6基铁酸盐作为质子传导固体氧化物燃料电池阴极的性能。通过设计合成Sr2Fe1.5Mo0.125Sn0.125Sc0.125Zr0.125O6材料，显著增强了氧和质子传输动力学，实现了优异的电化学性能和长期稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发高效稳定的中温固体氧化物燃料电池（SOFCs）需要高性能、无钴、成本效益高且与质子传导电解质兼容的阴极材料。虽然Sr2Fe2O6基铁酸盐提供了有前景的无钴替代方案，但其电化学性能需要进一步提升以与最先进的阴极竞争。

Method: 本研究提出并验证了多元素掺杂策略作为定制SFO性能的优越方法。具体设计了Sr2Fe1.5Mo0.125Sn0.125Sc0.125Zr0.125O6氧化物，通过固相反应法合成，并系统评估其作为质子传导SOFCs阴极的性能。其性能与一系列单掺杂（Mo、Sn、Sc、Zr）改性的SFO阴极进行了基准比较。

Result: 结构表征证实成功形成了相纯的钙钛矿结构且元素分布均匀。电导率弛豫测量显示，SFO-ZSSM相比所有单掺杂对应物表现出显著增强的氧和质子传输动力学，显示出明显的协同效应。采用SFO-ZSSM阴极的燃料电池在700、650和600°C下分别实现了1580、1137和854 mW cm-2的优异峰值功率密度，显著优于单掺杂阴极电池。电化学阻抗谱进一步证实了其优越的催化活性，显示出最低的极化电阻。

Conclusion: SFO-ZSSM电池在100小时内表现出优异的操作稳定性，这归因于其坚固的微观结构和无钡组成。多元素掺杂策略被证明是提升SFO基阴极性能的有效方法，为开发高性能无钴阴极材料提供了重要途径。

Abstract: The development of efficient and stable intermediate-temperature solid oxide fuel cells (SOFCs) necessitates high-performance cathode materials that are cobalt-free, cost-effective, and compatible with proton-conducting electrolytes. While Sr2Fe2O6 (SFO)-based ferrites offer a promising cobalt-free alternative, their electrochemical performance requires further enhancement to compete with state-of-the-art cathodes. This study proposes and validates a multi-element doping strategy as a superior approach to tailor the properties of SFO. The specific oxide Sr2Fe1.5Mo0.125Sn0.125Sc0.125Zr0.125O6 (SFO-ZSSM) is designed, synthesized via a solid-state reaction method, and systematically evaluated as a cathode for proton-conducting SOFCs (H-SOFCs). Its performance is benchmarked against a series of SFO cathodes modified with single dopants (Mo, Sn, Sc, Zr). Structural characterization confirms the successful formation of a phase-pure perovskite structure with homogeneous elemental distribution. Electrical conductivity relaxation (ECR) measurements reveal that SFO-ZSSM exhibits dramatically enhanced oxygen and proton transport kinetics compared to all singly-doped counterparts, demonstrating a significant synergistic effect. Consequently, fuel cells employing the SFO-ZSSM cathode deliver exceptional peak power densities of 1580, 1137, and 854 mW cm-2 at 700, 650, and 600 °C, respectively, significantly outperforming cells with single-doped cathodes. Electrochemical impedance spectroscopy further corroborates its superior catalytic activity, showing the lowest polarization resistance. Moreover, the SFO-ZSSM cell demonstrates excellent operational stability over 100 hours, attributed to its robust microstructure and Ba-free composition.

</details>


### [4] [Band Renormalization in Metal-Organic Framework/Au(111) Epitaxial Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23441)
*Xiaoqing Yuan,Shaoze Wang,Xiaoyue He,Zhecheng Sun,Lei Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过扫描隧道显微表征和紧束缚分析，揭示了M3(HITP)2/Au(111)异质结构的界面耦合机制，包括衬底对金属有机框架电子结构的重整化效应以及框架对金表面电子态的量子限制作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维共轭金属有机框架（2D conjugated metal-organic frameworks）在化学电阻传感、电催化和能量存储等领域具有广阔应用前景。然而，其与金属电极的界面相互作用（interfacial interaction）对电子性质和器件性能至关重要，但微观机制尚不明确，特别是M3(HITP)2/metal异质结构的界面相互作用机制。

Method: 研究采用扫描隧道显微表征（scanning tunneling microscopic characterization）和紧束缚分析（tight-binding analysis）方法，对在Au(111)衬底上外延生长的单层M3(HITP)2（M = Ni, Cu）进行系统研究。通过扫描隧道谱映射（scanning tunneling spectroscopic mapping）揭示其晶格结构。

Result: 研究发现M3(HITP)2/Au(111)异质结构具有公度kagome-hexagonal-honeycomb三重晶格架构（commensurate kagome-hexagonal-honeycomb triple-lattice architecture）。Au(111)衬底重整化了M3(HITP)2的电子能带结构（renormalizes the electronic band structure），钉扎了费米能级（pinning the Fermi level），并在0.4 eV处产生配体衍生的平带（ligand-derived flat band）。同时，M3(HITP)2晶格通过电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）和量子限制（quantum confinement）强烈调制Au(111)的表面电子态，形成量子围栏网络（quantum corral network）。

Conclusion: 该原子尺度研究阐明了M3(HITP)2/Au(111)外延异质结构的层间耦合机制（interlayer coupling mechanisms），推进了对金属有机框架/金属界面相互作用的理解，这对电子和能量存储器件至关重要。研究发现形成完全色散的电子能带和稳健的量子围栏网络需要至少包含十个孔的晶粒。

Abstract: Two-dimensional conjugated metal-organic frameworks hold great promise for applications in chemiresistive sensing, electrocatalysis, and energy storage. Their interfacial interaction with metal electrodes, which has been rarely investigated, exerts a critical influence on the electronic properties and device performance. As a representative material, M3(HITP)2 (M = Ni, Cu; HITP = 2,3,6,7,10,11-hexaiminotriphenylene) exhibits excellent performance in various electronic devices, yet the microscopic mechanism of the interfacial interaction in M3(HITP)2/metal heterostructures remains unclear. Here, we report the synthesis, scanning tunneling microscopic characterization, and tight-binding analysis of monolayer M3(HITP)2 epitaxially grown on Au(111). Scanning tunneling spectroscopic mapping reveals a commensurate kagome-hexagonal-honeycomb triple-lattice architecture. The Au(111) substrate renormalizes the electronic band structure of M3(HITP)2, pinning the Fermi level and generating a ligand-derived flat band at 0.4 eV that corrects prior misassignment of orbital character. Meanwhile, the periodic and microporous M3(HITP)2 lattice strongly modulates the surface electronic state of Au(111) via electron-phonon coupling and quantum confinement, the latter of which gives rise to a quantum corral network exhibiting two resonant states within each pore. The formation of fully dispersive electronic bands and the robust quantum corral network requires crystallites comprising at least ten pores. The atomic-scale investigation of M3(HITP)2/Au(111) epitaxial heterostructures elucidates interlayer coupling mechanisms and advances the understanding of metal-organic framework/metal interfaces that are integral to electronic and energy-storage devices.

</details>


### [5] [Exploring the extremes: atomic basis for multi-elemental materials science under complex thermodynamic conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23489)
*Anton Bochkarev,Yury Lysogorskiy,Aparna Subramanyam,Ralf Drautz,Danny Perez*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种化学无关、信息熵最大化的数据生成协议（SMAX），用于解决传统机器学习原子间势在复杂多元素体系中的失效问题，显著提升了模型在极端条件和远离平衡态体系中的预测鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代材料科学面临从传统高纯度、少元素体系向复杂多元素体系（Mendeleev materials）的转变需求，特别是在循环经济和极端条件应用背景下。传统机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potentials）在复杂化学体系中经常失效，主要原因是训练数据集存在系统性偏差，过度强调低能量、近平衡结构。

Method: 引入了一种化学无关、信息熵最大化的数据生成协议（chemistry-agnostic, information-entropy-maximization protocol），通过将结构采样与热力学偏差解耦，为整个元素周期表的原子相互作用提供稳健的物理先验。基于生成的统计最大化熵数据集（SMAX dataset）训练图原子团簇展开模型（Graph Atomic Cluster Expansion, GRACE）。

Result: 在多个严格基准测试中显示出显著改进的鲁棒性，包括锡的大应变相变、钨基合金的缺陷演化以及催化反应势垒预测。该方法能够自主解析多元素混合物中的涌现结构，如包含地壳中九种最丰富元素的体系，无需依赖先验化学假设。

Conclusion: 该方法为导航未来材料设计相关的广阔化学和构型空间建立了可扩展的原则性方法，实现了"通过模拟发现"的新范式，使无偏采样协议能够自主解析多元素混合物中的涌现结构。

Abstract: Modern materials science has historically been founded on combining restricted subsets of the periodic table, favoring high-purity, few-element systems. However, the demands of an emerging circular economy, together with the need to understand materials behavior under planetary and industrial extremes, increasingly require mastering Mendeleev materials - chemically and structurally complex systems that span large portions of the periodic table. In these regimes, current universal machine-learning interatomic potentials often fail, largely due to systematic gaps in traditional training datasets that heavily emphasize low-energy, near-equilibrium structures. We address this limitation by introducing a chemistry-agnostic, information-entropy-maximization protocol for data generation. By decoupling structural sampling from thermodynamic bias, our approach provides a robust physical prior for atomic interactions across the entire periodic table, including regimes far from equilibrium and under extreme conditions. Training a Graph Atomic Cluster Expansion (GRACE) model on the resulting statistically maximized entropy (SMAX) dataset yields markedly improved robustness across a range of stringent benchmarks. These include large-strain phase transformations in tin, defect evolution in tungsten-based alloys, and catalytic reaction barrier prediction. More broadly, our approach establishes a scalable and principled methodology for navigating the vast chemical and configurational space relevant to future materials design. It enables a paradigm of discovery by simulation in which unbiased sampling protocols autonomously resolve emergent structures in multi-elemental mixtures-such as systems containing the nine most abundant elements in the Earth's crust-without reliance on a priori chemical assumptions.

</details>


### [6] [Defect-Engineered h-BN as a Platform for Single-Atom HER Catalysts: Descriptor Screening Refined by Electrochemical Stability Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23493)
*Ana S. Dobrota,Natalia V. Skorodumova,Igor A. Pašti*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过密度泛函理论（DFT）筛选六方氮化硼（h-BN）缺陷锚定的单原子催化剂用于析氢反应（HER），发现基于吸附自由能的初步筛选需结合电化学稳定性分析才能识别真正稳健的体系，最终确定Pd@VB为最优候选。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺陷工程使六方氮化硼（h-BN）能够作为稳定孤立金属原子的平台，但系统识别具有催化活性的结构仍然有限。需要开发系统方法筛选h-BN缺陷锚定的单原子催化剂用于析氢反应（HER）。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）筛选过渡金属和贵金属在h-BN的B空位、N空位和BN空位锚定的单原子催化剂。通过内聚能基准测试评估热力学稳定性，电子结构分析研究导电性和金属电荷态，氢吸附自由能筛选HER活性，并引入Pourbaix分析评估电化学稳定性。

Result: B空位为单原子提供最强的热力学稳定作用，空位类型调控导电性和金属电荷态。氢吸附自由能筛选出Cu@VN和Pd@VB为接近热中性的候选物，与Pt(111)相当。Pourbaix分析表明Cu@VN在低pH下不稳定且易受OHads毒化，而Pd@VB在宽电位-pH范围内保持稳定且具有催化可及性。

Conclusion: 基于描述符的HER筛选可扩展候选物池，但严格的电化学过滤对于识别真正稳健的体系至关重要。提出的多步策略为缺陷工程二维（2D）载体上单原子催化剂的理性发现提供了通用框架。

Abstract: Defect engineering enables hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) to act as a platform for stabilizing isolated metal atoms, yet systematic identification of catalytically viable motifs remains limited. Here, density functional theory is used to screen transition and coinage metals anchored at B, N, and BN vacancies in h-BN for hydrogen evolution reaction (HER) activity. Cohesive-energy benchmarking reveals that B vacancies provide the strongest thermodynamic stabilization of single atoms, while electronic-structure analysis demonstrates vacancy-dependent modulation of conductivity and metal charge state. Hydrogen adsorption free energies identify Cu@VN and Pd@VB as near-thermoneutral candidates comparable to Pt(111). However, incorporation of electrochemical stability through Pourbaix analysis significantly refines this selection: Cu@VN is unstable at low pH and susceptible to OHads poisoning, whereas Pd@VB remains stable and catalytically accessible across a broad potential-pH range. These results show that descriptor-based HER screening can generate an expanded pool of candidates, but rigorous electrochemical filtering is essential to identify truly robust systems. The presented multi-step strategy provides a general framework for rational discovery of single-atom catalysts on defect-engineered 2D supports.

</details>


### [7] [Strain patterning of flexomagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23494)
*Tamalika Samanta,Zachary T. LaDuca,An-Hsi Chen,Sangsoo Kim,Ying-Ting Chan,Jiaxuan Wu,Yujia Teng,Debarghya Mallick,Matthew Brahlek,T. Zac Ward,Katherine Su,Jia-Mian Hu,Weida Wu,Turan Birol,Hanfei Yan,Michael S. Arnold,Karin M. Rabe,Jason K. Kawasaki*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种通过氦离子注入和光刻掩模图案化横向应变梯度的方法，在反铁磁节线半金属GdAuGe外延薄膜中实现了室温附近的铁磁响应，证实了应变梯度诱导的挠曲磁效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挠曲磁效应（flexomagnetism）——磁有序与应变梯度的耦合——能够实现均匀应变无法达到的新型对称破缺磁相。然而，由于空间变化应变的控制极为困难，挠曲磁效应难以理解。

Method: 研究开发了一种自上而下的策略，通过光刻定义的掩模进行氦离子注入来图案化横向应变梯度。使用反铁磁节线半金属（antiferromagnetic nodal line semimetal）GdAuGe的外延薄膜，通过磁力显微镜（magnetic force microscopy）和纳米束X射线衍射（nanobeam x-ray diffraction）分别将磁响应与最大应变梯度区域进行空间关联。

Result: 横向应变梯度∂εzz/∂x在GdAuGe中诱导了接近室温的铁磁响应，而均匀应变的GdAuGe则保持顺磁或反铁磁性。通过空间关联证实了挠曲磁响应。

Conclusion: 该方法为通过图案化应变梯度精确控制量子材料薄膜中的磁相开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Flexomagnetism, the coupling of magnetic ordering to strain gradients, provides access to novel symmetry-broken magnetic phases that cannot be accessed via uniform strain. However, flexomagnetism is hard to understand because it is extremely difficult to control a spatially varying strain. Here, we develop a top-down strategy to pattern transverse strain gradients using helium ion implantation through a lithographically defined mask. Using epitaxial films of the antiferromagnetic nodal line semimetal GdAuGe, we demonstrate that transverse strain gradients $\partial \varepsilon_{zz}/\partial x$ induce near-room-temperature ferromagnetic response, compared to the retained para or antiferromagnetism for homogeneously strained GdAuGe. We spatially correlate the magnetic response with the regions of largest strain gradient, via magnetic force microscopy and nanobeam x-ray diffraction, respectively, to confirm the flexomagnetic response. Our approach opens new avenues for the precise control of magnetic phases in thin films of quantum materials via a patterned strain gradient.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高压硅酸盐的电导率深刻影响岩石行星的内部动力学。研究旨在探究含铁后钙钛矿（post-perovskite）在超级地球（super-Earth）地幔条件下的电子电导率特性，特别是其金属化（metallization）可能性。

Method: 采用久保-格林伍德形式（Kubo-Greenwood formalism）进行第一性原理（ab initio）电子电导率计算。电子结构通过多体微扰理论（many-body perturbation theory）获得，并包含了局域Fe-3d轨道间的动态屏蔽（dynamical screening）和关联效应（correlations）。

Result: 与在类似条件下报道过金属化的(Fe,Mg)O不同，具有类地铁含量的后钙钛矿在超级地球地幔中不太可能通过带隙闭合（band-gap closure）实现金属化，导致可忽略的低频电导率。

Conclusion: 任何显著的电导率都需要非电子机制，例如热激活的小极化子跳跃（thermally activated small-polaron hopping），这超出了带传导（band conduction）的范畴。后钙钛矿的金属化可能性远低于之前研究的(Fe,Mg)O体系。

Abstract: The electrical conductivity of high-pressure silicates profoundly influences the interior dynamics of rocky planets. Employing the Kubo-Greenwood formalism, we perform ab initio calculations of electronic conductivity in Fe-bearing post-perovskite under super-Earth mantle conditions, up to 4000 K and 500 GPa. Electronic structures are obtained via many-body perturbation theory, incorporating dynamical screening and correlations among localized Fe-3d orbitals. In contrast to (Fe,Mg)O, for which metallization has been reported at comparable conditions, our results indicate that post-perovskite with Earth-like Fe contents is unlikely to metallize in super-Earth mantles via band-gap closure, yielding negligible low-frequency conductivity. Any substantial conductivity would require non-electronic mechanisms, such as thermally activated small-polaron hopping, which fall beyond the scope of band conduction.

The two-regime behavior can be explained by a change of the dominant carrier recombination channel. ### [14] [kALDo 2.0: Scalable Thermal Transport from First Principles and Machine Learning Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23728)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: kALDo2.0作为一个综合计算平台，将第一性原理精度与机器学习势的可扩展性相结合，为研究复杂材料的热输运性质提供了强大工具。软件特别适用于处理强非谐性材料和需要长程静电修正的体系，推动了热输运研究从晶体到无序材料的扩展。

Abstract: We introduce kALDo2.0, an open-source Python package for computing vibrational, elastic, and thermal transport properties of solids from first principles and machine-learned interatomic potentials. Building on the anharmonic lattice dynamics (ALD) framework, kALDo2.0 provides efficient CPU and GPU-accelerated implementations of the Boltzmann transport equation (BTE) for crystals and the quasi-harmonic Green-Kubo (QHGK) method. QHGK extends thermal transport predictions beyond crystals to disordered materials, including glasses, alloys, and complex nanostructures. kALDo2.0 introduces native integration with modern machine-learned potentials (MLPs), enabling thermal transport workflows that combine the accuracy of first-principles methods with the scalability of classical force fields. It also features comprehensive support for temperature-dependent effective potentials workflows, flexible storage backends for large-scale calculations, and advanced quantification of anharmonicity. The software seamlessly interfaces with electronic structure codes (Quantum ESPRESSO, VASP), molecular dynamics packages (LAMMPS), and MLPs (ACE, NEP, MACE, MatterSim, Orb), enabling thermal transport studies from 0 K to finite temperatures. kALDo2.0 implements multiple BTE solution strategies and essential physical corrections, including isotopic scattering and non-analytical terms for polar materials. A modular Python architecture with lazy evaluation and multiple storage formats (ASCII, NumPy, HDF5) enables simulations of systems containing up to tens of thousands of atoms. This paper describes the theoretical framework, implementation details, software architecture, and validation examples demonstrating kALDo2.0's capabilities for studying complex materials, including halide perovskites with strong anharmonicity and polar oxides requiring long-range electrostatic corrections.

Motivation: 卤素插层到层状材料二碲化钨（WTe2）中为调控其结构和电子性质提供了独特途径。研究旨在探索新型溴插层相的特性，并与碘插层类似物进行比较，以理解阴离子插层在过渡金属二硫族化物中的稳定性和结构灵活性。

Method: 研究合成了新型溴插层相WTe2Brx（x=0.5, 1.0, 1.25），并重新研究了碘插层类似物WTe2I。通过结构分析确定晶体结构：WTe2Br0.5为正交晶系空间群Pmmn，WTe2Br1.25为空间群Imm2，WTe2I则表现出非公度和公度（3+1）维调制变体。同时进行了电子结构计算。

Result: 溴插层体系在室温下表现出快速可逆的"呼吸"行为，允许客体分子在环境条件下从范德华间隙吸收或释放。WTe2Br0.5保持均匀堆叠序列，而WTe2Br1.25采用两种不同类型溴层交替排列的结构。WTe2I的公度多型体结构调制锁定在有理矢量q=(1/2, 0, 1/6)，也可描述为三维超晶胞。电子结构计算显示WTe2Br0.5和公度调制的WTe2I均为金属，费米能级处存在由插层引起的平带。

Conclusion: 这些发现证明了阴离子插层在过渡金属二硫族化物（transition metal dichalcogenides）中具有异常的稳定性和结构灵活性。不同卤素插层相的结构多样性和独特的"呼吸"行为为调控层状材料的性质提供了新的途径。

Abstract: Halogen intercalation into the layered material tungsten ditelluride (WTe2) provides a unique pathway to tune its structural and electronic properties. In this study, we detail the synthesis and characterization of the new bromine-intercalated phases WTe2Brx (x = 0.5, 1.0, and 1.25), and reinvestigate the iodine-intercalated analogue, WTe2I. A defining feature of the bromine system is its rapid and reversible "breathing" behavior at room temperature, allowing guest molecules to be absorbed or released from the van der Waals gaps under ambient conditions. Structural analysis shows that the bromine-poor phase WTe2Br0.5 crystallizes in the orthorhombic space group Pmmn, thereby maintaining a uniform stacking sequence. In contrast, the bromine-rich WTe2Br1.25 phase (space group Imm2) adopts an architecture where two distinct types of bromine layers alternate between the host layers. For the iodine system, the compound WTe2I exhibits both incommensurate and commensurate (3+1)D modulated variants in the superspace group P21/m(α0γ)00. In the commensurate polytype, the structural modulation locks into a rational vector, q = (1/2, 0, 1/6), which can be described also as a 3D supercell. Electronic structure calculations show WTe2Br0.5 and commensurately modulated WTe2I to be metals with flat bands at the Fermi energy arising from the intercalation. These findings demonstrate the unusual stability and structural flexibility of anionic intercalation in a transition metal dichalcogenides.

</details>

Method: 采用借鉴胶体纳米晶体（colloidal nanocrystals）合成概念的快速沉淀路线（fast precipitation route），成功制备了碘化物层状双钙钛矿(CnH(2n+1)NH3)4AgBiI8 (n=10,12,14)。通过X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）研究晶体结构，并结合热分析和变温衍射（temperature-dependent diffraction）研究相变行为。

Conclusion: 通过借鉴胶体纳米晶体合成概念的快速沉淀法，成功制备了结构稳定的无铅碘化物层状双钙钛矿材料。这些材料不仅保持了碘化物钙钛矿的窄带隙特性，还通过层状结构设计缓解了结构稳定性限制，为低毒性光电材料开发提供了新途径。

Abstract: Lead-free iodide double perovskites are an interesting class of materials since they combine a relatively low toxicity (compared to the lead counterpart) with the small bandgap typical of iodide-based perovskite structures. Their reported number is small due to their lower structural stability compared to the chloride and bromide analogues, hence their difficult synthesis. The structural constraints that limit stability, on the other hand, can be much relieved in layered, organic-inorganic perovskites. Following this line of thought, we report here a successful fast precipitation route to iodide layered (CnH(2n+1)NH3)4AgBiI8 (n = 10, 12, and 14) double perovskites that borrow concepts from the synthesis of colloidal nanocrystals. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高接触电阻是二维半导体集成到电子器件中的主要障碍。虽然界面工程（如使用V族半金属和基于强界面掺杂的电荷转移接触）已显示出改善接触性能的潜力，但仍需更有效的解决方案。

Method: 采用多种表征技术：角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）、X射线光电子衍射（X-ray photoelectron diffraction）、低能电子衍射（low-energy electron diffraction）和扫描隧道谱（scanning tunnelling spectroscopy）。通过对比原始Bi层和氧化Bi层与单层MoS₂的接触特性进行研究。

Abstract: High contact resistance remains a central obstacle to the integration of two-dimensional (2D) semiconductors in electronic devices. Recent advances have demonstrated that contact performance can be dramatically improved through interface engineering, including the use of group-V semimetals and charge-transfer contacts based on strong interfacial doping. Here, we show that controlled interfacial oxidation provides an effective route to convert a semimetal contact into a charge-transfer contact that degenerately $n$-dopes single layer MoS$_2$. Using a combination of angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, X-ray photoelectron diffraction, low-energy electron diffraction and scanning tunnelling spectroscopy, we demonstrate that putting single layer MoS$_2$ in contact with a pristine Bi layer merely results in weak doping, whereas oxidation of the Bi layer leads to a pronounced occupation of the MoS$_2$ conduction band with an electron density on the order of $10^{13}$~cm$^{-2}$. The cause of this strong electron doping is the fact that an ultrathin $β$-Bi$_2$O$_3$ layer forms below the MoS$_2$ and that this has a particularly low work function, thereby acting as an efficient electron donor to MoS$_2$. Interfacial oxidation thus emerges as a powerful design knob for engineering charge-transfer contacts to 2D semiconductors.

Abstract: We resolve a phase identification controversy in the Ag-Sn-S material system by unraveling the polymorphic structure of nanocrystals within the argyrodite material family. However, despite their well-studied bulk applications, the limited exploration at the nanoscale has left considerable potential for the discovery of emerging properties due to size effects. We show that Zn2+ is incorporated in the canfieldite-like structure through the replacement of Ag+, boosting the emission. ### [20] [Dirac semimetal phases in chiral carbon nanoscrolls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24141)
*Tzu-Ching Hsu,Jhih-Shih You,Hsiu-Chuan Hsu,Ion Cosma Fulga*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究理论分析了手性碳纳米卷（carbon nanoscrolls）在轴向磁场下的拓扑性质，发现手性结构破坏镜面对称性，导致狄拉克锥（Dirac cones）在偏离半磁通量子的位置出现，且这些狄拉克锥受联合反演-时间反演对称性保护。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料卷曲成螺旋几何结构会诱导手性（chirality），从而重塑其电子能带结构。本研究旨在理论探究碳纳米卷在轴向磁场下的拓扑性质，特别关注通过边缘位移编码手性的结构。

Method: 采用理论分析方法研究手性碳纳米卷，重点关注通过边缘位移（shifted edge alignments）编码手性的结构，并与无位移结构进行对比分析。

Result: 手性碳纳米卷缺乏镜面对称性，导致狄拉克锥在偏离半磁通量子（half a flux quantum）的磁通值处出现。这些狄拉克锥受联合反演-时间反演对称性（combined inversion-time reversal symmetry）保护，即使子晶格对称性（sublattice symmetry）被破坏也保持鲁棒性。狄拉克锥的数量及其实空间概率分布取决于卷曲圈数和磁场强度。

Conclusion: 该研究阐明了手性在纳米卷几何结构能带拓扑中的关键作用，揭示了手性结构如何通过破坏对称性影响狄拉克锥的位置和拓扑保护机制。

Abstract: Chirality induced by rolling a two-dimensional material into a spiral geometry reshapes its electronic band structure. In this work, we theoretically investigate the topological properties of carbon nanoscrolls under an axial magnetic field, focusing on structures in which chirality is encoded through shifted edge alignments. In contrast to unshifted structures, where mirror symmetry pins the Dirac cones to half a flux quantum, chiral carbon nanoscrolls lack this symmetry, and Dirac cones emerge at magnetic flux values away from half a flux quantum. We demonstrate that these Dirac cones are topologically protected by combined inversion-time reversal symmetry and remain robust even when sublattice symmetry is broken. Furthermore, we show that the number of Dirac cones and their real-space probability distributions depend on the number of turns and the magnetic field strength. Our study elucidates the role of chirality in the band topology of nanoscroll geometries.

### [21] [Spin dynamics of the spin-1 triangular lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet K$_2$Ni(SeO$_3$)$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24212)
*Chaebin Kim,Sathvik Nallapati,E. A. Ghioldi,Long Chen,Alexander I. Kolesnikov,Haidong Zhou,Shang-Shun Zhang,Cristian D. Batista,Martin Mourigal*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）探究了近乎理想的spin-1三角晶格海森堡反铁磁体K₂Ni(SeO₃)₂的自旋动力学，发现即使在有序温度以下，相干单磁振子激发（coherent one-magnon excitations）也与宽的高能连续谱（broad high-energy continuum）共存，表明S=1时仍存在显著的量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在spin-1/2三角晶格海森堡反铁磁体中，强量子涨落（strong quantum fluctuations）和非传统自旋动力学已得到确认，但它们在spin-1情况下的存在性仍是一个悬而未决的问题。本研究旨在探究spin-1三角晶格海森堡反铁磁体K₂Ni(SeO₃)₂的自旋动力学。

Method: 研究采用非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）技术探测K₂Ni(SeO₃)₂的自旋动力学。同时，运用两种互补的理论方法进行分析：一种是谱一致（spectrally consistent）的1/S修正自旋波理论（1/S-corrected spin wave theory），另一种是超越平均场（beyond-mean-field）的Schwinger玻色子理论（Schwinger boson theory）。

Result: 在有序温度T_N以下，观测到相干单磁振子激发（coherent one-magnon excitations）与宽的高能连续谱（broad high-energy continuum）共存。两种理论方法各自再现了连续谱的不同方面，但均不完整，这证明了S=1时仍存在显著的量子涨落，并主要反映在连续谱的谱分布（spectral distribution）中。在T_N以上，连续谱的带宽（bandwidth）得以保持，而谱权重（spectral weight）随着磁振子失去空间相干性而重新分布。

Conclusion: 研究确立了K₂Ni(SeO₃)₂作为模型三角反铁磁体的地位，并指出带宽守恒（bandwidth conservation）和连续谱内的谱权重分布是理解超越spin-1/2的有序量子磁体自旋动力学的组织原则（organizing principles）。结果强调了对二维反铁磁体相互作用多磁振子（interacting multi-magnon）部分进行受控计算的需求。

Abstract: Strong quantum fluctuations and unconventional spin dynamics are well established in the spin-1/2 triangular lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet. However, their survival in the spin-1 case remains an open question. We investigate the spin dynamics of K$_2$Ni(SeO$_3$)$_2$, a nearly ideal spin-1 triangular lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet, using inelastic neutron scattering. Below the ordering temperature $T_{\rm N}$, we observe coherent one-magnon excitations coexisting with a broad high-energy continuum. Two complementary approaches, a spectrally consistent $1/S$-corrected spin wave theory and a beyond-mean-field Schwinger boson theory, reproduce different facets of the continuum. Neither alone is complete, demonstrating substantial quantum fluctuations survive for $S\!=\!1$ and are reflected primarily in the spectral distribution of the continuum. Above $T_{\rm N}$, the continuum bandwidth is conserved while spectral weight is redistributed as magnons lose spatial coherence. Our results establish K$_2$Ni(SeO$_3$)$_2$ as a model triangular antiferromagnet, identifying bandwidth conservation and the distribution of spectral weight within the continuum as organizing principles to understand the spin dynamics of ordered quantum magnets beyond spin-1/2. Our results highlight the need for controlled calculations of the interacting multi-magnon sector of 2D antiferromagnets.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解析功能特性生长机制与厚度演化是薄膜材料发现与优化的关键任务，传统方法需要大量实验预算。本研究旨在建立系统化途径来阐明生长模式并区分铁电薄膜中铁电与电化学贡献。

Method: 采用厚度梯度库（thickness-gradient libraries）与自动化扫描探针显微技术（automated scanning probe microscopy）相结合的方法。以Hf0.5Zr0.5O2（HZO）梯度薄膜在LaxSr1-xMnO3（LSMO）底电极上的生长为模型系统，运用自动化压电响应力显微术（piezoresponse force microscopy）、光谱学和光刻技术进行分析。

Result: 研究发现不可逆形貌变形源于LSMO表面的电化学活性，而HZO中的可逆相位反转反映铁电开关行为。通过自动化形貌高度图扫描量化了厚度梯度上的成核密度、颗粒尺寸演化和粗糙度相关性，表明生长过程中羽流稳定性的改善抑制了界面反应并促进了致密细晶HZO的形成，有利于铁电相形成。

Conclusion: 这种材料工程与自动化扫描探针显微技术相结合的方法框架，为复杂氧化物薄膜中铁离子（ferroionic）和铁电响应的高通量、机制解析表征建立了平台。

Abstract: Resolving growth mechanisms and thickness evolution of functional properties is one of the key tasks in materials discovery and optimization involving thin-film materials, traditionally requiring significant experimental budgets. Here we introduce the combination of thickness-gradient libraries and automated scanning probe microscopy as a systematic pathway to elucidate growth modes and disentangle ferroelectric and electrochemical contributions in ferroelectric thin films. As a model system, we explore the Hf0.5Zr0.5O2 (HZO) gradient thin films grown on LaxSr1-xMnO3 (LSMO) bottom electrode thin films. Automated piezoresponse force microscopy, spectroscopy, and lithography reveals that irreversible topographic deformation arises from electrochemical activity at the LSMO surface, whereas reversible phase inversion in HZO reflects ferroelectric switching. Automated topography height-map scans are used to further quantify nucleation density, particle-size evolution, and roughness correlations across the thickness-gradient, demonstrating that improved plume stabilization during growth suppresses interfacial reactions and promotes dense, fine-grained HZO conducive to ferroelectric phase formation. This combined materials-engineering and automated-SPM framework establishes a platform for high-throughput, mechanism-resolved characterization of ferroionic and ferroelectric responses in complex oxide films.

</details>


### [23] [Resolving the Metastable Si-XIII Structure through Convergent Theory and Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24248)
*Fabrizio Rovaris,Corrado Bongiorno,Anna Marzegalli,Mouad Bikerouin,Davide Spirito,Gerald J. K. Schaffar,Mohamed Zaghloul,Agnieszka Anna Corley-Wiciak,Francesco Montalenti,Verena Maier-Kiener,Giovanni Capellini,Antonio M. Mio,Emilio Scalise*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过理论计算与实验表征相结合的方法，成功确定了硅（silicon）高压相Si-XIII的晶体结构，填补了硅元素同素异形体（allotropy）研究的重要空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅作为现代技术的基石材料，其同素异形体的探索是调控材料光电功能的关键前沿。Si-XIII相在20多年前被发现后一直未能确定结构，这构成了对元素硅同素异形体理解的重要缺失。

Method: 采用收敛性方法学（convergent methodology），结合先进理论建模与实验表征。基于实验观察构建结构模型，通过第一性原理优化（first-principles optimization）验证，并系统性地对照多种实验特征进行测试。

Result: 提出的晶体结构能够合理解释该相的所有特征指纹：晶面间距（interplanar spacings）、拉曼频率（Raman frequencies）、热力学稳定性（thermodynamic stability）和动力学路径（kinetic pathways）。

Conclusion: 这些发现为硅的高压相图（high-pressure phase diagram）提供了关键缺失部分，展示了计算预测与实验验证相结合在解决材料科学复杂结构问题中的强大能力。

Abstract: Silicon is the undisputed cornerstone of modern technology, with applications ranging from micro- and opto-electronics to quantum technologies. Recently, the exploration of its allotropes has emerged as a pivotal frontier for engineering materials with tailored optical and electronic functionalities. High-pressure experiments have revealed several metastable silicon phases, among which is Si-XIII. First observed more than 20 years ago, this phase has remained structurally unidentified, representing a significant gap in our understanding of elemental silicon allotropy. In this work, a convergent methodology is employed combining advanced theoretical modeling with experimental characterization to finally resolve the long-standing structural assignment of Si-XIII. Guided by careful experimental observations, a structural model validated through first-principles optimization and systematically tested against multiple experimental signatures is constructed. All the fingerprints of this phase are rationalized by our proposed crystal structure: interplanar spacings, Raman frequencies, thermodynamic stability, and kinetic pathways. These findings provide a crucial missing piece in the high-pressure phase diagram of silicon and demonstrate the power of integrating computational predictions with experimental validation to resolve complex structural problems in materials science.

</details>

### [24] [Dispersionless Hirota system and hidden symmetries of heavenly equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23506)
*Andriy Panasyuk,Adam Szereszewski*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将Konopelchenko等人的观察重新表述于I和II型Plebański天方程（I,II PHE）的框架中，通过引入5D类比方程和特殊对称性，建立了与色散less Hirota系统的联系，并获得了依赖于对称变换Φ的度量显式公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在将2021年Konopelchenko等人关于4D色散less Hirota系统与描述中性签名自对偶真空爱因斯坦度量的general heavenly equation之间关系的观察，重新置于I和II型Plebański天方程（I,II PHE）的语境中进行阐释。

Method: 首先寻找I和II型Plebański天方程的5维类比方程，然后考虑一种特殊对称性（推广了I或II型PHE的tri-holomorphic对称性），通过对此对称性进行约化（模仿自对偶真空爱因斯坦度量向特殊Einstein-Weyl结构的约化），得到I和II型PHE的色散less Hirota系统类比。

Result: 这种视角允许重新解释对称变换f↦Φ(f)，并获得依赖于Φ的度量显式公式。论文还提供了展示Weyl旋量如何随Φ变化的若干示例。

Conclusion: 研究成功地将先前关于Hirota系统与general heavenly equation关系的观察，系统性地重新表述于I和II型Plebański天方程的框架中，建立了5D类比方程与对称性约化的理论联系，并获得了度量的显式构造方法。

Abstract: In 2021 Konopelchenko, Schief and Szereszewski observed that solutions of 4D dispersionless Hirota system also solve the general heavenly equation describing self-dual vacuum Einstein metrics in neutral signature. They also noticed that the symmetry $f\mapsto Φ(f)$ of the Hirota system essentially changes the properties of the corresponding metric.
  In this paper we restate these observations in the context of I and II Plebański heavenly equation (I,II PHE). Namely, we first find 5D analogues of these equations. We then consider a special type of symmetry generalizing the so-called tri-holomorphic symmetry of I or II PHE. The reduction with respect to this symmetry (which in a sense imitates the reduction of self-dual vacuum Einstein metrics with respect to a tri-holomorphic symmetry ending in special Einstein--Weyl structures) gives an analogue of the dispersionless Hirota system for I and II PHE. Such a point of view allows to reinterpret the symmetry $f\mapsto Φ(f)$ mentioned and obtain explicit formulas for the metric depending on $Φ$. We present some examples showing how the Weyl spinor changes along with $Φ$.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [25] [Measurement of the Muon Flux at SND@LHC: Results from the 2023-2025 Proton and Heavy-Ion Periods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23412)
*The SND@LHC Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: SND@LHC实验报告了2023-2025年间在探测器中心31×31 cm²基准区域内测量的μ子通量，包括质子碰撞和重离子碰撞数据，结果与蒙特卡洛模拟预测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SND@LHC实验研究前向赝快度（forward pseudorapidity）范围7.2<η<8.4内的中微子。源自ATLAS碰撞点（IP1）的μ子是CC中微子相互作用的主要背景，并决定乳胶靶（emulsion target）的更换频率，因此精确表征该通量至关重要。

Method: 使用SND@LHC探测器进行测量，该探测器由否决系统、闪烁光纤（SciFi）追踪器与乳胶云室（ECCs）交错排列、以及下游μ子系统组成。测量基于2023年至2025年的数据，在探测器中心31×31 cm²基准区域（fiducial area）内进行。

Result: 质子碰撞测量的μ子通量为：(1.90±0.04)×10⁻² nb/cm² (2023)、(3.74±0.06)×10⁻² nb/cm² (2024)、(2.48±0.04)×10⁻² nb/cm² (2025)。重离子碰撞测量的通量为：(3.13±0.11)×10⁴ nb/cm² (2023)、(5.54±0.17)×10⁴ nb/cm² (2024)、(3.60±0.13)×10⁴ nb/cm² (2025)。不确定性主要由系统效应主导，统计成分对总不确定性的贡献≲1%。

Conclusion: 测量结果与蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）预测一致，为SND@LHC实验中微子研究的背景估计和实验运行提供了重要数据支持。

Abstract: The SND@LHC experiment investigates neutrinos in the forward pseudorapidity range of $7.2 < η< 8.4$. The detector consists of a veto system, a scintillating fiber (SciFi) tracker interleaved with emulsion cloud chambers (ECCs), and a downstream muon system. Muons originating from collisions at ATLAS (IP1) constitute the primary background for CC neutrino interactions and determine the replacement frequency of the emulsion target. A precise characterization of this flux is therefore essential. In this work, we report the muon flux measured in the central $31 \times 31 \text{ cm}^2$ fiducial area of the detector using data from 2023 through 2025. The measured fluxes for proton collisions are: $(1.90 \pm 0.04) \times 10^{-2} \text{ nb/cm}^2$ (2023), $(3.74 \pm 0.06) \times 10^{-2} \text{ nb/cm}^2$ (2024), and $(2.48 \pm 0.04) \times 10^{-2} \text{ nb/cm}^2$ (2025). The measured fluxes for heavy-ion collisions are $(3.13 \pm 0.11) \times 10^4 \text{ nb/cm}^2$, $(5.54 \pm 0.17) \times 10^4 \text{ nb/cm}^2$, and $(3.60 \pm 0.13) \times 10^4 \text{ nb/cm}^2$ in 2023, 2024, and 2025, respectively. Uncertainties are dominated by systematic effects, with the statistical component contributing $\lesssim 1\%$ to the total uncertainty. These results are in agreement with Monte Carlo predictions.

</details>

Zheng,W. Q. Zheng,X. R. Zheng,Y. H. Zheng,B. Zhong,C. Zhong,H. Zhou,J. Q. Zhou,S. Zhou,X. Zhou,X. K. Zhou,X. R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,J. H. Zou*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 首次测量了质心能量3.51-4.95 GeV范围内e⁺e⁻→Σ⁻Σ⁺过程的玻恩截面和有效形状因子，并首次以5.5σ显著性观测到ψ(3770)→Σ⁻Σ⁺衰变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究e⁺e⁻→Σ⁻Σ⁺过程的玻恩截面和有效形状因子，探索粲偶素态（charmonium states）的衰变特性，并检验矢量介子主导模型（vector-meson-dominance model）。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的44 fb⁻¹积分亮度e⁺e⁻对撞数据，通过拟合与质心能量相关的修饰截面（dressed cross sections）进行分析。

Result: 首次观测到ψ(3770)→Σ⁻Σ⁺衰变（显著性5.5σ，包含系统不确定性），提供了其他可能粲偶素态分支比与电子部分宽度乘积的90%置信水平上限，并确定了Σ同位旋三重态玻恩截面比值。

Conclusion: 测量结果为测试矢量介子主导模型提供了关键数据，首次观测到的ψ(3770)→Σ⁻Σ⁺衰变扩展了对粲偶素态衰变特性的理解。

Abstract: Using $e^+e^-$ collision data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 44 fb$^{-1}$ collected with the BESIII detector at the BEPCII collider, we report the first measurement of Born cross sections and effective form factors for $e^+e^-\toΣ^-\barΣ^+$ at centre-of-mass energies between 3.51 and 4.95 GeV. With a fit to the $\sqrt{s}$-dependent dressed cross sections, the decay $ψ(3770)\toΣ^-\barΣ^+$ is observed for the first time with a significance of 5.5$σ$, including systematic uncertainties. Upper limits at the 90\% confidence level on the product of the branching fraction and the electronic partial width are provided for other possible charmonium(-like) states. The ratios of Born cross sections for the $Σ$ isospin-triplet states are determined and can be used to test the vector-meson-dominance model.

</details>


### [27] [Combination of ATLAS and CMS searches for Higgs boson pair production at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23991)
*ATLAS,CMS Collaborations*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: ATLAS和CMS合作组结合了大型强子对撞机（LHC）Run 2期间在13 TeV质心能量下收集的质子-质子对撞数据，对希格斯玻色子对（HH）产生进行了联合搜索分析，给出了总信号强度的上限和测量值，并对希格斯玻色子三线性自耦合（trilinear self-coupling）及双希格斯玻色子与双矢量玻色子耦合（couplings of two Higgs bosons to two vector bosons）设置了约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过结合ATLAS和CMS实验的数据，提高对希格斯玻色子对（HH）产生过程的探测灵敏度，从而更精确地测量希格斯玻色子的自相互作用（self-interaction）特性，这对验证标准模型（Standard Model, SM）预测和理解电弱对称性破缺机制至关重要。

Method: 研究结合了ATLAS和CMS合作组在大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider, LHC）Run 2期间收集的质子-质子对撞数据，质心能量为13 TeV，积分亮度（integrated luminosity）范围为126至140 fb⁻¹。通过联合分析多个搜索通道，测量了总HH信号强度，并设置了相关耦合参数的约束。

Result: 在95%置信水平下，总HH信号强度的观测上限为2.5（以测量截面与标准模型预测的比值定义），而测量值为0.8^{+0.9}_{-0.7}。观测显著性（observed significance）为1.1个标准差。对归一化耦合参数κ_λ和κ_{2V}的观测约束分别为-0.71 < κ_λ < 6.1和0.73 < κ_{2V} < 1.3。

Conclusion: 通过结合ATLAS和CMS实验的数据，研究显著提高了对希格斯玻色子对产生过程的探测灵敏度，为希格斯玻色子三线性自耦合和双希格斯玻色子与双矢量玻色子耦合提供了目前最严格的约束，结果与标准模型预测基本一致，但需要更多数据来获得明确的发现。

Abstract: This Letter presents a combination of searches for Higgs boson pair (HH) production performed by the ATLAS and CMS Collaborations using proton-proton collision data sets recorded at $\sqrt{s} = 13$ TeV during the Large Hadron Collider Run 2, corresponding to integrated luminosities ranging between 126 and 140 $\mathrm{fb^{-1}}$. The upper limit at the 95% confidence level on the total HH signal strength, defined as the ratio of the measured cross section to the SM prediction, corresponds to 2.5, with an expected value of 1.7 (2.8) assuming the absence (presence) of the standard model (SM) HH signal. The strength of the HH signal is measured to be $0.8^{+0.9}_{-0.7}$ relative to the SM prediction. The observed significance is found to be 1.1 standard deviations whereas 1.3 are expected for the SM HH signal. Constraints are set on the Higgs boson trilinear self-coupling and on the couplings of two Higgs bosons to two vector bosons, both normalized to the SM predictions and denoted as $κ_λ$ and $κ_{2\mathrm{V}}$, respectively. The observed individual constraints at the 95% confidence level are $-0.71 < κ_λ< 6.1$ and $0.73 < κ_{2\mathrm{V}} < 1.3$, while the expected constraints assuming the presence of the SM HH signal are $-1.3 < κ_λ< 6.7$ and $0.66 < κ_{2\mathrm{V}} < 1.4$.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究首次测量了Λ_c^+→ΛX衰变中Λ超子的纵向极化，并利用极化信息搜索电荷宇称（CP）破坏，同时更新了分支比测量精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在首次测量Λ_c^+→ΛX衰变中Λ超子的纵向极化，并利用极化信息探索电荷宇称（CP）破坏现象，同时提高分支比测量精度。

Method: 基于BESIII探测器在质心能量4.600-4.699 GeV收集的4.5 fb⁻¹积分亮度数据，测量Λ和反Λ超子的纵向极化，并构建极化不对称性搜索CP破坏。

Result: 测得Λ极化P_Λ = -0.393±0.055(stat.)±0.020(sys.)，反Λ极化P_Λ̄ = 0.288±0.056(stat.)±0.017(sys.)；极化CP不对称性A_CP^pol = 0.15±0.12(stat.)±0.04(sys.)；分支比B(Λ_c^+→ΛX) = (38.07±0.38(stat.)±0.49(sys.))%；直接CP不对称性A_CP^dir = (1.5±1.0(stat.)±1.0(sys.))%。

Conclusion: 首次实现了Λ_c^+→ΛX衰变中Λ超子极化的测量，分支比测量精度较世界平均值提高四倍，未观察到粲重子衰变中CP破坏的证据。

Abstract: Based on $e^+e^-$ annihilation data collected with the BESIII detector at center-of-mass energies from 4.600 to 4.699 GeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 4.5 fb$^{-1}$, we present the first measurement of the longitudinal polarization of $Λ$ hyperons produced in the inclusive decay $Λ_c^+ \to ΛX$, where $X$ denotes any allowed final state. The polarizations are determined to be $\mathcal{P}_Λ = -0.393 \pm 0.055_{\mathrm{sta.}} \pm 0.020_{\mathrm{sys.}}$ and $\mathcal{P}_{\barΛ} = 0.288 \pm 0.056_{\mathrm{sta.}} \pm 0.017_{\mathrm{sys.}}$. We then search for CP violation using an asymmetry constructed from the $Λ$ polarization and the $Λ\to p π^-$ decay asymmetry parameters, and obtain $\mathcal{A}_{\mathrm{CP}}^{\mathrm{pol}} = 0.15 \pm 0.12_{\mathrm{sta.}} \pm 0.04_{\mathrm{sys.}}$. We also perform an updated measurement of the absolute branching fraction, resulted as $\mathcal{B}(Λ_c^+ \to ΛX) = (38.07 \pm 0.38_{\mathrm{sta.}} \pm 0.49_{\mathrm{sys.}})\%$, with precision improved by a factor of four relative to the current world average. A search for direct CP violation yields $\mathcal{A}_{\mathrm{CP}}^{\mathrm{dir}} = (1.5 \pm 1.0_{\mathrm{sta.}} \pm 1.0_{\mathrm{sys.}})\%$. No evidence for CP violation in inclusive charm baryon decays is observed.

</details>


### [29] [End-to-end Differentiable Calibration and Reconstruction for Optical Particle Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24129)
*Omar Alterkait,César Jesús-Valls,Ryo Matsumoto,Patrick de Perio,Kazuhiro Terao*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个端到端可微分光学粒子探测器模拟器，通过基于梯度的优化实现同时校准与重建，为粒子物理实验建立了新的模拟与重建范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验物理分析依赖高保真模拟器将传感器级信息转换为物理量，这需要精确的校准（calibration）来对齐模拟与真实数据，以及追踪（tracking）来从光学信号推断粒子性质。传统方法将模拟、校准和追踪作为独立问题处理，存在局限性。

Method: 开发了首个端到端可微分光学粒子探测器模拟器（end-to-end differentiable optical particle detector simulator），在单个可微分框架内统一了模拟、校准和追踪。该方法在光产生、传播和探测的所有关键阶段实现了平滑且物理意义明确的梯度，同时保持了计算效率。

Result: 基于梯度的校准与重建简化了现有分析流程，在精度和速度上匹配或超越了传统不可微分方法。该框架的模块化设计使其能轻松适应不同探测器几何结构和目标材料，为实验设计与优化提供了灵活基础。

Conclusion: 该技术已准备好应用于当前和未来的光学探测器实验，为粒子物理中的模拟与重建建立了新范式（new paradigm）。可微分模拟器通过统一传统分离的任务，显著提升了分析效率与性能。

Abstract: Large-scale homogeneous detectors with optical readouts are widely used in particle detection, with Cherenkov and scintillator neutrino detectors as prominent examples. Analyses in experimental physics rely on high-fidelity simulators to translate sensor-level information into physical quantities of interest. This task critically depends on accurate calibration, which aligns simulation behavior with real detector data, and on tracking, which infers particle properties from optical signals. We present the first end-to-end differentiable optical particle detector simulator, enabling simultaneous calibration and reconstruction through gradient-based optimization. Our approach unifies simulation, calibration, and tracking, which are traditionally treated as separate problems, within a single differentiable framework. We demonstrate that it achieves smooth and physically meaningful gradients across all key stages of light generation, propagation, and detection while maintaining computational efficiency. We show that gradient-based calibration and reconstruction greatly simplify existing analysis pipelines while matching or surpassing the performance of conventional non-differentiable methods in both accuracy and speed. Moreover, the framework's modularity allows straightforward adaptation to diverse detector geometries and target materials, providing a flexible foundation for experiment design and optimization. The results demonstrate the readiness of this technique for adoption in current and future optical detector experiments, establishing a new paradigm for simulation and reconstruction in particle physics.

</details>

### [30] [A new class of coherent states involving Fox-Wright functions and their generalization in the bicomplex framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23764)
*Snehasis Bera,Sourav Das,Abhijit Banerjee*

TL;DR: 本文基于Fox Wright函数构建了一类广泛的相干态（coherent states），包括离散谱和连续谱情形，并进一步推广到双复变元（bicomplex arguments）设置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在构建一类基于Fox Wright函数的广义相干态，这类相干态需要满足连续性、可归一化性和单位分解（resolution of unity）等关键要求，并探索其在连续谱和双复变元设置中的推广。

Method: 采用Fox Wright函数作为归一化函数（normalization function）引入相干态，通过离散到连续极限过程获得连续谱相干态，并引入FW广义多参数nu函数（FW generalized multi parameter nu function）作为连续谱归一化函数。进一步引入双复变元Fox Wright函数并研究其存在性。

Result: 成功构建了满足连续性、可归一化性和单位分解要求的Fox Wright相干态；获得了连续谱相干态并验证了FW广义多参数nu函数的归一化作用；建立了双复变元Fox Wright相干态并分析了其性质；将结果推广到双复变元设置并定义了相应的归一化函数。

Conclusion: 该工作系统构建了基于Fox Wright函数的相干态理论框架，包括离散谱、连续谱以及双复变元推广，为相干态研究提供了新的数学工具和理论扩展。

Abstract: In this work, an extensive class of coherent states is introduced by taking the Fox Wright function as the normalization function. It is demonstrated that these states satisfy the key requirements of continuity, normalizability and resolution of unity. Furthermore, coherent states associated with the continuous spectrum are obtained through a discrete to continuous limiting procedure. Moreover, FW generalized multi parameter nu function is introduced and shown to act as the normalization function for the Fox Wright coherent states in the continuous spectrum. Later the Fox Wright function with bicomplex arguments has been introduced and its existence has been investigated. Bicomplex Fox Wright coherent states are also developed for the discrete spectrum based on this new function and their properties are analyzed. Subsequently, the results regarding Fox Wright coherent states are generalized to the bicomplex setting. In addition, a bicomplex FW generalized multi-parameter nu function is defined to demonstrate that it provides the normalization for these states in the continuous spectrum.

### [31] [From quantum time to manifestly covariant QFT: on the need for a quantum-action-based quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23625)
*N. L. Diaz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于量子时间（QT）方案的第二量子化方法，旨在使洛伦兹协变性（Lorentz covariance）在希尔伯特空间层面显式化。通过引入时空经典力学（SCM）和量子作用量（quantum action）为基础的量子化，构建了时空版本的量子力学（SQM），解决了标准量子场论（QFT）中协变性隐藏的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在将量子时间（quantum time, QT）方案从单粒子推广到量子场论（QFT），使洛伦兹协变性（Lorentz covariance）在希尔伯特空间层面显式化，而非像标准正则表述中那样隐藏。这源于对量子场论中协变性表述更基础层面的追求。

Method: 提出了一种第二量子化（second-quantized）方法，其中基本粒子是QT粒子本身，自然引出时空场代数（spacetime field algebras）和量子作用量（quantum action）的概念。通过引入时空经典力学（spacetime classical mechanics, SCM）作为第二量子化形式的经典对应物，并证明了一个"不可行定理"（no-go theorem），指出狄拉克量子化（Dirac quantization）会坍缩回标准QFT。最终采用基于量子作用量的量子化方法，构建了时空版本的量子力学（spacetime version of quantum mechanics, SQM）。

Result: 研究表明，简单的多体构造会导致不一致性。通过SCM的狄拉克量子化会坍缩回标准QFT，从而隐藏协变性。然而，基于量子作用量的量子化方法成功构建了SQM，使协变性在相互作用的量子场论中显式化。这一解决方案与量子态概念的真正时空推广密切相关，该推广由因果性要求，并与最近的"随时间状态"（states over time）提议以及dS/CFT启发的微观类时纠缠（timelike entanglement）和涌现时间（emergent time）概念紧密联系。

Conclusion: 论文成功构建了时空版本的量子力学（SQM），使洛伦兹协变性在量子场论中显式化。这一进展依赖于量子态概念的真正时空推广，并与因果性、类时纠缠和涌现时间等前沿概念建立了重要联系，为量子场论的基础表述提供了新的视角。

Abstract: In quantum time (QT) schemes, time is promoted to a degree of freedom, allowing Lorentz covariance to be made explicit for single particles. We ask whether this can be lifted to QFT, so that Lorentz covariance becomes manifest at the Hilbert-space level, rather than being hidden as in the standard canonical formulation. We address this question by proposing a second-quantized approach in which the elementary particle is the QT particle itself, leading naturally to the notion of spacetime field algebras and of quantum action. We show, however, that a naive many-body construction runs into inconsistencies. To pinpoint their origin we introduce a classical counterpart of the second-quantized formalism, spacetime classical mechanics (SCM), and prove a no-go theorem: Dirac quantization of SCM collapses back to standard QFT and therefore hides covariance. We circumvent this problem by presenting a quantum-action--based quantization that yields a spacetime version of quantum mechanics (SQM), making covariance manifest for (interacting) QFTs. Finally, we show that this resolution is tied to a genuine spacetime generalization of the notion of quantum state, required by causality and closely connected to recent ``states over time'' proposals and, in dS/CFT-motivated settings, to microscopic notions of timelike entanglement and emergent time.

</details>


### [32] [Perfect transmission of a Dirac particle in one-dimension double square barrier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23650)
*Xu Zhang,Qiang Gu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究表明狄拉克粒子（Dirac particles）在克莱因区（Klein zone）的完美隧穿（perfect Klein tunneling）与非相对论共振透射（resonant transmission）之间存在连续过渡，揭示了克莱因佯谬（Klein paradox）与共振透射机制的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管克莱因完美隧穿（perfect Klein tunneling）与非相对论共振透射在现象上相似，但传统观点认为两者的物理机制存在根本差异。本研究旨在探索这两种现象之间是否存在更深刻的联系。

Method: 采用相对论双势垒模型（relativistic double-barrier model），通过束缚态分析（bound-state analysis）和波包动力学（wave-packet dynamics）两种方法进行研究。

Result: 研究发现完美透射曲线可以从势垒上方区域连续过渡到克莱因区，且在克莱因区内即使对于亚临界势垒高度（subcritical barrier heights）也能发生完美透射。

Conclusion: 这些发现表明克莱因完美隧穿与共振透射之间存在联系，为理解克莱因佯谬的物理本质提供了新视角。

Abstract: Dirac particles can undergo perfect transmission through a sufficiently high potential barrier in the Klein zone. Although the perfect Klein tunneling (often referred to as the Klein paradox) is similar to the non-relativistic resonant transmission which occurs only when the kinetic energy exceeds the barrier, the underlying mechanism is believed to be fundamentally distinct. In this work, we show that for the relativistic double-barrier model the perfect-transmission curve can pass continuously from the above-barrier zone to the Klein zone. Additionally, in the Klein zone, perfect transmission occurs even for subcritical barrier heights, supported by both bound-state analysis and wave-packet dynamics. These findings suggest a connection between perfect Klein tunneling and resonant transmission, and provide new insights into the physical nature of the Klein paradox.

</details>


### [33] [Spin stiffness and resilience phase transition in a noisy toric-rotor code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23751)
*Morteza Zarei,Mohammad Hossein Zarei*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将经典XY模型的配分函数量子形式化，用于识别噪声环面转子码中的韧性相变，建立了噪声宽度与XY模型温度的映射关系，并引入了表征逻辑子空间噪声韧性的拓扑序参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在为连续变量量子码的可纠正性提供数学严谨的分析框架。通过将环面转子码在冯·米塞斯分布描述的相移噪声下的保真度与XY模型配分函数建立联系，探索噪声环境下的量子编码韧性。

Method: 采用XY模型配分函数的量子形式化方法，将环面转子码的噪声宽度映射到XY模型的温度参数。发展了XY模型中自旋刚度（spin stiffness）的量子形式化，并将其映射到环面转子码逻辑子空间的量子门保真度。

Result: 发现环面转子码在临界宽度σ_c≈0.89处存在混合态相变，对应于XY模型的Kosterlitz-Thouless相变。逻辑子空间在σ<σ_c时表现出部分噪声韧性，韧性序参数接近1，在σ_c处降至零，但未表现出完全韧性。

Conclusion: 配分函数的量子形式化为研究连续变量量子码的可纠正性提供了数学严谨的框架。该工作揭示了环面转子码在二维及更高维度中的噪声韧性特征，为理解量子编码在噪声环境下的行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: We use a quantum formalism for the partition function of the classical $XY$ model to identify a resilience phase transition in a noisy toric-rotor code. Specifically, we consider the toric-rotor code under phase-shift noise described by a von Mises probability distribution and show that the fidelity between the final state after noise and the initial state is proportional to the partition function of the $XY$ model. We map the temperature of the $XY$ model to the width of the noise in the toric-rotor code, such that a Kosterlitz--Thouless phase transition at a critical temperature $T_{c}$ corresponds to a mixed-state phase transition at a critical width $σ_c$. To characterize this phase transition, we develop a quantum formalism for the spin stiffness in the $XY$ model and show that it is mapped to the gate fidelity in the logical subspace of the toric-rotor code. In particular, we introduce a topological order parameter that characterizes the resilience of the toric-rotor code to decoherence within the logical subspace. We show that the logical subspace does not exhibit complete resilience to noise, which is a necessary condition for correctability. However, it exhibits partial resilience to noise for widths less than $σ_c\approx 0.89$, where the resilience order parameter takes values near $1$ and then drops to zero at $σ_c$. We also use our results to shed light on the correctability of toric-rotor codes in higher dimensions $d > 2$. Our work shows that the quantum formalism for partition functions provides a mathematically rigorous framework for studying correctability in continuous-variable quantum codes.

</details>


### [34] [Characterization of Josephson Junction Aging and Annealing Under Different Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23888)
*Rangga P. Budoyo,Rasanayagam S. Kajen,Bing Wen Cheah,Long H. Nguyen,Rainer Dumke*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了约瑟夫森结（Josephson junctions）在不同储存条件下的老化行为以及氮气与空气环境中热退火对结电阻的影响，发现老化遵循对数曲线，且无法通过退火将电阻降至初始值以下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解约瑟夫森结的老化行为以及退火对结电阻的影响，对于构建大规模超导量子处理器至关重要。

Method: 研究约瑟夫森结在不同储存条件（实验室环境、氮气气氛、真空）下从制备后到2-3个月的老化过程，并比较氮气环境与空气环境中最高250°C的热退火效果。

Result: 老化曲线遵循对数曲线，老化幅度主要由制备条件决定，老化速度由储存条件决定。实验室环境储存的老化速度更快，且储存条件改变时老化速度显著变化。氮气环境中所有测试温度下电阻均下降，而空气环境中200°C时电阻增加、250°C时电阻下降。

Conclusion: 约瑟夫森结的老化行为受储存条件显著影响，且无法通过退火将电阻降至初始值以下，表明电阻调谐存在下限。

Abstract: Understanding the aging behavior of Josephson junctions and the effect of annealing on junction resistances is important in building large-scale superconducting quantum processors. Here we study the effects of aging of Josephson junctions under different storage conditions from immediately after fabrication up to 2 to 3 months. We find that the aging curve follows a logarithmic curve, with the aging amplitude mainly determined by fabrication conditions and the aging speed determined by storage conditions. Junctions stored at ambient laboratory conditions aged faster compared to junctions stored in a nitrogen atmosphere or vacuum, with the aging speed appreciably changes when the storage condition changed. We also compared the effect of thermal annealing under nitrogen environment with annealing under ambient conditions up to 250$^\circ$ C. We find that under nitrogen environment, the resistances decreased at all temperatures tested, while under ambient environment the resistances increased at 200$^\circ$ C and decreased at 250$^\circ$ C instead. We were unable to decrease the resistance below the initial-time resistance, suggesting a lower limit on the range of resistance tuning.

</details>

### [35] [Universality of the Blandford-Znajek emission in stationary and axisymmetric spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23417)
*Filippo Camilloni,Luciano Rezzolla*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了Blandford-Znajek（BZ）机制在不同黑洞时空中的普适性，发现其最低阶贡献在所有时空下保持不变，而高阶项则能反映时空的强场特性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Blandford-Znajek（BZ）机制被广泛认为是提取吸积黑洞旋转能量并驱动相对论性喷流的最有力过程。本研究旨在探索该机制在不同黑洞时空中的普适性，特别是在Konoplya-Rezzolla-Zhidenko形式框架下。

Method: 采用Konoplya-Rezzolla-Zhidenko形式体系，研究BZ机制在一般性黑洞时空中的行为。分析BZ功率在不同阶次上的贡献，特别关注最低阶和次高阶项的表现。

Result: 研究发现BZ功率的最低阶贡献在不同黑洞时空中保持不变，具有不变性（invariant）。然而在次高阶（next-leading-order）上，不同时空会导致不同的BZ光度（luminosity）。

Conclusion: 缓慢旋转的黑洞无法通过喷流功率测量来区分，但快速旋转的黑洞在同时获得BZ光度和黑洞角速度独立测量时，有可能提供时空强场特性的信息。

Abstract: The Blandford-Znajek (BZ) mechanism is widely recognised as the most compelling process to extract rotational energy from an accreting black hole and power the emission of relativistic jets. We explore the universality of this process for generic black-hole spacetimes within the Konoplya-Rezzolla-Zhidenko formalism and find that the lowest-order contribution to the BZ power is invariant across different black-hole spacetimes. We also show that at the next-leading-order, different black-hole spacetimes will lead to different BZ luminosities. As a result, while slowly rotating black holes cannot be distinguished via measurements of their jet power, rapidly rotating ones have the potential of providing information on the strong-field properties of the spacetime when independent measurements of the BZ luminosity and of the black-hole angular velocity are available.

</details>


### [36] [Polarisation Singularities of Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23425)
*Claire Rigouzzo,Sebastian Golat,Alex J. Vernon,Kyan Louisia,Eugene Lim,Francisco J. Rodriguez-Fortuno*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于波场偏离理想平面波时产生的复杂几何结构，特别是当多个单色波干涉时出现的偏振奇点。这些奇点产生于纯圆偏振或线偏振的轨迹，在随机背景场中尤为显著。

Method: 基于电磁描述的理论框架，构建了引力波偏振奇点的类比理论。通过平面波干涉的数值模拟来验证理论，并分析产生的奇点密度分布特征。

Result: 研究证明偏振奇点是引力波的普遍特征，但其维度依赖于场的自旋。通过平面波干涉模拟展示了这些奇点的具体形态，并分析了相应的奇点密度分布规律。

Conclusion: 该工作成功将偏振奇点理论扩展到引力波和高自旋场，揭示了这些奇点的普遍性和维度依赖性，为理解波场几何结构提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Departure from idealised plane waves gives rise to intricate geometric structures in wave fields. One such structure is the polarisation singularity, which emerges when multiple monochromatic waves interfere (such as would be the case for stochastic backgrounds), producing loci of purely circular or linear polarisation. In this work, we extend the theory of polarisation singularities to gravitational waves and higher spin fields. Building on the electromagnetic description, we formulate the gravitational analogue of polarisation singularities and show that they are generic features of gravitational waves. Their dimension, however, depends on the spin of the field. We illustrate these results with simulations of plane-wave interference and analyse the resulting singularity densities.

</details>


### [37] [Scalar Bosons with Coulomb Potentials in a Space with Dual Topological Defects in Rainbow Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23519)
*L. G. Barbosa,J. V. Zamperlini,L. C. N. Santos*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括：构建描述组合拓扑缺陷及能量相关时空变形的有效度规；在此背景下建立包含标量、矢量和非最小耦合的克莱因-戈尔登方程（Klein-Gordon equation）；通过变量分离法求解方程；考虑广义库仑型相互作用以统一分析散射态和束缚态；通过相应S矩阵的极点确定束缚态谱。

Result: 研究结果展示了拓扑缺陷与彩虹引力修正如何共同影响标量玻色子的谱性质。通过数值计算和适当极限下的解析近似，分析了两种特定彩虹函数选择对能谱的影响，并在适当极限下一致地恢复了已知结果。

Conclusion: 结论表明，标量玻色子的谱特性受到拓扑缺陷与彩虹引力修正之间相互作用的显著影响，该研究为理解能量相关时空变形与拓扑结构在量子动力学中的耦合效应提供了理论框架。

Abstract: This work studies the relativistic quantum dynamics of scalar bosons in a spacetime containing both a cosmic string and a global monopole within the framework of Rainbow Gravity. An effective metric is constructed to describe the combined topological defects together with the energy-dependent deformation of spacetime. The Klein-Gordon equation is formulated in this background, including scalar, vector, and nonminimal couplings, and its solutions are obtained by separation of variables. Generalized Coulomb-type interactions are considered, allowing a unified analysis of scattering and bound states. The bound-state spectrum is determined from the poles of the corresponding $S$-matrix. Two specific choices of rainbow functions are examined, and their influence on the energy spectrum is analyzed through numerical calculations and, in suitable limits, analytical approximations. The results show how the interplay between topological defects and rainbow gravity corrections affects the spectral properties of scalar bosons, while known results are consistently recovered in appropriate limits.

### [38] [Mimetic gravity in the extended objects framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23538)
*Efraín Rojas*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究从描述任意维度扩展物体在余维一平坦时空背景中测地演化的最一般二阶导数理论出发，确定了产生二阶运动方程的子集模型，形成了有趣的Lovelock型膜引力理论，该理论扩展了测地膜引力方法并允许重新表述为拟态嵌入引力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于从最一般的二阶导数理论出发，探索描述扩展物体在平坦时空背景中测地演化的理论框架，旨在确定产生物理合理二阶运动方程的特定子集模型。

Method: 研究方法基于从最一般的二阶导数理论出发，通过数学推导确定产生二阶运动方程的子集模型，并运用变分技术阐明暗流及其切向分量的力学功能。

Result: 研究确定了形成Lovelock型膜引力理论的模型子集，该理论扩展了测地膜引力方法，允许重新表述为拟态嵌入引力，并基于弹性理论为特定流提供了可能的起源解释。

Conclusion: Lovelock型膜引力理论自然地推广了测地膜引力的几何特性，能够重新表述为拟态嵌入引力，并引入了通过特定暗流表征的虚构物质，该虚构能量-动量张量具有类似完美流体的特性。

Abstract: Starting from the most general second-order in derivatives theories describing extended objects of arbitrary dimension evolving geodetically in a codimension-one flat ambient space-time, we determine the subset of models yielding second-order equations of motion, forming an intriguing theory known as Lovelock-type brane gravity (LBG). These models further extend the so-called geodetic brane gravity (GBG) approach, thereby naturally promoting the GBG geometric properties, allowing LBG to be reformulated as a mimetic embedding gravity and, in turn, the possibility of introducing fictional matter through a peculiar current $\mathcal{T}^{a\,μ}$. Grounded in the elasticity theory, we provide a possible origin of such a current. Finally, variational techniques are employed to elucidate the mechanical function of both the dark current $\mathcal{T}^{a\,μ}$ and its tangential components $\mathcal{T}^{ab}$; these serve as the constituents of a fictional energy-momentum tensor that shares characteristics with a perfect fluid.

### [39] [Photon rings, gravitational lensing, and ISCOs of exotic compact objects in Einstein-scalar-Maxwell theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23657)

Result: 研究证明了存在具有壳层结构的带电ECOs，其密度在中间半径处达到峰值。当要求不存在线性稳定光子环时，ECOs的光子回波（photon echoes）消失。引力透镜偏折角在撞击参数与ECOs半径同量级时达到最大值。同时确定了允许大质量粒子最内稳定圆轨道存在的参数空间范围。

Conclusion: 该研究在爱因斯坦-标量-麦克斯韦理论框架下成功构建了具有壳层结构的带电奇异致密天体模型。通过分析光子环稳定性、引力透镜效应和大质量粒子轨道等观测特征，为这类ECOs的观测识别提供了理论依据和参数约束。

Abstract: In Einstein-scalar-Maxwell theories with a coupling between the scalar field $φ$ and the electromagnetic field strength $F$ of the form $μ(φ) F$, we investigate the existence of exotic compact objects (ECOs) and their observational signatures in photon and massive-particle dynamics. For $μ(φ)$ diverging at the origin while all physical quantities remain finite, we demonstrate the existence of electrically charged ECOs with a shell-like structure whose density peaks at an intermediate radius. We compute their mass and radius, together with the scalar and vector field profiles, on a static and spherically symmetric background. We then examine the existence of photon rings and place bounds on a model parameter by requiring the absence of a linearly stable photon ring. Under this condition, photon echoes from ECOs are absent. We also compute the gravitational-lensing deflection angle $Ψ$ and show that it attains a maximum for an impact parameter of the same order as the ECO radius. ### [40] [Acoustic Black Hole in Hayward Spacetime: Shadow, Quasinormal Modes and Analogue Hawking Radiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23755)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用相对论性Gross-Pitaevskii理论构建Hayward时空中的声学黑洞模型。通过分析临界零测地线（critical null geodesics）绘制声学视界阴影，并运用WKB方法数值计算准正规模频率、灰体因子和能量发射率。

Conclusion: 本研究成功构建了规则黑洞时空中的声学黑洞模型，揭示了其物理特性随调节参数的变化规律。这些发现不仅扩展了声学黑洞的理论框架，还可能为未来天体物理黑洞观测提供新的应用可能性。

Abstract: In this paper, we study an acoustic black hole in Hayward spacetime from the relativistic Gross-Pitaevskii theory. By examining the critical null geodesics, the shadow of the acoustic horizon is sketched. Then the quasinormal mode (QNM) frequencies of the acoustic Hayward black hole are computed numerically using the WKB method, which are shown to be more stable than those of the Hayward black hole, and the variations in the QNM frequencies are shown to correlate with the behavior of the effective potential. Moreover, the WKB method is also employed to calculate the grey-body factor and energy emission rate of the analogue Hawking radiation. It is shown that, as the tuning parameter increases, both the grey-body factor and the energy emission rate are enhanced, which can likewise be attributed to changes in the effective potential. Besides, the radius of acoustic shadow increases with the tuning parameter as well. Our results not only construct an acoustic black hole in regular black hole spacetime, but may also provide potential applications in future observations of astrophysical black holes.

### [41] [Dynamical Evolutions of Electrically Charged Proca Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23829)
*Yahir Mio,Miguel Alcubierre*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了带电Proca星（charged Proca stars）的动力学稳定性，通过数值演化分析发现参数空间可分为三个区域：引力束缚稳定构型、引力束缚不稳定构型以及引力非束缚不稳定构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究构建了具有电荷参数q的稳态带电Proca星，发现存在临界电荷值qc，当q>qc时超临界解仅存在于有限电荷范围内。本文旨在通过动力学演化研究这些带电Proca星的稳定性特性。

Method: 在原有稳态构型上施加小但有限的微扰，然后在保持球对称性的条件下进行数值演化（numerical evolutions），通过时间演化追踪不稳定构型的最终状态。

Result: 对于任意给定族，参数空间可分为三个区域：引力束缚稳定构型（gravitationally bound stable configurations）、引力束缚不稳定构型以及引力非束缚不稳定构型。不稳定构型的最终状态取决于结合能（binding energy）和微扰的具体形式，可能坍缩为带电Reissner-Nordstrom黑洞、迁移到稳定分支的新状态或弥散至无穷远。

Conclusion: 带电Proca星的动力学稳定性表现出丰富的相空间结构，其最终演化命运由结合能和初始微扰特性共同决定，揭示了这类天体物理对象在广义相对论框架下的复杂动力学行为。

Abstract: In a previous work we constructed different families of stationary electrically charged Proca stars characterized by a charge parameter $q$, by solving the Einstein--Maxwell--Proca system in spherical symmetry, and imposing a harmonic time dependence ansatz for the Proca field (Mio and Alcubierre, 2025). We showed that there is a critical value for the charge $q_c$ that corresponds to the value for which the Coulomb repulsion of the charged Proca field exactly cancels the Newtonian gravitational attraction, and we found that supercritical solutions can only exist for a limited range of charges above this critical value $q>q_c$. Here we study the dynamical stability properties of these charged Proca stars by adding a small but finite perturbation to the original stationary configurations, and then performing numerical evolutions while keeping the spherical symmetry. We show that, for any given family, the parameter space can be separated into three regions corresponding to gravitationally bound stable configurations, gravitationally bound unstable configurations, and gravitationally unbound unstable configurations. For the unstable configurations we follow the evolution in time in order to determine their final state, and find that this final state can be collapse to a charged Reissner--Nordstrom black hole, migration to a new state in the stable branch, or dispersion to infinity, depending on the value of the binding energy and the specific form of the perturbation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用形状空间（shape space）上的纯粹形状动力学（pure shape dynamics），通过仿射参数化（affine parametrization）作为规范选择进行微扰分析，所有物理上有意义的结果都以参数化无关的方式表达。

Result: 中心构型（central configurations）周围的线性扰动满足形状空间上的二阶方程，其高频谱定义了一个无量纲常数c_rel。在重参数化不变性（reparametrization invariance）、谱普适性（spectral universality）和严格双曲性（strict hyperbolicity）条件下，c_rel作为涌现的光锥速度（emergent light-cone velocity），赋予乘积空间ℝ×𝒮有效的洛伦兹结构（Lorentzian structure）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，因果结构和最大信号速度可以从关系性构型空间的几何和谱特性中动态涌现，这为理解相对论运动学的起源提供了新颖的视角。

Abstract: We show that a universal propagation scale can emerge from purely relational, scale-invariant $N$-body dynamics formulated on shape space, i.e. the space of configurations modulo translations, rotations, and dilatations. Although pure shape dynamics treats only unparametrized curves as fundamental, we adopt an affine parametrization as a gauge choice to perform a perturbative analysis, with all physically meaningful results expressed in parametrization-independent terms. Linear perturbations around central configurations satisfy second-order equations on shape space whose high-frequency spectrum defines a dimensionless constant $c_{\mathrm{rel}}$. Under general conditions of reparametrization invariance, spectral universality, and strict hyperbolicity, $c_{\mathrm{rel}}$ functions as an emergent light-cone velocity, endowing the product space $\mathbb{R} \times \mathcal{S}$ with an effective Lorentzian structure. These results suggest that causal structure and a maximal signal speed may arise dynamically from the geometry and spectral properties of relational configuration space, providing a novel perspective on the origin of relativistic kinematics.

### [44] [Freezing lakes as analogue models of $Λ$CDM cosmology and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24019)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在扩展先前基于传导的湖冰生长与宇宙膨胀之间的类比，通过纳入浮力驱动的热输运（buoyancy-driven heat transport）来丰富这一物理对应关系。

Method: 重新表述了斯蒂芬问题（Stefan problem），同时考虑传导和热对流通量，推导出冰厚度s(t)的演化方程，该方程在结构上类似于宇宙学尺度因子a(t)的弗里德曼方程（Friedmann equations）。

Result: 除了重现辐射、物质和曲率类似的行为外，研究引入了热对流的简化描述，产生了两个额外的有效贡献：一个直接类似于宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）的常数项，以及一个s^{-1}项，后者在弗里德曼宇宙学形式中对应于负能量密度和状态方程参数w=-2/3的流体。

Conclusion: 结果表明演化方程之间存在结构类比，展示了经典移动边界问题中的非线性输运机制如何在简化且解析可处理的框架内重现宇宙学中熟悉的标度项层次结构。

Abstract: We extend previous conduction-based analogies between ice growth in a lake and cosmological expansion by incorporating buoyancy-driven heat transport. Reformulating the Stefan problem with both conductive and convective fluxes yields an evolution equation for the ice thickness $s(t)$ that is structurally analogous to the Friedmann equations for the cosmological scale factor $a(t)$. Beyond reproducing radiation-, matter-, and curvature-like behaviors, we introduce a reduced description of convection in which the vertically integrated heat flux reaching the moving ice-water interface is modeled as a power-law function of the instantaneous liquid-layer thickness, generating two additional effective contributions. The first is a constant term, directly analogous to a cosmological constant, arising from the persistence of buoyancy-driven transport under geometric confinement. The second is a $s^{-1}$ contribution originating from the coupling between the moving ice boundary and the convective boundary layer. This term reflects the specific reduced flux-height Ansatz adopted, rather than a universal physical prediction. When expressed in Friedmann-like cosmological form, this term entails a fluid with negative energy density and equation-of-state parameter $w=-2/3$. In cosmology this term may be an effective one associated to a network of domain walls made of exotic energy/matter, but it might also arise from an energy exchange between cosmological components. Overall, the results should be interpreted as a structural analogy between evolution equations, showing how nonlinear transport mechanisms in a classical moving-boundary problem can reproduce the hierarchy of scaling terms familiar from cosmology within a reduced and analytically tractable framework.

### [45] [The Shape of Eccentricity: Rapid Classification of Eccentric Binaries with the Wavelet Scattering Transform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24079)
*Priscilla Canizares,Seppe J. Staelens,Isobel Romero-Shaw*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究提出使用小波散射变换（wavelet scattering transform）作为引力波信号中轨道偏心率（orbital eccentricity）的快速筛选工具，以区分准圆形合并（quasi-circular mergers）与动态相互作用驱动的偏心率合并（eccentric mergers）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）探测到的引力波信号目前均与准圆形致密双星并合（quasi-circular CBCs）一致，但预计有少量通过动态相互作用驱动的并合在进入LVK探测器敏感频带时仍保留可测量的轨道偏心率（measurable orbital eccentricity）。由于偏心率引力波波形模型计算成本高昂，且偏心率信号预期稀少，对所有探测信号进行生产级推断（production-level inference）效率低下。

Method: 研究将小波散射变换（wavelet scattering transform, WST）应用于大量真实噪声中的合成波形（synthetic waveforms），并使用简单的线性和浅层神经网络分类器（linear and shallow neural-network classifiers）评估其区分能力。该方法旨在提供一种在探测与分析之间的中间步骤（intermediate step），快速评估信号中是否存在偏心率潜力。

Result: 研究发现WST表示能够有效区分偏心率双星（eccentric binaries）与准圆形双星（quasi-circular binaries），并提供引力波信号的紧凑多尺度表示（compact multi-scale representation）。该方法在10%虚警率（false alarm rate）下达到约64%的探测准确率（detection accuracy），AUC值为0.844，平均精度（average precision）为0.876。分类器在区分偏心率与自旋诱导进动（spin-induced precession）方面也表现出稳健性能。

Conclusion: 小波散射变换可作为引力波信号中轨道偏心率存在的有效快速筛选工具，为哪些信号应进行完整的偏心率推断（full eccentric inference）提供快速建议，从而优化计算资源分配，支持对动态驱动并合（dynamically driven mergers）的识别。

Abstract: The gravitational-wave (GW) detections reported by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) collaboration have so far been consistent with quasi-circular compact binary coalescences (CBCs). Nevertheless, a small fraction of binaries driven to merge through dynamical interactions in dense stellar environments or in field triples may retain measurable orbital eccentricity when entering the sensitive frequency band of LVK detectors. Confident measurement of eccentricity in the LVK band would provide strong evidence for such dynamically driven mergers; however, eccentric gravitational-waveform models are computationally expensive, and performing production-level inference on all detected signals is not an efficient use of resources when eccentric signals are expected to be rare. An intermediate step between detection and analysis, in which the signal is assessed for the potential presence of eccentricity, could provide quick recommendations for which signals should undergo full eccentric inference. We apply the wavelet scattering transform (WST) to a large set of synthetic waveforms in realistic noise and assess its discriminatory power using simple linear and shallow neural-network classifiers. We find that the WST representation enables effective discrimination between eccentric and quasi-circular binaries and provides a compact multi-scale representation of GW signals. Our approach achieves ~64% percent detection accuracy at a false alarm rate of 10%, with an AUC of 0.844 and an average precision of 0.876. We also examine the ability of our classifiers to distinguish eccentricity from spin-induced precession and find robust performance across a range of spin-precession magnitudes.

### [46] [An Upper Bound for the Mass of Microscopic Clocks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24177)

Abstract: According to general relativity, clocks are the basic measuring devices needed to probe spacetime geometry. However, it is generally accepted that the mass of clocks capable of measuring small time intervals must be bounded from below. In this article, we consider two gravitationally induced phenomena: first, the extent to which such a mass disturbs the geometry that the clocks intended to probe; second, the magnitude of the gravitational self-interaction. We adopt the semiclassical coupling between gravity and quantum matter in the non-relativistic regime to obtain upper bounds on the mass of the clocks for a given time resolution and running time.

</details>


### [47] [Dynamics of spinning particles in pp-wave spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24267)
*K. Andrzejewski*

Main category: gr-qc
