Method: 采用适当的自旋补充条件，运用多种哈密顿形式（包括非最小耦合形式），并利用与共形场相关的运动常数进行解析分析。这些方法使得对pp波时空中自旋粒子动力学的深入研究成为可能。

Result: 建立了自旋粒子在pp波时空中的运动与电磁场之间的明确关系。这一关系基于规范-引力对偶原理，揭示了两种不同物理系统之间的深刻联系。

Conclusion: 通过系统的解析研究，成功揭示了pp波时空中自旋粒子动力学与电磁场系统之间的对应关系，这为理解规范-引力对偶在具体物理系统中的应用提供了重要见解。

Abstract: In this work, we study the dynamics of a spinning particle in pp-waves spacetimes; in particular, plane gravitational waves and impulsive shockwaves. W pay special attention to analytical considerations; this is possible due to an appropriate choice of the spin supplementary condition, various Hamiltonian formalisms (including a non-minimal one) and constants of motion associated with conformal fields. Based on these results, we establish a relation between the motions of a spinning particle in pp-waves and electromagnetic fields suggested by a gauge-gravity duality.

### [48] [From QED$_3$ to Self-Dual Multicriticality in the Fradkin-Shenker Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23420)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于深入理解Fradkin-Shenker Z₂规范-希格斯格点模型的相图结构，特别是其多临界共形场论（CFT）中无质量、相互非局域的电磁粒子特性。通过引入交错推广，旨在探索具有扩展对称性的理论框架及其在量子多临界现象中的应用。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）引入交错推广的Fradkin-Shenker模型，赋予电磁粒子全局U(1)_e和U(1)_m荷；2）提出基于QED₃（具有N_f=2狄拉克费米子味和带Yukawa耦合的荷二希格斯场）的连续量子场论描述；3）使用大N_f展开计算算符标度维度；4）构建Higgs-Yukawa-QED₃与easy-plane ℂℙ¹模型间的多临界对偶。

Result: 研究结果表明：1）交错模型的多临界CFT具有(O(2)_e×O(2)_m)⋊ℤ₂ᴰ对称性，其中部分对称性在场论描述中是演生的；2）大N_f展开计算的算符标度维度与演生选择定则一致；3）通过单荷磁单极算符的变形可精确重现原始Fradkin-Shenker相图特征；4）提出的对偶关系揭示了Néel-VBS相变的一级线终止于解禁闭量子多临界点。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了交错Fradkin-Shenker模型与Higgs-Yukawa-QED₃场论间的对应关系，揭示了多临界CFT的(O(2)_e×O(2)_m)对称性结构。提出的对偶框架将规范-希格斯系统与自旋-1/2反铁磁体系统联系起来，为理解解禁闭量子临界现象提供了统一的理论描述。

Abstract: We consider the Fradkin-Shenker ${\mathbb Z}_2$ gauge-Higgs lattice model in 2+1 dimensions, i.e. the toric code deformed by an in-plane magnetic field. Its phase diagram contains a multicritical CFT with gapless, mutually non-local electric and magnetic particles, exchanged by a ${\mathbb Z}_2^{\mathsf{D}}$ self-duality symmetry. We introduce a staggered generalization of the model in which these particles carry global $U(1)_e$ and $U(1)_m$ charges, respectively, and we propose a continuum QFT description in terms of QED$_3$ with $N_f = 2$ Dirac fermion flavors and a charge-two Higgs field with Yukawa couplings. The conjectured phase diagram harbors a multicritical CFT with $(O(2)_e \times O(2)_m)\rtimes\mathbb{Z}_2^\mathsf{D}$ symmetry, some of which is emergent in the QFT description. We compute the scaling dimensions of some operators using a large-$N_f$ expansion and find agreement with the emergent selection rules. The staggered model admits a deformation to the original Fradkin-Shenker model, which maps to unit-charge monopole operators in Higgs-Yukawa-QED$_3$ that break the $U(1)_e \times U(1)_m$ symmetry. We show explicitly that this deformation reproduces all features of the Fradkin-Shenker phase diagram. Finally, we propose a multicritical duality between Higgs-Yukawa-QED$_3$ and the easy-plane $\mathbb{ CP}^1$ model (i.e. two-flavor scalar QED$_3$ with a suitable potential), which describes spin-1/2 anti-ferromagnets on a square lattice. This duality implies a first-order line of Néel-VBS transitions ending in a deconfined quantum multicritical point, described by the same $O(2)_e \times O(2)_m$ symmetric CFT that arises in the staggered Fradkin-Shenker model, which separates it from a gapped ${\mathbb Z}_2$ spin liquid phase.

### [49] [Signatures of Green's function zeros and their topology using impurity spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23477)
*Sayan Mitra,Fang Xie,Marek Kolmer,Qimiao Si,Chandan Setty*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过一维哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）的精确对角化分析，揭示了格林函数零点（Green's-function zeros）在杂质散射体系中表现为带隙内谱权重，这种"零子（zeron）"激发可通过杂质和磁场调控其拓扑性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑绝缘体（topological insulators）中格林函数零点编码了非平庸拓扑结构，但这些零点的实验探测面临挑战。研究旨在探索格林函数零点的可观测物理表现及其调控手段。

Method: 采用含杂质和塞曼场（Zeeman field）的一维哈伯德模型的精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法，辅以精确解析结果支持。在幺正散射极限（unitary scattering regime）下，将杂质问题映射到掺杂莫特绝缘体（doped Mott insulator）。

Result: 格林函数零点表现为带隙内谱权重，对应"零子"激发——吸引势下为局域双占据态（localized doublon），排斥势下为局域空穴态（holon）。零子谱权重及其关联的零点在临界塞曼场以上消失。

Conclusion: 格林函数零点可能已在实验中观测到，杂质和磁场调控可作为控制其拓扑性质的实际工具。该研究建立了拓扑特征与可观测物理量之间的直接联系。

Abstract: Topology without quasiparticles has emerged as a key framework for understanding Mott insulators, where Green's-function zeros encode nontrivial topological structure. Yet, experimental detection of these zeros represents a challenge. Using exact diagonalization of the one-dimensional Hubbard model with an impurity and Zeeman field, supported by exact analytic results, we show that Green's-function zeros manifest as an in-gap spectral weight in the unitary scattering regime. In this limit, we map the impurity problem onto a doped Mott insulator and identify the resulting in-gap state as a "zeron" excitation which is a localized doublon (holon) for an attractive (repulsive) potential. The zeron spectral weight and its associated zero vanish above a critical Zeeman field. Our results imply that Green's function zeros have in fact already been observed in experiments, and establish impurity and magnetic-field tuning as practical tools for controlling their topology.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索开放量子系统中对称保护拓扑（symmetry-protected topological, SPT）态在退相干作用下的非平衡拓扑响应，超越传统的平衡线性响应理论框架。

Method: 通过分析受乘积对称性G×S保护的SPT波函数，其中G缺陷被S荷装饰，研究局域退相干对S荷密度的作用如何诱导G对称性的自发强-弱对称破缺（spontaneous strong-to-weak symmetry breaking, SWSSB）。

Result: 研究结果表明，局域退相干普遍诱导G对称性的自发强-弱对称破缺（SWSSB）。该机制可推广至高形式对称性、空间调制对称性保护的SPT相，以及无能隙SPT态，显示退相干诱导的SWSSB超越了传统的零形式对称性框架。

Conclusion: 该研究为SPT序提供了一个定性的、通道定义的指纹，这一指纹内在于开放系统动力学，超越了平衡线性响应理论，为理解开放量子系统中的拓扑响应提供了新视角。

Abstract: We explore nonequilibrium topological responses of symmetry-protected topological (SPT) states in open quantum systems subject to decoherence. For SPT wavefunctions protected by a product symmetry G $\times$ S , where G defects are decorated with S charge, we show that local dephasing of the S charge density generically induces spontaneous strong-to-weak symmetry breaking (SWSSB) of G in the resulting mixed-state ensemble. We extend this mechanism to SPT phases protected by higher-form and spatially modulated symmetries, and further to gapless SPT states, demonstrating that dephasing-induced SWSSB persists well beyond conventional gapped 0-form settings. Our results provide a qualitative, channel-defined fingerprint of SPT order that is intrinsic to open-system dynamics and goes beyond equilibrium linear response.

### [51] [Spontaneous altermagnetism in multi-orbital correlated electron systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23522)
*Nitin Kaushal,Adarsh S. Patri,Marcel Franz*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种在强关联系统中实现自发交变磁体（spontaneous altermagnet）的新机制，通过三轨道系统规避了Goodenough-Kanamori规则的限制，并预测了手性分裂磁振子（chirally split magnons）和混合手性磁振子-轨道子（magnon-orbiton）模式的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnets）因其在自旋电子学（spintronics）和磁子学（magnonics）中的潜在应用而备受关注。然而，先前理论预测的自发交变磁体所需的自旋和轨道序违反了Goodenough-Kanamori（GK）规则，这促使研究者寻找更现实的实现途径。

Method: 研究考虑了一个具有$t_{2g}^{2}$电子的二维系统，采用无偏平均场（unbiased mean-field）和密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group）计算来提供稳定性判据。通过分析三轨道系统，揭示了规避GK规则的新微观机制。

Result: 研究识别出一种允许形成自发交变磁体莫特绝缘体（spontaneous altermagnetic Mott insulator）的新微观机制，并首次揭示了这些系统中手性分裂磁振子的存在及其微观起源。此外，预测在弱原子自旋轨道耦合（atomic spin-orbit coupling）下，施加小的面内磁场会诱导出具有非零轨道极化的混合手性磁振子-轨道子模式。

Conclusion: 具有三个活性轨道的材料为实现这种奇异态提供了更现实的途径。该研究不仅解释了如何规避GK规则，还预测了具有可测量自旋电导率和热梯度下有限纵向与横向轨道电导率的新颖激发模式，扩展了强关联系统中交变磁现象的研究范围。

Abstract: Altermagnets have attracted considerable attention in recent years owing to their potential technological applications in spintronics and magnonics. Recently, a new class of spontaneous altermagnets has been theoretically predicted in a correlated two orbital model, driven by the coexistence of antiferromagnetic spin and staggered orbital ordering, thus broadening the scope of altermagnetic phenomena to systems with strong correlations. It has been noted, however, that the required spin and orbital order violates the well-established Goodenough-Kanamori (GK) rules, which underlie much of our understanding of magnetism in complex systems. Here we show that materials with three active orbitals may offer a more realistic route to this exotic state. Specifically, we consider a two-dimensional system with $t_{2g}^{2}$ electrons and identify a novel microscopic mechanism that allows the formation of a spontaneous altermagnetic Mott insulator. We explain how the GK rules are circumvented and provide the stability criteria by employing unbiased mean-field and density matrix renormalization group calculations. In addition, for the first time, we uncover the presence and microscopic origin of chirally split magnons in these spontaneous altermagnets, with experimentally measurable spin conductivities. Finally, we predict that the application of a small in-plane magnetic field induces, in the presence of weak atomic spin-orbit coupling, an as-yet unreported hybrid chiral magnon-orbiton mode with a non-zero orbital polarization giving rise to finite longitudinal and transverse orbital conductivities under a thermal gradient.

### [52] [Generic Long-Range Order-Parameter Correlations in Metallic Quantum Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23554)
*T. R. Kirkpatrick,D. Belitz*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了金属磁体中序参量与传导电子耦合导致零温下长程关联的普遍现象，并分析了不同磁体类型中这种关联对量子相变性质的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在阐明金属磁体中序参量与传导电子耦合对零温下关联性质的影响，以及这种长程关联如何改变不同磁体类型的量子相变行为。

Method: 基于非磁相中的单粒子激发及其在序参量共轭场作用下的修正，结合重整化群（renormalization group）理论进行简单而系统的分析。

Result: 在所有类型金属磁体中，序参量与传导电子耦合导致零温下长程关联；这种关联通常将均匀磁化3-d系统、磁向列相（magnetic nematics）和交变磁体（altermagnets）的量子相变从二阶改为一阶，但非中心对称铁磁体（non-centrosymmetric ferromagnets）在3-d系统中例外。

Conclusion: 金属磁体中序参量与传导电子的耦合普遍导致零温长程关联，这种关联对不同磁体类型的量子相变性质产生系统性影响，其中在淬火无序（quenched disorder）系统中相变仍为二阶但临界行为被修正。

Abstract: It is shown that in all types of metallic magnets the coupling of the order parameter to the conduction electrons leads to an order-parameter susceptibility that is long-ranged at zero temperature. This is true for all known classes of ferromagnets, and also for antiferromagnets and spin-density wave systems, helimagnets, magnetic nematics, and altermagnets. The consequences for the magnetic quantum phase transition vary between different classes of magnets. In almost all 3-d systems with a homogeneous magnetization, as well as in magnetic nematics and in altermagnets, the long-ranged correlations generically modify the nature of the magnetic quantum phase transition from second order to first order. The only exception are non-centrosymmetric ferromagnets with a strong spin-orbit interaction, where the correlations change the order of the transition in 2-d systems, but not in 3-d ones. In helimagnets, spin-wave systems, and N{é}el antiferromagnets their effect is even weaker and does not change the order of the transition if the ordering wave number is sufficiently large. In systems with quenched disorder the transition generically is of second order, but the correlations modify the critical behavior. These conclusions are reached by very simple considerations that are based entirely on the single-particle excitations in the nonmagnetic phase and their modifications by a field conjugate to the order parameter, augmented by renormalization-group considerations.

</details>

*Li Chen,Zhiping Yao*

Method: 通过建立递归关系（recursion relation）直接定义第二量子化的Halperin态，该方法绕过了对第一量子化母哈密顿量的精确对角化需求。

Result: 验证了递归定义的第二量子化Halperin态确实是相应第二量子化母哈密顿量的零模（zero mode），并且具有正确的填充因子（filling factor）。

Conclusion: 成功开发了一种避免精确对角化的递归公式来构建Halperin态，为研究分数量子霍尔效应（fractional quantum Hall effect）中的多组分态提供了更高效的计算工具。

Abstract: We give a recursion relation for the second-quantized fermionic (bosonic) Halperin state, which avoids exact diagonalization of its two-component first-quantized parent Hamiltonian. We validate this formula by proving that the second-quantized Halperin state, as recursively defined in this formula, is indeed a zero mode of the corresponding second-quantized parent Hamiltonian and that it has the correct filling factor.

### [54] [Phonon-Assisted Photoluminescence and Ultrafast Exciton Dynamics in Two-Dimensional Silicon Carbide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23925)
*Afreen Anamul Haque,Rishabh Saraswat,Aniket Singha,Rekha Verma,Sitangshu Bhattacharya*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究采用从头算多体微扰理论（fully ab initio many body perturbation theory）分析了二维六方碳化硅（2D hexagonal silicon carbide）中的声子辅助光致发光（phonon assisted photoluminescence），揭示了其作为高效、无应变声子辅助发射平台的潜力，并建立了宽禁带二维半导体中超快激子动力学（ultrafast exciton dynamics）的定量框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声子辅助光致发光为研究低维半导体中的激子-声子相互作用（exciton-phonon interactions）提供了直接窗口。研究旨在通过对比二维六方碳化硅（h-SiC）与二维六方氮化硼（h-BN），深入理解声子辅助发射机制和激子动力学过程。

Method: 采用完全从头算多体微扰理论（fully ab initio many body perturbation theory），包括有限动量贝特-萨尔皮特方程计算（finite momentum Bethe-Salpeter calculations）。通过显式解析激子-声子矩阵元（exciton-phonon matrix elements），识别声子辅助边带形成的主要贡献者并量化其光谱权重。

Result: 研究发现高能光学TO/LO声子（optical TO/LO phonons）是边带形成的主要贡献者。h-SiC表现出与h-BN相当的显著声子辅助边带，尽管其激子-声子能量分离更小且分辨的复制峰较少。K-K激子（K-K exciton）主导近紫外零声子发射，而谷间激子（intervalley excitons）通过对称性允许的光学声子耦合获得辐射特性。温度依赖散射率显示在10K时亮激子寿命约为300fs，表明本征声子通道驱动的快速激子弛豫。

Conclusion: 研究确立了单层SiC作为对称性激活的高效、无应变声子辅助发射平台，并为宽禁带二维半导体中的超快激子动力学提供了定量框架。这些发现对于理解和设计基于声子辅助发射的低维半导体光电器件具有重要意义。

Abstract: Phonon assisted photoluminescence provides a direct window into exciton phonon interactions in low dimensional semiconductors. Using fully ab initio many body perturbation theory, including finite momentum Bethe Salpeter calculations, we investigate phonon assisted emission and exciton dynamics in two dimensional hexagonal silicon carbide and benchmark its response against 2D hexagonal boron nitride. By explicitly resolving exciton phonon matrix elements, we identify high energy optical TO LO phonons as the dominant contributors to sideband formation and quantify their spectral weights. h SiC exhibits pronounced phonon assisted sidebands comparable to h BN, despite a smaller exciton phonon energy separation and fewer resolved replicas. The bright K K exciton governs near UV zero phonon emission, while intervalley excitons acquire radiative character through symmetry allowed optical-phonon coupling. Temperature dependent scattering rates reveal an ultrashort bright exciton lifetime of approximately 300 fs at 10 K, highlighting rapid exciton relaxation driven by intrinsic phonon channels. These results establish monolayer SiC as a symmetry-activated platform for efficient, strain-free phonon-assisted emission and provide a quantitative framework for ultrafast exciton dynamics in wide bandgap 2D semiconductors.

</details>


### [55] [Quantum spin models of commensurate $p$-wave magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23986)
*GiBaik Sim,Stephan Rachel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过微观相互作用模型首次理论实现了p波磁体（p-wave magnet）作为基态，揭示了量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）在稳定该相中的关键作用，并探讨了其在自旋电子学（spintronics）中的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: p波磁体作为一种新型磁性相，在动量空间展现出奇宇称、时间反演对称的自旋劈裂，被认为是自旋电子学（spintronics）的有前景平台。然而，对其稳定机制的理论理解仍然有限。

Method: 首先引入哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）并推导相应的低能自旋哈密顿量。在经典层面分析后，进一步考虑量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）对能级简并的解除作用。

Result: 经典层面p波磁体虽稳定但与竞争的非共面态简并；量子涨落解除简并，选择p波磁体为唯一基态。所得电子结构通过埃德尔斯坦效应（Edelstein effect）展现有限自旋积累。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了自发p波磁性（spontaneous p-wave magnetism）的可能性，并讨论了理论在准二维蜂窝状磁体如Ni₂Mo₃O₈中的相关性，凸显了p波磁性在自旋电子学应用中的潜力。

Abstract: The $p$-wave magnet has emerged as a new type of magnetism exhibiting odd-parity, time-reversal-symmetric spin splitting in momentum space, and has attracted considerable interest as a promising platform for spintronic applications. However, the theoretical understanding of the fundamental mechanism responsible for stabilizing this phase remains limited. In this work, we identify a microscopic interacting model that realizes the $p$-wave magnet as its ground state. We first introduce a Hubbard model and derive the corresponding low-energy spin Hamiltonian. At the classical level, we find that the $p$-wave magnet is stabilized but remains energetically degenerate with competing noncoplanar states. Quantum fluctuations lift this degeneracy, selecting the $p$-wave magnet as the unique ground state. The resulting electronic structure exhibits finite spin accumulation via the Edelstein effect, highlighting the potential of $p$-wave magnetism for spintronic applications. We further discuss the relevance of our theory to quasi-two-dimensional honeycomb magnets such as Ni$_2$Mo$_3$O$_8$. Our findings establish the possibility of spontaneous $p$-wave magnetism.

</details>


### [56] [Triplon-mediated pairing and the superconducting gap structure in bilayer nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23989)
*Huimei Liu,Giniyat Khaliullin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过三子（triplon）介导配对机制解释了双层镍酸盐的超导能隙结构，揭示了α带能隙更大和动量依赖各向异性的微观起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究双层镍酸盐中超导能隙结构的微观机制，旨在解释实验观测到的两个关键特征：α带能隙更大（尽管其态密度较小）以及显著的能隙各向异性。

Method: 采用包含dx2-y2对称性导带与局域d3z2-r2自旋共存的模型，强层间耦合使局域矩进入单重态基态，其虚单重态-三重态激发（"三子"）介导传导电子间的配对相互作用。

Result: 该机制产生带间s+-配对，在成键β带和反键α带上具有相反的序参量符号。理论自然解释了α带能隙更大和动量依赖非局域近藤耦合导致的能隙各向异性。

Conclusion: 三子介导配对是双层镍酸盐超导性的微观起源，为理解其超导能隙结构提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the superconducting gap structure in bilayer nickelates within a model where conduction bands of dx2-y2 symmetry coexist with localized d3z2-r2 spins. Strong interlayer coupling drives the local moments into a singlet ground state, whose virtual singlet-triplet excitations ("triplons") mediate the pairing interaction between conduction electrons. This yields interband s+- pairing, with opposite signs of the order parameter on the bonding beta and antibonding alpha bands. Our theory naturally explains two key experimental features: a larger gap on the alpha band despite its smaller density of states, and pronounced gap anisotropy arising from momentum-dependent nonlocal Kondo coupling. These results support triplon-mediated pairing as the microscopic origin of superconductivity in bilayer nickelates.

### [57] [Emergence of geometric order from topological constraints in a three-dimensional Coulomb phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24051)
*Benjamin Canals*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了三维库仑相（Coulomb phase）在畴壁边界条件下有序性和几何极限形状（arctic limit shape）的涌现，揭示了三维系统中冻结与涨落自由度空间分离的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然二维六顶点模型（six-vertex model）中的北极圈现象（arctic circle phenomenon）已被充分研究，但其在三维系统中的扩展仍基本未被探索。本研究旨在理解拓扑约束与高维涌现几何之间的联系。

Method: 采用立方晶格模型，其伊辛自由度（Ising degrees of freedom）位于边上，基态流形受无散度（divergence-free）的3进/3出局部约束支配。通过应用畴壁边界条件（DWBC）并映射局部顶点极化密度（local vertex polarization density）进行数值分析。

Result: 畴壁边界条件部分解除了广泛的基态简并，在热力学极限下诱导出长程磁序。系统保留了展现库仑相特征的涨落分量，并提供了三维北极极限形状（3D arctic limit shape）的数值证据。

Conclusion: 研究成功将北极圈现象扩展到三维，揭示了拓扑约束如何在高维系统中产生涌现几何，为理解库仑相中的有序与无序共存提供了新视角。

Abstract: The emergence of order and geometric limit shapes in a three-dimensional (3D) Coulomb phase subject to domain wall boundary conditions (DWBC) is investigated. While the arctic circle phenomenon -- the spatial segregation of frozen and fluctuating degrees of freedom -- is well-established in the two-dimensional six-vertex model (square ice), its extension to 3D remains largely unexplored. A cubic lattice model with Ising degrees of freedom living on the edges, whose ground state manifold is governed by a divergence-free (3-in/3-out) local constraint, is considered. In the bulk, this model realizes a classical spin liquid characterized by algebraic correlations and pinch-point singularities in reciprocal space. It is demonstrated that applying DWBC partially lifts the extensive ground state degeneracy, inducing long-range magnetic order in the thermodynamic limit. Despite this ordering, it is found that the system retains a fluctuating component that exhibits the signature of a Coulomb phase. Finally, by mapping the local vertex polarization density, compelling numerical support is provided for a 3D generalization of the arctic limit shape, bridging the gap between topological constraints and emergent geometry in higher dimensions.

### [58] [Spontaneous Fully Compensated Ferrimagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24135)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该工作建立了自发fFIM的机制、涌现性质和材料实现的统一框架，为自旋电子学（spintronic）、谷电子学（valleytronic）和光电子学（optoelectronic）应用开辟了新的机会。

Abstract: We propose a general mechanism for the spontaneous emergence of filling-enforced fully compensated ferrimagnetism (fFIM), characterized by zero net magnetization yet ferromagnetic-like spin-split band structures. Using Hartree-Fock mean-field calculations of the Hubbard model, we map out the stability regime of spontaneous fFIM over a broad parameter space of interaction strength and staggered potential. We show the unique quantum-geometry-governed optical selection rules and the abundant valley- and spin-related physics of electronics and optics arising from the emergence of fFIM order, with tunable spin-polarized and valley-contrasting charge and spin currents. Furthermore, based on our theory, we demonstrate that spontaneous fFIM can be realized in nominally nonmagnetic graphene via defect engineering. Our results establish a unified framework for the mechanism, emergent properties, and materials realization of spontaneous fFIM, opening new opportunities for spintronic, valleytronic, and optoelectronic applications.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出涨落动力学平均场理论（fDMFT），通过功能积分将不同位点辅助杂质模型的集体涨落纳入框架。技术上，该方法涉及在自洽辅助经典场网格上获取DMFT解族。

Result: 理论的最小版本已能产生准确结果，低阶图修正仅提供微小改进。基于涨落局域场概念的框架在半满附近Hubbard模型中表现出优于其他已知DMFT图扩展的性能。

Conclusion: fDMFT为关联晶格系统提供了一个一致的理论框架，能够有效纳入长程关联，在Hubbard模型中展现出优越性能，为超越传统DMFT近似提供了新途径。

Abstract: Dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) provides an optimal local approximation for correlated lattice systems by mapping the lattice onto a self-consistent effective impurity model. To account for the missing long-range correlations, we propose a novel extended approach, which we term fluctuating dynamical mean-field theory (fDMFT). It incorporates collective fluctuations of auxiliary impurity models across different sites via functional integration. Technically, this method involves obtaining a family of DMFT solutions on a grid for a self-consistent auxiliary classical field applied to the lattice. While the result can, in principle, be improved diagrammatically, we find that the minimal version of the theory already yields accurate results, with lowest-order diagrammatic corrections offering only minor improvements. This consistent framework, based on our fluctuating local field concept, demonstrates superior performance for the nearly half-filled Hubbard model compared to other known diagrammatic extensions of DMFT.

### [60] [Vacancy-induced local moments in quantum paramagnetic phases: An SU($N$) designer Hamiltonian study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24203)
*Md Zahid Ansari,Souvik Kundu,Kedar Damle*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了非磁性杂质（空位无序）对SU(N)设计哈密顿量在二分晶格上稳定的量子顺磁相的影响。通过量子蒙特卡洛模拟发现，在价键固体有序态中，孤立空位会诱导出S=1/2的局域磁矩；而在自旋液体态中，空位不会产生局域磁矩，而是与稀释晶格最大密度二聚体堆积中的单体相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索非磁性杂质（空位无序）对SU(N)设计哈密顿量在二分晶格上稳定的量子顺磁相的影响。特别关注空位无序如何影响不同量子相中的局域磁矩形成机制。

Method: 采用量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）模拟研究低温磁化率，并使用零温投影蒙特卡洛（projector Monte Carlo）方法在价键基（valence bond basis）中分析基态波函数。在Lieb晶格上研究具有自旋液体特征的低温区域。

Result: 在价键固体有序（valence bond solid order）态中，孤立空位会诱导出S=1/2的局域磁矩，表现为磁化率的Curie尾。在自旋液体（spin liquid）态中，空位不会产生局域磁矩；局域磁矩的出现与稀释晶格最大密度二聚体堆积（maximum-density dimer packings）中的单体（monomers）相关。

Conclusion: 空位无序对量子顺磁相的影响取决于系统的基态性质：在价键固体有序态中会诱导局域磁矩，而在自旋液体态中则不会。这验证了近期关于空位无序在低温区域效应的理论论证，并揭示了局域磁矩形成机制与系统量子相性质的密切关联。

Abstract: We explore the effects of non-magnetic impurities (vacancy disorder) on the quantum paramagnetic phases stabilized by SU($N$) designer Hamiltonians on bipartite lattices. Using the results of our quantum Monte Carlo simulations, we demonstrate that isolated vacancies seed emergent spin $S=1/2$ moments in their vicinity when the low-temperature state has valence bond solid order. Indeed, our quantum Monte Carlo results for the low-temperature susceptibility in such regimes shows clear evidence of the vacancy-induced Curie tails associated with these emergent moments, and our zero-temperature projector Monte Carlo results on the ground-state wavefunction in the valence bond basis provide additional evidence in support of this picture. Further, for such designer Hamiltonians on the Lieb lattice with two additional sites on each bond of a square lattice, we identify a low-temperature spin liquid-like regime with no sign of spin or valence bond order. This liquid-like regime serves as a test bed for validating a recently-developed argument concerning the effects of vacancy disorder in such low temperature regimes. Consistent with this argument, we find that isolated vacancies do not seed emergent local moments in such spin liquids. Instead, in the presence of vacancy disorder, emergent local moments are associated with the presence of monomers in maximum-density dimer packings of the corresponding diluted lattice.

Result: 报告识别了包括"呼吸式"计算中心（"breathing" computing centers）、长期数据存储策略和软件效率认证在内的关键概念，并强调需要系统性教学、培训、指导以及新的支持形式来建立可持续的编码和计算实践。

Conclusion: 可持续转型不仅需要技术措施，还需要有针对性的意识建设、沟通策略、激励措施和社区驱动的倡议，同时伦理讨论应聚焦AI在ErUM-Data中的变革性使用，确保科学成果的责任仍由人类研究者承担。

Abstract: This workshop report from "Shaping the Digital Future of ErUM Research: Sustainability & Ethics" (Aachen, 2025) reviews progress on sustainability measures in data-intensive ErUM-Data research since the 2023 call-to-action on resource-aware research. It evaluates short-, medium-, and long-term actions around monitoring and reducing CO2 emissions, improving data and software FAIRness, optimizing workflows and computing infrastructures, and aligning operations with low-carbon energy availability, including concepts such as "breathing" computing centers, long-term data storage strategies, and software efficiency certification. The report stresses the need for systematic teaching, training, mentoring, and new support formats to establish sustainable coding and computing practices, particularly among students and early-career researchers, and highlights the importance of dedicated steering and funding instruments to embed sustainability in project planning. Ethical discussions focus on the transformative use of AI in ErUM-Data, addressing autonomy, bias, transparency, explainability, attribution of responsibility, and the risk of deskilling, while reaffirming that accountability for scientific outcomes remains with human researchers. Finally, the report emphasizes that sustainable transformation requires not only technical measures but also targeted awareness-building, communication strategies, incentives, and community-driven initiatives to move from awareness to action and to integrate sustainability and ethics into everyday scientific practice.

### [62] [Mathematical Paradoxes of Dirac Equation Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23384)
*V. P. Neznamov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文分析了狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）的Foldy-Wouthuysen和Feynman-Gell-Mann表示，发现这些表示中存在与理论物理前提相矛盾的数学悖论，提出仅使用正能量振幅态（amplitude states）可解决这些矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在研究狄拉克方程在电子（electrons）和正电子（positrons）与电磁场相互作用时的不同表示形式，特别关注量子电动力学（quantum electrodynamics）在微扰理论（perturbation theory）和非微扰强电磁场情况下的数学一致性。

Method: 方法包括分析狄拉克方程的Foldy-Wouthuysen表示和Feynman-Gell-Mann表示，考察这些表示在微扰理论和非微扰强电磁场情况下的数学性质，识别其中存在的数学悖论。

Result: 研究发现所考察的狄拉克方程表示中存在与理论物理前提相矛盾的数学伪影（mathematical artifacts），这些数学悖论可以通过仅使用正能量（包括实态和虚态）的振幅态来消除。

Conclusion: 结论表明，为确保量子电动力学的数学一致性，理论应仅采用正能量振幅态，这一限制可解决狄拉克方程不同表示中出现的数学悖论问题。

Abstract: This paper examines the Foldy-Wouthuysen and Feynman-Gell-Mann representations of the Dirac equation. The analysis is conducted for electrons and positrons interacting with electromagnetic fields. Versions of quantum electrodynamics are considered both within the scope of perturbation theory and in the nonperturbative case with strong electromagnetic fields. Mathematical artifacts that contradicting the physical premises of the theory are identified in the studied representations of the Dirac equation. These mathematical paradoxes are resolved if the theory only employs amplitude states (real and virtual) with positive energies.

### [63] [Integrability breaking in semiclassical strings in Koopman-Krylov space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23421)
*Rathindra Nath Das,Saskia Demulder*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半经典弦解中的可积性（integrability）是罕见性质，为了理解和表征非可积弦动力学的广阔图景，需要扩展Krylov方法来探测经典系统中的混沌现象。

Method: 引入Koopman-Krylov框架，该框架基于经典力学的Koopman-von Neumann描述，通过生成器扩展动态模态分解（gEDMD）来近似作用于可观测量上的Koopman生成器。

Result: 研究发现可积弦动力学的可积性破缺形变会导致谱权重的特征性重新分布，从而引起依赖于观测量的离域化和在Krylov空间中的扩散现象。

Abstract: While very powerful, integrability in semiclassical string solutions is known to be a rare property. Motivated by the need to understand and characterise the large landscape of non-integrable string dynamics, we extend Krylov methods for probing chaos to classical systems. We introduce a Koopman-Krylov framework, formulated in the Koopman-von Neumann description of classical mechanics and implemented via a generator extended dynamic mode decomposition (gEDMD) approximation of the Koopman generator acting on observables. Using this framework, we study how integrability-breaking deformations of integrable string dynamics induce characteristic redistributions of spectral weight, leading to observable-dependent delocalisation and spreading in Krylov space. We illustrate the Koopman-Krylov diagnostics across three classes of non-integrable semiclassical string solutions.

### [64] [Lightcone Bootstrap for Multipoint Defect Correlators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23428)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将光锥自举方法扩展到缺陷共形场论中的多点关联函数分析，特别是针对包含缺陷结构的共形场论体系，这有助于深入理解缺陷对共形场论谱结构的影响。

Method: 采用光锥自举方法，分析两个体算符（bulk operator）与一个缺陷算符（defect operator）的三点函数，通过要求交叉方程在光锥极限（lightcone limit）下的一致性来推导约束条件。

Result: 研究发现，为重现体通道（bulk channel）中领头扭度算符（leading-twist operator）的交换，存在两个新的扭度累积族（twist-accumulating families）的缺陷算符在大横向自旋极限下出现，并计算了这些缺陷算符的缺陷CFT数据。

Conclusion: 该工作首次将光锥自举应用于缺陷CFT的多点关联函数，揭示了缺陷谱在大横向自旋下的新结构特征，为理解缺陷共形场论的谱性质提供了新的理论工具和结果。

Abstract: We initiate the lightcone bootstrap analysis of multipoint correlators in a defect conformal field theory. The setup we consider is the three-point function of two bulk and one defect operator. Requiring consistency of the crossing equation in the lightcone limit, we find constraints on the defect spectrum at large transverse spin. Specifically, to reproduce the exchange of the leading-twist operator in the bulk channel we find two new twist-accumulating families of defect operators at large transverse spin and we compute their defect CFT data in this limit.

</details>


### [65] [A Menagerie of Wormholes and Cosmologies in the Gravitational Path Integral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23432)
*Panos Betzios,Paul Ghiringhelli,Ioannis D. Gialamas,Olga Papadoulaki*

TL;DR: 该论文分析了一类爱因斯坦-标量-麦克斯韦模型中具有渐近AdS边界条件的多种欧几里得鞍点，包括单边界解、虫洞结构以及振荡鞍点，发现了它们之间的相变，并将欧几里得虫洞解析延拓到洛伦兹FLRW宇宙，用于估计不同宇宙学结果的概率比。

Method: 采用一类爱因斯坦-标量-麦克斯韦（Einstein-Scalar-Maxwell）模型，分析包括单边界解、常规和葡萄酒杯型虫洞（wineglass wormholes）以及更奇异的（准）振荡鞍点在内的多种欧几里得鞍点构型。

Result: 发现了这些解之间的多个有趣相变，欧几里得虫洞背景可解析延拓到洛伦兹弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃克（FLRW）宇宙，其中一些包含早期暴胀期，并确定了它们在引力路径积分中成为主导鞍点的条件。

Conclusion: 通过分析这些欧几里得鞍点，论文能够估计不同宇宙学结果的概率比，为理解引力路径积分中各种几何构型的相对重要性提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We analyse a variety of Euclidean saddles in the gravitational path integral, with asymptotic AdS boundary conditions, in a class of Einstein-Scalar-Maxwell models. These include single boundary solutions, usual and wineglass wormholes, as well as more exotic (quasi)-oscillatory saddles. We find several interesting phase transitions between these solutions. The Euclidean wormhole backgrounds can be analytically continued to Lorentzian FLRW universes. Some of them contain an early period of inflation. We delineate the conditions under which they can be the dominant saddles in the gravitational path integral and use them to estimate ratios of probabilities for different cosmological outcomes.

### [66] [General Actions of Extended Objects and Volume-Preserving Diffeomorphism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23443)
*Pei-Ming Ho,Hikaru Kawai,Henry Liao*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究时空嵌入扩展物体（如弦）的世界面作用量，考虑黎曼、面积度规和体积度规三种时空背景。证明当作用量同时依赖世界面度规和诱导度规时，所有非平凡自洽作用量在经典层面等价，且体积保持微分同胚（VPD）对称性与完整微分同胚对称性物理约束力相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在系统研究扩展物体（包括弦和高维延展物体）在黎曼、面积度规和体积度规时空中的世界面作用量。动机在于统一理解包括Schild、Nambu-Goto和Polyakov作用量在内的各类作用量形式，并探讨不同对称性（体积保持微分同胚、完整微分同胚、Weyl对称性）对经典作用量的物理约束。

Method: 方法基于考虑世界面度规和诱导度规的一般函数形式作用量，分别在黎曼、面积度规和体积度规三种时空背景下分析。通过证明体积保持微分同胚（VPD）对称性与完整微分同胚对称性的等价性，建立广义Schild作用量与广义Nambu-Goto作用量的等价关系，并扩展至高维延展物体。

Result: 主要结论包括：（1）当作用量同时依赖世界面度规和诱导度规时，所有非平凡自洽作用量在经典层面等价；（2）体积保持微分同胚（VPD）对称性作为经典作用量的物理约束，与完整微分同胚对称性强度相当；（3）证明了广义Schild作用量与广义Nambu-Goto作用量的等价性，并建立了关于VPD的一般定理解释此等价性。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了不同形式弦作用量在经典层面的深层等价关系，特别是体积保持微分同胚（VPD）对称性的重要性。同时发现仅使用面积度规定义的Polyakov作用量在存在面积度规扰动时，若无其他相互作用项，无法描述临界弦（critical strings）。

Abstract: We consider actions that are general functions of the worldsheet/worldvolume metric and the induced metric for extended objects embedded in spacetime as Riemannian manifolds, areal-metric manifolds, and volume-metric manifolds. For strings on a Riemannian spacetime, we consider general actions respecting volume-preserving diffeomorphisms (VPD), general diffeomorphisms, and diffeomorphisms with Weyl symmetry, respectively. Well-known Schild, Nambu-Goto, and Polyakov actions are included as special cases. We reach two main conclusions: (1) When actions are functions of both the worldsheet metric and induced metrics, all nontrivial self-consistent actions are classically equivalent. (2) As a physical constraint on the classical action, VPD symmetry is as strong as the full diffeomorphism symmetry. The discussion is then extended to strings in spacetime manifolds equipped with the areal or volume metrics. Then, we further consider higher-dimensional extended objects in spacetime defined with areal or volume metrics, and show the equivalence between the generalized Schild actions and the generalized Nambu-Goto action. We prove a general theorem on VPD that explains this equivalence. Incidentally, while only the areal metric is needed to define the string worldsheet action, we show that the Polyakov action with an areal-metric perturbation cannot describe critical strings without other interaction terms.

Abstract: We develop an explicit model of quantum gravity coupled to the matter fields of the Standard Model, based on the 3-group structure and the 3BF action, within the framework of higher gauge theory. Finally, we discuss in some detail the structure of the resulting quantum gravity model, and provide a preliminary analysis of its semiclassical limit.

Abstract: We propose a correction to one of the elliptic blocks in the NS sector of 2d $\mathcal N = 1$ superconformal field theories. ### [70] [More on $T \overline{T}$-like deformations in higher dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24058)
*Nicolò Brizio,Moritz Kade,Alessandro Sfondrini,Dmitri P. Sorokin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了$T\overline{T}$形变（deformation）向三维及更高维场论（field theory）的多种可能推广，包括非局域非各向同性理论、Dirac-Nambu-Goto作用量（action）的流方程（flow equation），以及Born-Infeld和Dirac-Born-Infeld作用量的应力张量流（stress-tensor flow）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于将二维$T\overline{T}$形变推广到三维及更高维场论，探索不同推广路径的可行性及其理论性质。

Method: 方法包括：从二维$T\overline{T}$流出发推导其高维提升（higher-dimensional uplift）；基于Nambu-Goto作用量与$T\overline{T}$的关系，研究$d>2$维Dirac-Nambu-Goto作用量的流方程；推导$d$维Born-Infeld作用量以及$d=2$和$d=3$维Dirac-Born-Infeld作用量的应力张量流。

Result: 结果表明：二维$T\overline{T}$流的高维提升导致非局域（non-local）且非各向同性（non-isotropic）的三维理论；成功建立了仅用应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）表达的Dirac-Nambu-Goto作用量流方程；获得了Born-Infeld和Dirac-Born-Infeld作用量的应力张量流方程。

Conclusion: 本文系统研究了$T\overline{T}$形变向高维场论的多种推广方案，为理解高维可积形变（integrable deformation）提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate several possible generalisations of $T\overline{T}$ deformations to three- and higher-dimensional field theories. Starting from the two-dimensional $T\overline{T}$ flow, we work out its higher-dimensional uplift, which results in a non-local and non-isotropic three-dimensional theory. Starting instead from the relation between the Nambu-Goto action and $T\overline{T}$ in $d=2$, we study the flow equation obeyed by the Dirac-Nambu-Goto actions in $d>2$ dimensions, written in terms of the stress-energy tensor only. Similarly, we derive the stress-tensor flow obeyed by the Born-Infeld actions in $d$ dimensions and by the Dirac-Born-Infeld actions in $d=2$ and $d=3$.

### [71] [Asymptotically Solvable Quantum Circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24276)
*Samuel H. Pickering,Bruno Bertini*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究引入了一类"渐近可解（asymptotically solvable）"量子电路，其可解性约束仅影响超过可调阈值长度尺度的关联，使得系统在短时间尺度上表现通用行为，而在长时间尺度上可解析求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索如何在难以直接处理的通用情况下获得洞见，特别是理解可解性约束如何影响混沌量子电路（chaotic quantum circuits）中关联的生成，以及如何通过设计渐近可解系统来研究非平衡量子物质（non-equilibrium quantum matter）。

Method: 方法上引入了一类渐近可解量子电路家族，其可解性约束仅作用于可调阈值之外的长度尺度；通过计算平衡态（无限温度）下的动力学关联以及从兼容的非平衡初始态出发的量子淬火（quantum quenches）热化动力学来展示其特性。

Result: 结果表明，这类系统在短于阈值的时间内表现通用行为，而在长时间尺度上可解析求解；系统通常具有遍历性（ergodic），但包含一个非相互作用点（non-interacting point），可用于提供非可解早期时间区域的精确解析结果。

Conclusion: 结论是渐近可解量子电路为研究通用非平衡量子动力学提供了新框架，通过结合精确解析结果与数值实验，能够深入理解可解性约束对混沌动力学和关联生成的影响。

Abstract: The discovery of chaotic quantum circuits with (partially) solvable dynamics has played a key role in our understanding of non-equilibrium quantum matter and, at the same time, has helped the development of concrete platforms for quantum computation. It was shown that solvability does not prevent the generation of chaotic dynamics, however, it imposes non-trivial constraints on the generated correlations. A natural question is then whether it is possible to gain insight into the generic case despite the latter being very hard to access. To address this question here we introduce a family of 'asymptotically solvable' quantum circuits where the solvability constraints only affect correlations on length scales beyond a tuneable threshold. This means that their dynamics are only solvable for long enough times: for times shorter than the threshold they are generic. We show this by computing both their dynamical correlations on the equilibrium (infinite temperature) state and their thermalisation dynamics following quantum quenches from compatible (asymptotically solvable) non-equilibrium initial states. The class of systems we introduce is generically ergodic but contains a non-interacting point, which we use to provide exact analytical results, complementing those of numerical experiments, on the non-solvable early time regime.

</details>


### [72] [Information bound on navigation speed in smart active matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23988)
*Kristian Stølevik Olsen,Mitsusuke Tarama,Hartmut Löwen*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种自适应活性粒子模型，通过结合基于更新的间歇性运动与克拉默-拉奥不等式，推导出适用于多种信息处理策略的导航速度界限，揭示了认知系统的关键特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生命系统中智能行为常源于信息收集、处理和行动能力，而传统活性物质（active matter）框架通常忽略内部信息处理和决策过程。本研究旨在开发包含最小信息处理能力的自适应活性粒子模型，以实现对远距离目标的导航。

Method: 提出自适应活性粒子模型，结合基于更新（renewal-based）的间歇性运动与克拉默-拉奥不等式（Cramér-Rao inequality），推导导航速度界限。该框架能够捕捉认知系统的标志性特征，包括最优感知持续时间和平衡噪声与可靠性的速度-精度权衡（speed-accuracy trade-off）。

Result: 研究推导出适用于广泛信息处理策略的导航速度界限。允许存储信息在行动前退化（degrade）的分析表明，虽然信息劣化会减缓导航速度，但权衡关系主要受外部定向噪声（orientational noise）支配，且对记忆衰减（memory decay）表现出显著不敏感性。

Conclusion: 该自适应活性粒子框架成功将信息处理能力整合到活性物质研究中，揭示了认知系统的基本特征，包括最优感知策略和速度-精度权衡，为理解生命系统中信息处理与运动行为的耦合提供了新视角。

Abstract: Intelligent behavior in life-like systems often arises from the ability to gather, process, and act on information. While active matter provides a framework for studying life-like dynamics, it typically omits internal information-processing and decision-making. Here we introduce an adaptive active particle model that uses minimal information processing capabilities in order to navigate towards a distant target. By combining renewal-based intermittent motion with the Cramér-Rao inequality, we derive a bound on the navigation speed valid for a wide range of information processing strategies. The framework captures hallmark features of cognitive systems, including optimal sensing durations and a speed-accuracy trade-off that balances noise and reliability. Allowing stored information to degrade before action reveals that although deterioration slows navigation, the trade-off remains governed primarily by external orientational noise and is remarkably insensitive to memory decay.

</details>


### [73] [Exact Anomalous Current Fluctuations in Quantum Many-Body Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24008)
*Kazuya Fujimoto,Taiki Ishiyama,Taiga Kurose,Takato Yoshimura,Tomohiro Sasamoto*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文首次在量子多体系统中精确推导出M-Wright函数，通过分析一维无限强排斥相互作用费米-哈伯德模型中的自旋流积分，为探索量子多体系统中的反常积分电流奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管反常电流涨落（以M-Wright函数为特征）已在经典自动机中精确获得，且多种经典系统均能产生此类反常行为，但在量子多体系统中精确推导M-Wright函数一直未能实现。这类反常行为捕捉了一维多体输运的普遍性特征，引起了广泛关注。

Method: 通过分析一维费米-哈伯德模型（Fermi-Hubbard model）中无限强排斥相互作用下的积分自旋电流（integrated spin current），实现了量子多体动力学的精确微观推导。

Result: 首次在量子多体系统中获得了M-Wright函数的精确微观推导，为一维无限强排斥相互作用费米-哈伯德模型中的积分自旋电流提供了理论框架。

Conclusion: 该研究结果为探索广泛量子多体系统中的反常积分电流（anomalous integrated currents）奠定了基础，填补了量子领域反常电流涨落精确理论推导的空白。

Abstract: Fluctuations of integrated currents have attracted considerable interest over the past decades in the context of statistical mechanics. Recently, anomalous current fluctuations, characterized by the M-Wright function, were obtained exactly in a classical automaton [$Ž$. Krajnik et al., Phys. Rev. Lett. 128, 160601 (2022)], and previous studies have shown that the anomalous behavior can arise in a variety of classical systems. Despite the rapidly growing interest in such anomalous behaviors, which capture a universal aspect of one-dimensional many-body transport, the exact derivation of the M-Wright function in quantum many-body systems has remained elusive. In this Letter, we present the first exact microscopic derivation of the M-Wright function in quantum many-body dynamics by analyzing the integrated spin current in a one-dimensional Fermi-Hubbard model with infinitely strong repulsive interactions. Our results lay the groundwork for exploring anomalous integrated currents in a broad class of quantum many-body systems.

</details>

Result: 获得了嵌套高斯分布（nested Gaussian distribution），其方差与自旋扩散常数和静态自旋磁化率存在解析关系，揭示了XXZ链中反常涨落与单文件系统中反常电荷涨落具有相同的物理机制。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了观测到的反常涨落的普适流体动力学起源（universal hydrodynamic origin），为理解量子自旋链中的非平衡统计行为提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The quantum XXZ spin-1/2 chain features non-Gaussian spin current fluctuations in the regime of easy-axis anisotropy. Using ballistic macroscopic fluctuation theory, we derive the exact probability distribution of typical spin-current fluctuations in thermal equilibrium. The obtained nested Gaussian distribution is fully characterized by its variance which we analytically relate to the spin diffusion constant and static spin susceptibility, and compare our with numerical simulations. By unveiling how the same mechanism which leads to anomalous charge current fluctuations in single-file systems manifests in the XXZ chain, our approach establishes the universal hydrodynamic origin of the observed anomalous fluctuations.

### [76] [Imprints of $U_A(1)$ chiral anomaly and disorder in the Dirac eigenspectrum of QCD at finite temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24227)
*Ravi Shanker,Harshit Pandey,Sayantan Sharma*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该研究通过格点QCD计算，系统分析了狄拉克本征值谱随温度变化的性质，揭示了中间能级统计与手征对称性有效恢复及无序效应之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于深入理解QCD中狄拉克本征值谱的性质，特别是其如何反映多体系统中相互作用与无序（disorder）的相互作用，以及手征对称性（chiral symmetry）不同子群的有效恢复信息。

Method: 采用重叠狄拉克算子（overlap Dirac operator）计算2+1味QCD系综的红外本征值，这些系综使用畴壁费米子离散化（domain wall fermion discretization）生成于大体积格点。通过归一化能级间距比（normalized level spacing ratios）识别具有中间能级统计（intermediate level statistics）的本征值，并利用特定随机矩阵模型（random matrix model）解释这些中间能级比。

Result: 研究发现存在具有中间能级统计的本征值，这些本征值与规范场中的无序（disorder）存在关联，表现为重整化Polyakov圈（renormalized Polyakov loop）值的相关性。中间本征模（intermediate eigenmodes）的存在与手征交叉转变（chiral crossover transition）附近手征对称性不同子群的有效恢复密切相关，而在较高温度下，当$U_A(1)$对称性有效恢复时，这些模式源于随机不相关无序（random uncorrelated disorder）的效应。

Conclusion: 研究首次计算了狄拉克谱的Thouless电导（Thouless conductance），该量可量化本征矢的结构刚性（structural rigidity），并作为诊断工具来理解反常$U_A(1)$手征对称性子群的恢复以及由无序驱动的局域化（localization）现象。

Abstract: We perform a comprehensive study of the properties of Dirac eigenvalue spectrum in QCD as a function of temperature on the lattice. In addition to effects due to interplay between interactions and disorder inherently present in a many-body system, the Dirac spectrum also contains crucial information about the effective restoration of different subgroups of almost exact two flavor chiral symmetry in QCD. We calculate the infrared eigenvalues of the overlap Dirac operator on 2+1 flavor QCD ensembles generated using domain wall fermion discretization, on a large volume lattice. From the normalized level spacing ratios we identify those eigenvalues which have intermediate level statistics, distinctly different from the majority in the bulk spectrum that follow universal level fluctuations similar to a random matrix of Gaussian unitary type. We provide an explanation of these intermediate level ratios in terms of a specific random matrix model and quantify correlation between these eigenstates and disorder in the gauge fields manifested in the renormalized Polyakov loop values. Whereas existence of these intermediate eigenmodes are intimately connected to the effective restoration of different subgroups of chiral symmetry close to chiral crossover transition, these arise due to effects of random uncorrelated disorder at higher temperatures when the $U_A(1)$ is effectively restored. We also, for the first time, calculate the Thouless conductance for the Dirac spectrum that quantifies the structural rigidity of the eigenvectors, and use it as a diagnostic tool to understand the restoration of the anomalous $U_A(1)$ subgroup of chiral symmetry and localization driven due to disorder.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超冷分子因其丰富的相互作用而在量子物质、化学动力学和信息处理领域具有重要价值，这些相互作用可通过外场调控。虽然磁场已通过Feshbach共振实现相互作用调控，但电场控制原子-分子Feshbach共振尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 研究采用基态钠-钾分子与钾原子的混合物，通过施加电场系统性地调控原子-分子Feshbach共振位置，分析共振位移与特定三原子束缚态的关系。

Conclusion: 电场为原子-分子共振提供了独立调控手段，开启了三原子量子态的光谱学研究途径，推进了可控多原子量子物质的发展。

Abstract: Ultracold molecules provide opportunities for exploring quantum matter, chemical dynamics and information processing thanks to their rich interactions, which can be controlled by external fields. Magnetic fields tune interactions through Feshbach resonances, enabling the formation of ultracold dimers and triatomic molecules from atom-dimer collisions. Here we demonstrate electric-field control of atom-molecule Feshbach resonances. In mixtures of ground-state sodium-potassium molecules and potassium atoms, electric fields shift resonance positions systematically, revealing specific trimer bound states and their electric-field dependent energies. The response differs markedly from isolated dimers, showing hindered rotation of the molecular constituent near an atom. Electric fields therefore add an independent knob for atom-molecule resonances, open spectroscopic access to triatomic quantum states, and advance controlled polyatomic quantum matter.

### [78] [Black hole scalar sirens in the Milky Way](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23415)
*Daniel Gavilan-Martin,Olivier Simon,Dhashin Krishna,Derek F. Jackson Kimball,Dmitry Budker,Arne Wickenbrock*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出黑洞标量警报（BH scalar sirens）概念，即自旋黑洞通过超辐射不稳定性产生标量粒子云，在强自相互作用下持续发射标量粒子，形成可观测的天体物理源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索一类新型天体物理标量粒子源，这类源不依赖于早期宇宙产生机制或宇宙学初始条件，为探测孤立黑洞和标量粒子提供独立目标。

Method: 通过计算银河系中约10^8个孤立恒星质量黑洞的标量粒子背景，分析标量云在超辐射不稳定性下的增长和耗散过程，特别关注粒子自相互作用（由衰变常数f表征）的影响。

Result: 发现黑洞标量警报在质量范围10^{-13}-10^{-11} eV和f≲10^{14}-10^{9} GeV内有效，产生的观测信号比该质量范围内的宇宙标量背景强两个数量级，且能谱更宽、速度更高（达~10^{-1}c）。

Conclusion: 标量粒子发射为探测孤立黑洞提供了新途径，揭示了标量粒子与黑洞联合发现的潜力，并激励在多个质量数量级上搜索标量粒子。

Abstract: Hypothetical light scalar particles trigger the superradiant instability around spinning black holes (BHs), causing clouds of scalars to grow around the BH. In the presence of sufficiently strong particle self-interactions (characterized by the decay constant $f$), scalars are ejected from BH orbits, resulting in coherent, non-relativistic emissions that continuously carry away the BH's angular momentum. Parameters exist for which cloud growth is much faster, and scalar depletion is much slower, than the age of the Galaxy. This defines a distinct class of astrophysical sources of scalars, which we call \emph{BH scalar sirens} -- BHs that persistently emit scalars effectively forever. We compute the scalar background from the expected population of $N_\text{BH}\sim 10^{8}$ isolated stellar-mass BHs in the Milky Way, which are sirens for scalars in the mass range $10^{-13}$--$10^{-11}\,$eV and $f\lesssim 10^{14}$--$10^{9}\,$GeV. This provides a detection target independent of early-universe scalar production or cosmological initial conditions. The generated observable signals are up to two orders-of-magnitude larger than those expected from a misaligned cosmic scalar in this mass range. The energy spectrum of emitted scalars is distinctly broader and at higher velocities (up to $\sim 10^{-1}c$) than that of virialized dark matter, and encodes the mass and spin distributions of the BH population. While stellar-mass Milky Way BHs are our primary target, our framework extends to supermassive, intermediate-mass and light BHs. Given the difficulty of directly observing populations of isolated BHs, scalar emissions offer a novel probe of these otherwise invisible objects, highlighting the potential for joint discovery between scalars and BHs, and broadly motivating searches for scalars over many orders-of-magnitude in mass.

</details>

Conclusion: 结论指出，结合量子信息启发的变量能够显著提高对顶夸克偶素效应的探测灵敏度，为探索这些微妙特征带来了新途径。该方法为研究近阈值顶夸克-反顶夸克产生过程中的量子特性提供了创新工具。

Abstract: We investigate near-threshold top-antitop production at the LHC, focusing on the impact of toponium formation on spin correlations and quantum information properties of the final state. Considering the top-antitop system as a mixed two-qubit state, we reconstruct spin density matrices via quantum tomography and evaluate several observables including some inspired by quantum information. We then compare their sensitivity in discriminating toponium effects from top-antitop production without these effects. Our results demonstrate that combining these variables is expected to significantly enhance sensitivity to toponium effects, bringing new ways to explore these subtle features.

### [80] [Kaons ($K^\pm$) in hot and dense QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24170)
*K. Azizi,G. Bozkır,N. Er,A. Türkan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文采用QCD求和规则（QCD sum-rule）系统研究了带电K介子双重态$K^{\pm}$在重离子实验相关温度-密度平面上的介质内性质，发现$K^{-}$质量随密度和温度单调下降，并观察到由Weinberg-Tomozawa矢量相互作用驱动的显著质量劈裂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于系统分析带电K介子双重态$K^{\pm}$在当前和未来重离子实验相关的完整温度-密度平面上的介质内性质，以理解手征对称性部分恢复的渐进过程。

Method: 方法基于QCD求和规则（QCD sum-rule）框架，结合温度与密度依赖的夸克、胶子和混合凝聚（condensates），推导出有效质量$m_{K^{\pm}}$、赝标量衰变常数$f_{K^{\pm}}$和矢量自能$Σ_{v}$的Borel变换求和规则。

Result: 真空结果$m_{K^{-}} = 494.6^{+4.9}_{-6.9}$~MeV和$f_{K^{-}} = 157.3^{+4.1}_{-2.9}$~MeV与粒子数据组（Particle Data Group）值在亚百分比水平高度一致。介质中$m_{K^{\pm}}$随重子密度和温度增加单调下降，表明手征对称性渐进部分恢复。在重子物质中观察到显著质量劈裂$Δm = m_{K^{-}} - m_{K^{+}}$，在$T=0$、$ρ\simeq 3.2\,ρ_{\rm sat}$时达到$|Δm| \sim 0.35$~GeV。

Conclusion: 研究核心成果是提取了临界起始密度$ρ_c$，该阈值标志着$K^{-}$性质的介质内修正开始向手征恢复相转变。需要强调的是，$ρ_c(T)$不应被解释为QCD临界点的精确确定，而应视为手征对称性恢复转变开始的指示器。

Abstract: We present a systematic QCD sum-rule analysis of the in-medium properties of the charged kaon doublet $K^{\pm}$ over the full $(T,ρ)$ plane relevant to current and forthcoming heavy-ion experiments. Working within the QCD sum-rule framework and incorporating temperature-and density-dependent quark, gluon, and mixed condensates, we derive Borel-transformed sum rules for the effective masses $m_{K^{\pm}}$, the pseudoscalar decay constants $f_{K^{\pm}}$, and the vector self-energy $Σ_{v}$ of both charged states simultaneously. Our vacuum results, $m_{K^{-}} = 494.6^{+4.9}_{-6.9}$~MeV and $f_{K^{-}} = 157.3^{+4.1}_{-2.9}$~MeV (with near-degenerate $K^{+}$ values), are in excellent agreement with Particle Data Group values at the sub-percent level. In the medium, $m_{K^{\pm}}$ decreases monotonically with increasing baryon density and temperature, signalling progressive partial restoration of chiral symmetry. A pronounced mass splitting $Δm = m_{K^{-}} - m_{K^{+}}$ develops in baryonic matter, driven by the opposite sign of the Weinberg--Tomozawa vector interaction for the two charge states; it reaches $|Δm| \sim 0.35$~GeV near $ρ\simeq 3.2\,ρ_{\rm sat}$ at $T = 0$ and is partially quenched by thermal fluctuations. A central outcome of this study is the extraction of the critical onset density $ρ_c$, defined as the threshold beyond which the in-medium modifications of $K^{-}$ properties signal the onset of the transition toward the chirally restored phase. We stress that $ρ_c(T)$ should not be interpreted as a precise determination of the QCD critical point-a task beyond the reach of any current effective framework-but rather as an indicator ....

Conclusion: AUSSIE方法在解决LHC物理中的逆问题时，无需传统迭代机制即可保持渐近正确性，同时最小化对参考模拟的依赖。

AUSSIE replaces the second OmniFold step with a new loss function that directly yields solutions with minimal dependence on the reference simulation. We showcase AUSSIE on various unfolding tasks, including full-phase-space jet substructure.

### [82] [Fermion Mass Hierarchy and a High Quality Axion From Gauged U(1) Flavor Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24253)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在同时解决粒子物理中的两个基本问题：费米子质量和混合的层次结构（flavor hierarchy）以及强CP问题（strong CP problem）。通过将Froggatt-Nielsen机制与Peccei-Quinn机制统一在一个框架中，寻求对这两个问题的协同解决方案。

Method: 研究提出基于规范U(1)_F味道对称性（gauged U(1)_F flavor symmetry）的模型框架，其中全局U(1)_PQ对称性作为规范对称性的副产品自然出现。该方法构建了三个DFSZ轴子模型的推广版本，将右手中微子质量标度识别为Froggatt-Nielsen标度，并提供了FN扇区的显式紫外完备化。

Result: 该框架产生了高质量轴子（high-quality axion），其势能受规范对称性保护免受量子引力修正影响。轴子同时作为味子场（flavon field），在中性介子的味改变衰变中产生可检验的预测。轴子还作为宇宙暗物质，产生正确的遗迹丰度且不引起宇宙学畴壁问题。通过轻子生成实现的重子不对称性在模型中可计算且量级正确。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一个统一框架，同时解释了费米子质量层次结构和强CP问题，并将轴子物理与味物理、暗物质、重子不对称等基本现象有机结合。模型提供了可检验的预测，并保持了轴子的高质量特性。

Abstract: We present a class of models based on a gauged $U(1)_F$ flavor symmetry that explains the hierarchical structure of fermion masses and mixings via the Froggatt-Nielsen (FN) mechanism, while also solving the strong CP problem by the Peccei-Quinn (PQ) mechanism. A global $U(1)_{\rm PQ}$ symmetry with a nonzero QCD anomaly emerges accidentally in this setup as a byproduct of the gauged $U(1)_F$ symmetry. The resulting axion is shown to be of high quality, with the axion potential safeguarded against quantum gravity corrections by the gauge symmetry. Three models, which are generalizations of the Dine-Fischler-Srednicki-Zhitnitsky (DFSZ) axion model, are presented realizing this idea. The right-handed neutrino mass scale is identified as the Froggatt-Nielsen scale in these models. We present explicit UV completions of the FN sectors of these models and show that they preserve the high quality of the axion. In these models, the axion acts as a flavon field, leading to testable predictions in flavor-changing decays of neutral mesons. The axion also serves as the dark matter of the universe with the right amount of relic abundance without causing cosmological domain wall problems. Baryon asymmetry of the universe is realized via leptogenesis which is calculable in these models and found to be of the right order of magnitude.

</details>

### [83] [Transport properties of monodisperse and bidisperse hard-sphere colloidal suspensions from multiparticle collision dynamics simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23472)
*Michael P. Howard*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究使用多粒子碰撞动力学（multiparticle collision dynamics）模拟了单分散和双分散硬球胶体悬浮液的剪切粘度、长时间自扩散系数和沉降速度，体积分数最高达0.40，为胶体悬浮液的输运性质提供了参考数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在为胶体悬浮液的输运性质（transport properties）提供参考数据，并验证多粒子碰撞动力学方法在模拟不同尺寸粒子悬浮液中的适用性。

Method: 采用多粒子碰撞动力学（multiparticle collision dynamics）结合离散粒子模型，模拟了体积分数最高达0.40的单分散和双分散硬球胶体悬浮液。双分散体系直径比为2和4，且每种粒子的体积分数相等。

Result: 单分散悬浮液的所有测量性质与先前文献吻合良好，但突显了模拟方法对离散化效应（discretization effects）的敏感性。双分散悬浮液的沉降速度与先前文献合理一致，包括直径比为4时较小粒子的方向反转现象。

Conclusion: 该工作为胶体悬浮液的输运性质提供了参考数据，并确立了多粒子碰撞动力学方法在模拟不同尺寸粒子悬浮液中的适用性。

Abstract: The shear viscosities, long-time self-diffusion coefficients, and sedimentation velocities in monodisperse and bidisperse hard-sphere colloidal suspensions are simulated for volume fractions up to 0.40 using multiparticle collision dynamics with a discrete particle model. The bidisperse suspensions have diameter ratios of 2 and 4 and equal amounts of each particle by volume. All measured properties for monodisperse suspensions are found to be in good agreement with prior literature; however, they highlight the sensitivity of the simulation method to discretization effects. The sedimentation velocities for the bidisperse suspensions are also in reasonable agreement with prior literature, including direction reversal for the smaller particles when the diameter ratio is 4. This work provides reference data for transport properties of colloidal suspensions and establishes the suitability of multiparticle collision dynamics for modeling suspensions of particles with different sizes.

### [84] [Universal Scaling of Macroscopic Softening and Microscopic Scission in Phantom Chain Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23669)
*Yuichi Masubuchi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了幻象链聚合物网络断裂的复杂性可完全解耦为两条普适主曲线：宏观软化由绝对拉伸主导，微观断裂仅由相对拉伸控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在解析幻象链聚合物网络（phantom-chain polymer networks）断裂中表观复杂性的物理本质，探索宏观力学响应与微观损伤机制之间的解耦关系。

Method: 基于先前提出的网络力学模型（network mechanics model），推导了定量描述微观损伤非线性增长的解析表达式，并结合聚合物溶液标度理论进行分析。

Result: 研究发现断裂复杂性可解耦为两条普适主曲线：宏观软化由绝对拉伸控制，微观断裂仅由相对拉伸主导。结合软化指数与聚合物溶液标度，得到了新颖的强度-模量关系：$σ_{nb} / G \propto (c / c^* )^{(-1/3)}$。

Conclusion: 幻象链聚合物网络的断裂行为可通过绝对拉伸与相对拉伸的分离进行完全解耦，这一发现为理解聚合物网络断裂的普适规律提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: This study demonstrates that the apparent complexity of fracture in phantom-chain polymer networks is fully decoupled into two universal master curves: (i) macroscopic softening governed by the absolute stretch, and (ii) microscopic scission governed solely by the relative stretch. Using the previously proposed network mechanics model, an analytical expression has been derived to quantitatively capture the nonlinear growth of microscopic damage. Combining the softening exponent with polymer-solution scaling yields a simple novel relationship, $σ_{nb} / G \propto (c / c^* )^{(-1/3)}$, where $σ_{nb}$ is the nominal broken strength, $G$ is the initial shear modulus, $c$ is the prepolymer concentration, and $c^*$ is its overlapping threshold.

</details>


### [85] [Exponential Stress Relaxation Driven by Elementary Plastic Events in Non-Ageing Liquid Foams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23690)
*F. Schott,B. Dollet,C. M. Schlepütz,C. Claudet,S. Gstöhl,R. Mokso,S. Santucci,C. Raufaste*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究利用快速X射线断层流变技术（fast X-ray tomo-rheoscopy）揭示了液态泡沫（liquid foams）在流动停止后的应力松弛（stress relaxation）行为，发现其遵循指数松弛规律，而非传统非晶固体中的幂律松弛或级联相关事件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液态泡沫作为典型的非热非晶固体（athermal amorphous solids），其弹性源于密集堆积气泡的堵塞（jamming）。研究旨在探究这类材料在流动停止后的应力松弛机制，特别是其与塑性活动（plastic activity）和配位数（coordination number）的关系。

Method: 采用快速X射线断层流变技术进行原位、时间分辨测量，监测液态泡沫在流动停止后的应力松弛过程。该方法能够同时追踪剪切应力、塑性活动和配位数的动态变化。

Result: 研究发现剪切应力、塑性活动和配位数在整个松弛过程中保持稳健的线性仿射关系（linear affine relationships），最终达到低于屈服值的残余应力状态（residual stress state）。松弛过程呈现指数规律，由单个塑性事件的持续时间主导，而非传统非晶固体中与剪切速率相关的级联相关事件。

Conclusion: 实验结果与Cuny等人提出的理论框架一致，表明残余应力源于应力张量的取向（orientation of the stress tensor）。该研究揭示了液态泡沫独特的松弛机制，区别于其他非晶固体材料。

Abstract: Liquid foams are archetypal athermal amorphous solids whose elasticity arises from the jamming of densely packed bubbles. We investigate the stress relaxation of non-ageing liquid foams following flow cessation, using fast X-ray tomo-rheoscopy. Thanks to in situ, time-resolved measurements, we uncover robust linear affine relationships between shear stress, plastic activity, and coordination number throughout the relaxation toward a residual stress state below the yield value. In contrast to previous studies on amorphous solids, we observe an exponential relaxation governed by the duration of individual plastic events, rather than by cascades of correlated ones associated with much longer, shear-rate-dependent timescales or power-law relaxations. Our results are consistent with a recent theoretical framework proposed by Cuny et al., suggesting that residual stress originates from the orientation of the stress tensor.

### [86] [Modeling of polymer phase transition from crystalline to conformationally disordered phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23756)
*V. V. Atrazhev,D. V. Dmitriev,V. I. Sultanov*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个基于物理的分析模型，用于描述从晶态到构象无序（condis）晶态的相变过程。该模型将自由能表示为温度和晶格参数（相邻链间平均距离）的函数，包含弹性和构象两个贡献项，成功预测了聚乙烯在不同压力下的相变行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立描述聚合物从晶态向构象无序晶态（condis phase）相变的物理模型。聚乙烯作为最简单的具有condis相的聚合物，被选为建模对象以验证该方法的有效性。

Method: 方法包括构建基于物理的分析模型，将自由能表达为温度和晶格参数的函数，包含弹性和构象两个贡献项。弹性项描述相邻链间的相互作用，构象项考虑单链在由相邻链形成的势管内的构象。模型参数通过分子动力学模拟结果进行校准。

Result: 模型成功描述了相变的物理图像：形成缺陷所需的能量随相邻链间距离增大而迅速降低，导致在一定温度下发生一级相变至condis相。模型在常压下的参数校准后，对500 atm和1000 atm压力的预测与分子动力学模拟结果完全一致。

Conclusion: 提出的分析模型有效描述了从晶态到构象无序晶态的相变物理机制。该模型不仅解释了实验观察到的现象，其在不同压力下的预测也与分子动力学模拟结果高度吻合，验证了模型的可靠性和适用性。

Abstract: A physics-based analytical model describing the phase transition from crystalline to conformationally disordered (condis) crystalline phase is developed. In the model, the free energy is written as a function of temperature and the lattice parameter (mean distance between neighboring chains). It consists of two contributions: elastic and conformational. The elastic contribution describes the interaction between neighboring chains, while the conformational part takes into account the conformation of one chain inside the potential tube, formed by the neighboring chains. To verify this approach, polyethylene - the simplest polymer possessing the condis phase - was chosen as a modeling object. Previous experiments and molecular dynamics simulations show that the typical conformation of a polymer chain in a crystalline phase consists mainly of trans dihedrals and a small fraction of gauche dihedrals, which can be considered as defects of the crystalline lattice. These defects displace the chain inside the tube thus increasing the potential energy. The energy required to form such a defect decreases rapidly with increasing distance between neighboring chains. This leads to a first-order phase transition at a certain temperature to the condis phase, in which distance between neighboring chains is large and a fraction of gauche dihedrals is high. This physical picture of the phase transition is described by the proposed analytical model, the parameters of which were calibrated against the results of molecular dynamics simulations for atmospheric pressure. The model predictions for the pressure of 500 atm and 1000 atm are in perfect agreement with the results of molecular dynamics simulations.

</details>

### [88] [Self-Buckling of Pressurized Cylindrical Tubes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23836)
*Morten Opstrup Andersen,Nikolaj Tønner Osvald Olsen,Diksha Bhola,Aleca Borsuk,Craig Brodersen,Anja Geitmann,Matteo Pezzulla*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过有限元模拟和桌面实验，探究了空心圆柱管在自重和内压作用下的屈曲行为，发现正内压可增强不稳定圆柱的刚度，而负压则导致稳定圆柱屈曲。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于双子叶植物叶栅栏组织柱状细胞的力学特性，这些细胞类似于受压的圆柱管。旨在探究重力与压力相互作用对空心圆柱管机械稳定性的影响。

Method: 采用有限元模拟（FEM simulations）和桌面尺度实验（desktop-scale experiments）相结合的方法。首先验证无压自重屈曲（self-buckling）模型，然后确定不同几何参数下的临界屈曲压力。

Result: 研究发现正内压可增强自重下不稳定圆柱的刚度，其有效杨氏模量（effective Young's modulus）与施加压力呈线性比例关系。相反，自重下稳定的圆柱在负压下会发生屈曲，这与经典的压力诱导环屈曲（pressure-induced ring buckling）结果相似。

Conclusion: 研究结果为重力与压力相互作用对空心圆柱管机械不稳定性的影响提供了新见解，对工程和生物结构在类似载荷下的研究具有参考价值。

Abstract: We investigate the buckling of hollow cylindrical tubes subject to their own weight and internal pressure, inspired by the columnar cells of the palisade mesophyll in dicotyledon leaves which resemble pressurized cylindrical tubes. When the internal pressure in the cylinder is equal to the outside pressure, the problem is usually termed self-buckling, which has been studied extensively for solid rods, hollow cylinders, and thin cylindrical shells. Specifically, we perform FEM simulations and desktop-scale experiments to determine the instability thresholds for different geometrical parameters. We first test our models against self-buckling results without pressure for solid rods and hollow cylindrical tubes, and then proceed to determine the critical buckling pressure for a set of material and geometrical parameters. We find that positive internal pressures can stiffen cylinders that are unstable under their own weight, leading to an effective Young's modulus that we show scales linearly with the applied pressure. On the contrary, cylinders that are stable under self-weight, buckle under a negative pressure, resembling classical results on pressure-induced ring buckling. Our findings offer new insights on the interplay between gravity and pressure for the mechanical instability of hollow cylindrical tubes, which we hope will be useful for the study of both engineering and biological structures under similar loads.

</details>


### [89] [Thermodynamic effects of solid electrolyte interphase formation from solvation and ionic association in water-in-salt electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23875)
*Daniel M. Markiewitz,Michael McEldrew,Conor M. E. Phelan,Qianlu Zheng,Jasper Singh,Robert S. Weatherup,Rosa M. Espinosa-Marzal,Martin Z. Bazant,Zachary A. H. Goodwin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过热力学理论分析水包盐电解质（WiSEs）中电化学稳定窗口（ESW）的扩展机制，重点关注双电层（EDL）中的水合作用和离子缔合，并利用分子动力学模拟进行参数化和验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水包盐电解质（Water-in-Salt-Electrolytes, WiSEs）作为下一代电解质具有广阔前景，其电化学稳定窗口（electrochemical stability window, ESW）的扩展机制需要深入理解。理解ESW扩展的关键在于分析溶质-溶剂相互作用和离子缔合，特别是电极-电解质界面处的反应物分布及其溶剂化环境。

Method: 研究进一步发展和分析了最近提出的WiSEs双电层（electrical double layer, EDL）中水合作用和离子缔合的热力学理论。该理论通过体相分子动力学模拟进行参数化，并与EDL模拟结果进行基准测试，获得了良好的定性一致性。

Result: 热力学理论成功解释了ESW的变化机制：一方面通过能斯特方程（Nernst equation）描述体相电解质活度变化直接影响电解质稳定性；另一方面通过巴特勒-沃尔默方程（Butter-Volmer equation）和耦合离子电子转移动力学，分析亥姆霍兹层（Helmholtz layer）中反应物浓度的热力学变化对反应动力学的影响。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解WiSEs中ESW扩展提供了热力学理论框架，强调了双电层中水合作用和离子缔合的关键作用，并通过模拟验证了理论的有效性，为优化电解质设计提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Water-in-Salt-Electrolytes (WiSEs) are a promising class of next-generation electrolytes. Unlike classical dilute electrolytes or more conventional battery electrolytes, WiSEs are characterised by their super-concentrated salt concentration with only a small amount of water, which gives rise to their expanded electrochemical stability window (ESW). The expansion of the ESW is, in part, due to the formation of an inorganic solid electrolyte interphase (SEI) that passivates the anode; this principle is also important in graphite and Li-metal anodes, and beyond Li-ion technologies. The solvation and ionic associations are key descriptors in understanding the expansion of the ESW. Specifically, as reactions which lead to the SEI (or cathode electrolyte interphase, CEI) must occur at the electrode-electrolyte interface, the distribution of reactants and their various solvation environments are critical. This distribution near the interface is referred to as the electrical double layer (EDL), in the absence of reactions. Here we further develop and analyse a recently proposed thermodynamic theory of hydration and ionic associations in the EDL of WiSEs. We parameterize this theory from bulk molecular dynamics simulations and benchmark it against EDL simulations, finding good qualitative agreement. Using this thermodynamic theory, we rationalise changes in the ESW through: changes in the activity in the bulk electrolyte through the Nernst equation, which directly changes the stability of the electrolytes; and thermodynamic changes to the kinetics of these reactions, from the Butler-Volmer equation and coupled ion electron transfer kinetics, through the concentration of reactant species in the Helmholtz layer.

</details>


### [90] [Activity-Driven Dewetting and Rupture in Thin Liquid Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23933)
*Preethi M,Daniya Davis,Bhaskar Sen Gupta*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 活性薄膜去润湿（thin-film dewetting）中，内部活性（internal activity）通过活性应力（active stresses）与基底粘附（substrate adhesion）的竞争，重构了经典的自旋不稳定性（spinodal instability），产生两个独立调控的动力学长度尺度，并将粗化指数（coarsening exponent）从约0.33提升至约0.6。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典薄膜去润湿由粘附介导的自旋不稳定性（adhesion-mediated spinodal instability）主导，其中曲率驱动扩散（curvature-driven diffusion）控制破裂后的粗化过程。本研究旨在探究内部活性如何从根本上重构这一不稳定性机制。

Method: 采用固体基底上活性液体薄膜（active liquid film）的微观模型，分析活性应力（active stresses）与薄膜-基底粘附（film-substrate adhesion）之间的竞争关系。通过生长规律分析（growth law analysis）研究持久自推进（persistent self-propulsion）引入的对流通量（advective flux）与曲率诱导化学势梯度（curvature-induced chemical potential gradients）的竞争。

Result: 活性将输运机制从曲率控制扩散（curvature-controlled diffusion）转变为持久性驱动运动（persistence-driven motion），使粗化指数（coarsening exponent）从约0.33连续增加到约0.6。同时，破裂前沿（rupture front）从耗散性扩展（dissipative spreading）转变为接近弹道标度（ballistic scaling）的强烈加速传播，表明活性并非简单重整化有效表面力，而是产生由持久长度（persistence length）与粘附平衡调控的独特非平衡界面不稳定性（nonequilibrium interfacial instability）。

Conclusion: 研究结果提供了将经典薄膜去润湿与在活性及生物材料中观察到的类去润湿破裂（dewetting-like rupture）联系起来的最小物理机制，揭示了活性如何通过持久长度与粘附的平衡产生独特的非平衡界面不稳定性。

Abstract: Thin-film dewetting is classically governed by an adhesion-mediated spinodal instability in which curvature-driven diffusion controls post-rupture coarsening. We show that internal activity fundamentally restructures this instability. Using a minimal microscopic model of an active liquid film on a solid substrate, we identify a competition between active stresses and film-substrate adhesion that produces two independently regulated dynamical length scales: vertical liquid accumulation and lateral rupture propagation. While passive films exhibit universal diffusion-limited growth, $\ell_z(t)\sim t^{1/3}$, activity converts transport from curvature-controlled diffusion to persistence-driven motion, yielding a continuous increase of the coarsening exponent from $\approx 0.33$ to $\approx 0.6$. The growth law analysis shows that persistent self-propulsion introduces an advective flux that competes with curvature-induced chemical potential gradients, enhancing growth when the persistence length becomes comparable to the evolving domain size. Simultaneously, the rupture front transitions from dissipative spreading to strongly accelerated propagation approaching ballistic scaling. This decoupling shows that activity does not simply renormalize effective surface forces but generates a distinct nonequilibrium interfacial instability governed by the balance between persistence length and adhesion. The results provide a minimal physical mechanism linking classical thin-film dewetting to dewetting-like rupture observed in active and biological materials.

</details>


### [91] [Solubilization kinetics of oils by ionic and nonionic micelles: theoretical model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24052)
*Alexey Kabalnov*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过理论模型分析实验数据，发现非离子表面活性剂对烃类的增溶过程基本无势垒且受扩散控制，而离子表面活性剂的增溶速率慢1-2个数量级，表明存在明显的势垒阻碍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在分析文献中关于增溶动力学（solubilization kinetics）的实验数据，探究不同类型表面活性剂（非离子型与离子型）在烃类增溶过程中的速率差异及其物理机制。

Method: 采用先前提出的理论模型分析实验数据，确定油分子在胶束核心与周围水溶液之间的交换速率。使用菲克扩散模型（Fickean diffusion model）解释增溶趋势，并应用泊松-玻尔兹曼模型（Poisson-Boltzmann model）模拟离子胶束双电层区域的排除效应。

Result: 非离子型乙氧基表面活性剂对烃类分子的增溶基本无势垒（barrier-free），受扩散控制；而离子型表面活性剂的增溶速率慢1-2个数量级，表明烃类进入胶束时存在明显的势垒。泊松-玻尔兹曼模型的预测与实验结果基本吻合。

Conclusion: 离子胶束的双电层区域因低介电常数而排除烃类分子，形成增溶势垒；而非离子基团（如低聚乙氧基）则无此势垒。本文分析仅针对"慢"增溶机制，未涵盖实验中观察到的快速"灾难性"增溶（catastrophic solubilization）。

Abstract: Experimental data on solubilization kinetics found in literature were analyzed by using the model proposed earlier (1). The rates of oil molecular exchange between the micellar core and the surrounding aqueous solution were determined. It was concluded that the solubilization of hydrocarbon molecules by nonionic surfactants of ethylene oxide type is essentially barrier-free, that is, is diffusion controlled. It is quite different for ionic surfactants, where the rate is one-two orders of magnitude slower, indicating the existence of a potential barrier for hydrocarbons to get inside the micelles. A Fickean diffusion model of solubilization has been proposed to explain these trends. For ionic micelles, the hydrocarbons are predicted to be excluded from the micellar double layer region because of their low dielectric constant. The Poisson-Boltzmann model was used to model this effect; the diffusion retardation factors were compared with the experiment and a fair agreement was seen. For nonionic groups, such as oligoethylene oxide, on the other hand, no such barrier was predicted to exist. The analysis of this paper is performed only for the case of the 'slow' solubilization; it does not cover the case of the rapid, 'catastrophic' solubilization observed in the other group of experiments; the distinction between the slow and fast mechanisms is discussed and a possible explanation is suggested.

</details>


### [92] [MesoMem: A mesoscale membrane model based on an additive potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24123)
*Pietro Sillano,Siewert-Jan Marrink,Timon Idema*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的无溶剂单粒子厚度粗粒化脂质双层模型，该模型采用加和势能，通过LAMMPS模拟展示了自组装层状结构和囊泡形成，并成功再现了膜的理论波动谱和可调机械特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在生物膜建模中，连接原子尺度细节与连续介质力学（continuum mechanics）是一个核心挑战，特别是在跨越大长度和时间尺度的介观现象研究中。需要开发能够准确描述膜行为且计算高效的模型。

Method: 本文引入了一种新的无溶剂（solvent-free）、单粒子厚度（one-particle-thick）的粗粒化（coarse-grained）脂质双层模型，采用加和势能（additive potential）。该模型通过独立的倾斜（tilt）和展曲（splay）能量项处理取向弹性，并在LAMMPS分子动力学引擎中实现。

Result: 模拟显示从无序状态自发自组装形成层状结构和稳定囊泡。系统动力学相图揭示了由温度和各项同性吸引陡度控制的凝胶状（gel-like）、流体（fluid）和气态（gas）等不同相区。模型准确再现了无张力膜的理论$1/q^{4}$波动谱，并表现出可调的机械特性，包括生物学相关的弯曲刚度（bending rigidities）和面积压缩模量（area compressibility moduli）。

Conclusion: 该模型能够纳入渗透压（osmotic pressure）和自发曲率（spontaneous curvature），并通过模拟胶体纳米颗粒的粘附包裹（adhesive wrapping）展示了其在复杂膜重塑中的适用性，成功恢复了颗粒尺寸和粘附强度的预测依赖性。

Abstract: Bridging the gap between atomistic detail and continuum mechanics is a central challenge in modeling biological membranes, particularly for mesoscopic phenomena spanning large length and time scales. In this work, we introduce a new, solvent-free, one-particle-thick, coarse-grained model for lipid bilayers, governed by an additive potential. Our approach treats orientational elasticity through distinct additive energy terms for tilt and splay, offering an unbiased potential form. The model is implemented in the LAMMPS molecular dynamics engine. Our simulations show spontaneous self-assembly of lamellar structures and stable vesicles from disordered states. We map the dynamical phase diagram of the system, identifying distinct gel-like, fluid, and gas regimes, controlled by temperature and the steepness of the isotropic attraction. The model accurately reproduces the theoretical $1/q^{4}$ fluctuation spectrum for tensionless membranes and exhibits tunable mechanical properties, including biologically relevant bending rigidities and area compressibility moduli. We show how we can include osmotic pressure and spontaneous curvature in our model. Finally, we demonstrate the model's applicability to complex membrane remodeling by simulating the adhesive wrapping of colloidal nanoparticles, recovering the predicted dependency on particle size and adhesion strength.
