### [93] [Duality of Theoretical Approaches to Understand the Electrical Double Layer in Concentrated Electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24205)
*Zachary A. H. Goodwin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文综述了两种超越平均场理论的方法来理解浓电解质中电双层（EDL）的行为，分析了它们在处理离子-溶剂相关性、静电相互作用和排除体积效应方面的优缺点，并讨论了未来发展方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解浓电解质中电双层（electrical double layer, EDL）的分布对于超级电容器、电池和电催化等技术至关重要。原子尺度方法虽能提供详细信息但计算成本过高，因此需要发展连续介质理论来研究强相关性的浓电解质体系。

Method: 论文分析了两种超越平均场（beyond mean-field）的简化理论方法：一是基于局部密度近似（local-density approximation, LDA）的方法，通过离子聚集和溶剂化处理静电和特异性相互作用；二是超越LDA的方法，更严格地处理静电相关性和排除体积效应（excluded volume effects），但简化了化学相互作用。

Result: LDA方法能提供简单的概念理解，在积分量方面与实验有合理的一致性，但在离子分布和德拜电容（Debye capacitance）方面吻合较差。超越LDA的方法在离子分布、微分电容等方面能获得优异的一致性，但主要适用于简化的硬球体系。

Conclusion: 论文阐述了这两种方法的优缺点及其对理解异常欠屏蔽（anomalous underscreening）现象的贡献，并概述了这些理论方法的未来发展方向，旨在为浓电解质电双层理论的发展提供指导。

Abstract: Understanding the electrical double layer (EDL), i.e, the distribution of electrolyte at an electrified interface, in concentrated electrolytes is important for various technologies, such as supercapacitors, batteries and electrocatalysis. Atomistic approaches offer unprecedented detail, but are too computationally expensive to exhaustively investigate the EDL of concentrated electrolytes, motivating the development of continuum theories. In these concentrated electrolytes, correlations between ions and solvents are strong, through electrostatic and specific interactions, as well as significant excluded volume effects of the complicated molecular species, making the development of theories challenging. Thus far, there are mainly two distinct \textit{simple} theoretical approaches to understand the EDL of concentrated electrolytes, with account of these correlations beyond mean-field. One is a local-density approximation (LDA) based on treating electrostatic and specific interactions beyond mean-field through the ionic aggregation and solvation; where a simple conceptual understanding can be gained and reasonable agreement with experiments in terms of integrated quantities, but poor agreement for ion profiles and Debye capacitance. The other approach is to treat electrostatic correlations and excluded volume effects more rigorously with beyond LDA approaches, but at the cost of simplifying the chemical interactions between species; where excellent agreement can be obtained for ion profiles, differential capacitance, etc., but mainly for the simplified hard-sphere systems that the theories are based on. Here, we describe the merits and downfalls of these two approaches, how they have contributed to understanding anomalous underscreening, and outline future directions for these theoretical approaches.

</details>


### [94] [Active fluctuations induce buckling of living surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24272)
*Matteo Ciarchi,Andriy Goychuk,Erwin Frey*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了活性组织中的张力波动如何通过零均值乘性调制局部表面张力，导致随机屈曲（stochastic buckling）和波长选择现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性组织（active tissues）表现出时空相关的张力波动，这些波动可能影响组织的力学稳定性。研究旨在理解这种活性波动如何通过调制局部表面张力，引发确定性弹性动力学无法解释的不稳定性。

Method: 采用一个最小化的过阻尼表面模型（minimal overdamped surface model），其中活性波动作为零均值乘性调制（zero-mean, multiplicative modulation）作用于局部表面张力。通过基于Novikov-Furutsu定理的非马尔可夫理论（non-Markovian theory）进行分析，并与模拟结果进行对比。

Result: 研究发现，尽管确定性弹性动力学（弹性张力加弯曲）对所有非零波数都能稳定平坦状态，但足够持久的活性波动（sufficiently persistent active fluctuations）会在有限傅里叶模式带（finite band of Fourier modes）中产生正的系综增长率，导致随机屈曲并伴随波长选择（wavelength selection）。

Conclusion: 基于Novikov-Furutsu定理的非马尔可夫理论能够准确捕捉模拟中观察到的失稳阈值（instability threshold）和不稳定带（unstable band），表明活性波动是驱动组织形态发生中随机屈曲现象的关键机制。

Abstract: Active tissues exhibit tension fluctuations that are correlated in space and time. We study a minimal overdamped surface model in which such fluctuations enter as a zero-mean, multiplicative modulation of the local surface tension. Although the deterministic elastic dynamics (tension plus bending) stabilizes the flat state for all nonzero wave numbers, we find that sufficiently persistent active fluctuations generate positive ensemble growth rates for a finite band of Fourier modes, leading to stochastic buckling with wavelength selection. A non-Markovian theory based on the Novikov--Furutsu theorem captures the instability threshold and unstable band observed in simulations.

### [95] [ECH Constraints and Twist Dynamics in the Spatial Isosceles Three-Body Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24025)
*Xijun Hu,Lei Liu,Yuwei Ou,Zhiwen Qiao,Pedro A. S. Salomão*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 该研究利用嵌入接触同调（ECH）分析空间等腰三体问题的动力学约束，证明在临界能量以下，每个紧致能面必须包含无穷多个周期轨道；在临界能量以上，存在无穷多周期轨道和无穷多抛物线轨迹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于应用嵌入接触同调（Embedded Contact Homology, ECH）理论分析空间等腰三体问题的动力学约束，特别是探索能面上周期轨道的存在性与数量问题。

Method: 研究方法包括：将临界能量以下的动力学与紧致三球面上的Reeb流等同；对欧拉轨道（Euler orbit）进行定量估计，包括其横向旋转数的单调性以及作用量与接触体积的严格不等式；结合ECH对具有两个简单周期轨道的紧致三球面上Reeb流的分类。

Result: 主要结果包括：在临界能量以下，排除了双轨道情形，迫使每个紧致能面必须包含无穷多个周期轨道；在临界能量以上，证明了存在无穷多个周期轨道和无穷多个抛物线轨迹（parabolic trajectories）。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，嵌入接触同调为三体问题提供了强有力的动力学约束工具，通过欧拉轨道界定的盘状全局截面（disk-like global surfaces of section）和由旋转数与接触体积定义的非平凡扭转区间（twist interval），系统地编码了周期轨道的相对缠绕信息。

Abstract: We study dynamical constraints arising from Embedded Contact Homology (ECH) in the spatial isosceles three-body problem. For energies below the critical level, the dynamics on the energy surface is identified with a Reeb flow on the tight three-sphere. We obtain quantitative estimates for the Euler orbit, including monotonicity of its transverse rotation number and a strict inequality comparing its action with the contact volume. Combined with the ECH classification of Reeb flows on the tight three-sphere with two simple periodic orbits, these estimates rule out the two-orbit scenario, thus forcing every compact energy surface below the critical level to have infinitely many periodic orbits. The result admits a dynamical interpretation via disk-like global surfaces of section bounded by the Euler orbit. In this setting, the rotation number and the contact volume define a non-trivial twist interval which encodes the relative winding of periodic orbits. For energies above the critical level, where the energy surface is non-compact, we prove the existence of infinitely many periodic orbits and infinitely many parabolic trajectories via twist estimates near infinity.

### [96] [Symmetry-breaking bifurcation of coupled topological edge states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23710)
*Rujiang Li,Letian Xu,Muhammad Imran,Wencai Wang,Yongtao Jia,Ying Liu*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该论文提出利用耦合拓扑边缘态（CTESs）的对称性破缺分岔作为在非线性拓扑晶格中实现自发对称破缺（SSB）的普适机制，并以双SSH链光学谐振腔阵列为例进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为非线性拓扑晶格中的自发对称破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking, SSB）提供一种普适机制。当前研究需要一种通用的原理来实现拓扑系统中的对称性破缺现象。

Method: 采用由两个Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）链组成的光学谐振腔阵列作为研究模型。通过分析耦合拓扑边缘态（coupled topological edge states, CTESs）在非线性强度增加时的行为变化，研究其对称性破缺分岔过程。

Result: 研究发现随着非线性强度增加，对称的CTESs经历超临界分岔（supercritical bifurcation）。超过临界阈值后，原本稳定的对称态变得不稳定，形成一对稳定的非对称态。对称CTESs两侧均显示子晶格极化（sublattice polarization），而非对称CTESs中占据主导的一侧表现出更强的子晶格极化。

Conclusion: 该工作为在非线性拓扑晶格中实现自发对称破缺提供了一种普适机制。研究发现链间耦合（interchain coupling）增强时，稳定CTESs的频率范围扩大，而稳定非对称CTESs的频率范围减小。

Abstract: We propose that the symmetry-breaking bifurcation of coupled topological edge states (CTESs) can be used as a general principle for achieving spontaneous symmetry breaking (SSB) in a nonlinear topological lattice. Using an optical resonator array composed of two Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) chains as an example, we find that as the nonlinearity strength increases, the symmetric CTESs undergo a supercritical bifurcation. Beyond the critical threshold, the originally stable symmetric state becomes unstable, leading to the formation of a pair of stable asymmetric states. Both sides of the symmetric CTESs exhibit sublattice polarization, while the side of the asymmetric CTESs that is predominantly occupied demonstrates stronger sublattice polarization. We further find that as interchain coupling increases, the frequency range for stable CTESs expands, while the frequency range for stable asymmetric CTESs decreases. Our work provides a universal mechanism for realizing SSB in nonlinear topological lattices.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用共振选择性晶格激发机制，将强太赫兹（THz）脉冲调谐至与红外活性声子模式共振，通过瞬态晶格形变调控体相β-硼酸钡（beta-BaB2O4）中的二次谐波产生（SHG）。

Conclusion: 共振选择性晶格激发机制为调控材料非线性光学响应提供了新型太赫兹控制方案，克服了传统方法的局限性，具有重要应用前景。

Abstract: Dynamical control of the nonlinear optical properties of solids -- with light itself -- will be essential for future ultrafast photonic technologies. Previously, methods to modulate nonlinear processes including second-harmonic generation (SHG) have relied primarily on non-resonant light-matter interaction or photo-generation of hot electrons in nanoscale materials. However, these approaches are typically constrained by limited interaction lengths and the initial frequency conversion is relatively weak under equilibrium conditions. Here, an approximately 30\% modulation of efficient phase-matched SHG in bulk beta-barium borate (beta-BaB2O4) is achieved through transient lattice deformation by intense terahertz (THz) pulses that are tuned to resonance with an infrared-active phonon mode. The effect originates from modification of the index of refraction ellipsiod and the corresponding nonlinear phase-matching conditions, rather than from direct modulation of the nonlinear susceptibility through THz-mediated chi^(3) processes. This mechanism, of resonant selective lattice excitation, points toward novel THz-control schemes to tune the nonlinear optical response in materials.

### [99] [Composite based magnetoelectric scaled devices with large output voltages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23562)
*Emma Van Meirvenne,Aude Brinkmann-Hornbogen,Bart Soree,Christoph Adelmann,Florin Ciubotaru*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过有限元方法分析纳米尺度磁电复合器件中由磁化旋转引起的差分电压生成，揭示了尺寸和材料参数对器件性能的影响机制，展示了在微缩器件中实现超过200 mV输出电压的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究纳米尺度磁电（magnetoelectric, ME）复合器件中，由磁化从基态旋转到面外（out-of-plane, OOP）构型时直接磁电效应产生的差分电压生成机制。研究关注设计微缩磁电柱时如何通过尺寸和材料选择来产生大输出电压。

Method: 采用在COMSOL Multiphysics中开发的有限元方法（finite element method, FEM）模型，对磁致伸缩铁磁层和压电层通过应变机械耦合的复合器件进行综合分析。系统性地研究了尺寸和材料参数对器件性能的影响。

Result: 研究发现在微缩尺寸下存在两种不同的应变传递机制，器件纵横比和磁状态共同决定影响压电层应变传递的主导机制。表面夹持效应随柱面积减小而减弱，使用更硬的电极或夹持层可增强应变传递。具有大磁弹性耦合常数或大泊松比的磁致伸缩材料可显著提高小尺寸下的输出电压。

Conclusion: 该研究为设计微缩磁电柱时的尺寸和材料选择提供了重要见解，展示了在微缩器件中实现超过200 mV输出电压的可行性，凸显了这些结构在微电子应用中的集成潜力。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the differential voltage generation arising from the direct magnetoelectric (ME) effect in nanoscale composite devices upon magnetization rotation from the magnetic ground state to an out-of-plane (OOP) configuration. These composite devices comprise a magnetostrictive ferromagnetic layer and a piezoelectric layer, mechanically coupled through strain. Using a finite element method (FEM) model, developed in COMSOL Multiphysics, we provide a comprehensive analysis of strain transfer mechanisms and resulting voltage generations. Here, the influence of dimensional and material parameters on the device performance is systematically examined. Our results indicate the presence of two distinct strain transfer mechanisms at scaled dimensions, where the device aspect ratio and the magnetic state both determine the dominant mechanism influencing the strain transfer to the piezoelectric layer. Moreover, we observed that the influence of surface clamping diminished as the pillar area was reduced. We also saw that the strain transfer to the piezoelectric layer can be enhanced by using stiffer electrodes or clamping layers. Lastly, we concluded that magnetostrictive materials with large magnetoelastic coupling constants or large Poisson ratios may strongly increase the output voltage at small dimensions. This study provides insight in the dimension and material selection when designing scaled ME pillars, with the aim of generating large output voltages. We showed that output voltages exceeding 200 mV can be achieved in scaled devices, underscoring the potential of these structures for integration into microelectronic applications.

</details>


### [100] [Hierarchical symmetry breaking in Moiré graphene domain-wall networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23570)
*Xue Yan,Kaiyun Chen,Yuan Yan,Fan Feng,Minglei Sun,Christan Brandl,Jefferson Zhe Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了石墨烯双层莫尔（moiré）系统中存在两种对称性破缺：堆垛对称性破缺产生拓扑保护的一维态，而网络几何对称性破缺则自发形成手性网络构型。通过应变和层间柔性的相图分析，发现了三种平衡网络形态，其边界态局域化依赖于网络对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔网络形成破坏了石墨烯双层的堆垛对称性，产生承载拓扑保护一维态的畴壁。然而，仅靠拓扑无法完全确定这些系统的构型，需要研究网络几何层面的额外对称性破缺机制。

Method: 采用原子结构弛豫和电子结构计算，通过晶格弛豫研究TDW网络的手性几何形成。开发了基于应变和层间柔性的综合相图，识别平衡网络形态。使用紧束缚计算分析不同网络构型的电子态分布。

Result: 发现了三种平衡网络形态：直线型、单-手性和双-手性网络。手性网络源于莫尔几何约束下TDW能量的全局最小化。直线网络承载结中心态，而手性网络将谱权重转移到不对称边缘模式。边界态的局域化依赖于网络对称性。

Conclusion: 堆垛和网络层面的双重对称性破缺为理解和控制莫尔双层中的低能电子态提供了新途径。网络对称性决定了拓扑保护边界态的局域化特性，这为调控莫尔材料的电子性质开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Moiré network formation in graphene bilayers breaks stacking symmetry, giving rise to domain walls that host topologically protected one-dimensional states. Here we show that these systems undergo an additional symmetry breaking at the level of the domain-wall network geometry, leading to the spontaneous emergence of chiral network configurations that are not determined by topology alone. Using atomistic structural relaxation and electronic-structure calculations, we show that TDW networks adopt chiral geometries through lattice relaxation. Via developing a comprehensive phase diagram defined by strain and interlayer flexibility, we discover three equilibrium network morphologies: straight, mono-chiral, and dual-chiral. Chiral networks arise from the global minimization of TDW energy under moiré geometric constraints. Tight-binding calculations show that straight networks host junction-centred states, whereas chiral networks shift spectral weight toward asymmetric edge modes. While topologically protected states naturally emerge at AB/BA domain boundaries in moiré bilayers, we demonstrated that the localization of boundary states is network-symmetry dependent. Our results show that symmetry breaking at both the stacking and network levels provides a new way to understand and control low-energy electronic states in moiré bilayers.

</details>


### [101] [Double-Carrier Fitting of Hall Resistance Assisted by Gate-Induced Shubnikov-de Haas Oscillations in Possible Excitonic Insulator Ta2Pd3Te5](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23608)
*Xing-Chen Guo,An-Qi Wang,Xiu-Tong Deng,Yu-Peng Li,Guo-An Li,Zhi-Yuan Zhang,Xiao-Fan Shi,Xiao Deng,Zi-Wei Dou,Guang-Tong Liu,Fan-Ming Qu,Jie Shen,Li Lu,Zhi-Jun Wang,You-Guo Shi,Hang Li,Tian Qian*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究在Ta2Pd3Te5材料上构建了双载流子平台，通过分析霍尔电阻曲线形状和门电压诱导的Shubnikov-de Haas振荡，将双载流子模型的四参数拟合简化为单参数拟合，为霍尔电阻的双载流子拟合提供了可靠方法，并为Ta2Pd3Te5中激子绝缘体态的存在提供了新证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 霍尔效应（Hall effect）是材料在磁场作用下的重要现象，通过霍尔电阻随磁场变化的曲线可以提取载流子浓度等关键信息。然而，当曲线呈现非线性时需要使用双载流子模型（double-carrier model）进行拟合，该模型包含四个未知参数（两种载流子的浓度和迁移率），导致拟合通常不唯一，显著降低了可靠性和准确性。

Method: 在可能的激子绝缘体（excitonic insulator）Ta2Pd3Te5上构建双载流子平台，通过分析霍尔电阻曲线的形状特征，并结合门电压诱导的Shubnikov-de Haas振荡（gate-induced Shubnikov-de Haas oscillations）方法，将四参数拟合问题简化为单参数拟合。

Result: 成功实现了双载流子模型的简化拟合，将原本需要确定四个未知参数的复杂问题转化为仅需单一参数的拟合过程。该方法显著提高了霍尔电阻双载流子拟合的可靠性和准确性。

Conclusion: 该研究为霍尔电阻的双载流子拟合提供了一种可靠方法，同时为Ta2Pd3Te5材料中激子绝缘体态的存在提供了新的实验证据，解决了传统双载流子模型拟合中参数不唯一的问题。

Abstract: Hall effect is an important phenomenon when a magnetic field is applied to materials. From the curve depicting the Hall resistance versus the magnetic field, crucial information such as carrier concentration can be extracted. If the curve exhibits a linear dependence up to rather high magnetic fields, it indicates that charge transport involves only a single type of carrier, and if a non-linear curve is measured, then the double-carrier model should be considered for fitting. However, this model involves four unknown parameters, including the concentration and mobility of the two carriers, resulting in that such fitting is usually non-unique, which significantly reduces the reliability and accuracy. In this work, a double-carrier platform was constructed on a probable excitonic insulator Ta2Pd3Te5, and the four-parameter fitting based on the double-carrier model was simplified to a single-parameter fitting by employing methods such as analyzing the shape of the Hall resistance curve and generating gate-induced Shubnikov-de Haas oscillations. Thus, we provide a reliable method for double-carrier fitting of Hall resistance and a new evidence for the existence of excitonic-insulator state in Ta2Pd3Te5.

Abstract: The low-temperature metallic phase of 1T-TaS2 may originate from current- and voltage-driven destabilization of the commensurate charge density wave (CDW) in a strongly correlated Mott insulator, alongside the robust yet rarely realized influence of intrinsic electronic distortions. Electrical pulse-driven transport, combined with second harmonic response, reveals abrupt switching, negative differential resistance (NDR), and multiscale domain-wall reorganization. ### [106] [The temporal picture for Bloch electron dynamics in homogeneous electric fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23965)
*G. J. Iafrate,V. N. Sokolov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了在任意时间依赖性均匀电场中加速的布洛赫电子的瞬态图像，分析了从注入瞬间到多个布洛赫周期的完整时间演化过程，揭示了电子从真实质量到有效质量动态转变的惯性变化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解布洛赫电子在任意时间依赖性均匀电场中的瞬态行为，特别是从电子注入瞬间到经历多个布洛赫周期的完整时间演化过程。这有助于揭示电子在超强电场作用下从真实质量到有效质量动态转变的物理机制。

Method: 研究方法基于薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）的性质，采用矢量势规范（vector potential gauge）描述电场，并以布洛赫电场的瞬时本征态作为基态来描述电场中的布洛赫动力学。针对不同时间序列，建立并比较薛定谔方程的解。

Result: 研究获得了恒定电场一阶近似下的动量期望值，推导出的速度是文献中讨论的类Zitterbewegung行为的场依赖性推广。动量期望值及其时间导数的早期和长期极限表明，电子在电场作用下加速通过能带时，对布洛赫加速的阻力从真实质量动态转变为有效质量动态。

Conclusion: 结论表明，电子从早期注入的自由质量电子转变为有效质量电子的惯性变化，源于真实质量电子"穿戴"（dressing-up）到晶体态中。这种时间依赖性"穿戴"行为对于理解布洛赫电子在超强电场中的一般动力学具有重要意义。

Abstract: The transient picture for a Bloch electron accelerating in an arbitrarily time-dependent homogeneous electric field is developed. The temporal sequence for the analysis includes the instant after electron injection, followed by the time required for a small change in electron wavenumber away from initial injection, leading to the final time evolution over many Bloch periods. The time-dependent behavior is studied using the properties of the Schrödinger equation. The electric field is described through the vector potential gauge, and the instantaneous eigenstates of the Bloch, electric-field-dependent Hamiltonian are used as basis states in describing the Bloch dynamics in the electric field. For each temporal sequence considered, the solution to the Schrödinger equation is established and comparatively discussed. The expectation value of the momentum is obtained for the special case of first order in a constant electric field; the resulting velocity derived is a field-dependent generalization of the natural Zitterbewegung-like behavior discussed in the recent literature. The early-time and long-time limits of the momentum expectation value and its time derivative demonstrate that the resistance to Bloch acceleration after initial band injection varies from real mass to effective mass dynamics as the electron accelerates through the band under the influence of electric field. This changing inertia from early injection of a free-mass electron is the result of the {\it real mass} electron {\it dressing-up} into the states of the crystal to become {\it an effective mass} electron. The ramifications of this temporal {\it dressing} behavior are discussed in considering the general dynamics of Bloch electrons subject to ultrastrong electric fields.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子干涉仪被认为是构建电子飞行量子比特（electronic flying qubits）的潜在候选方案。该方案需要超快电压脉冲，其持续时间短于器件中的飞行时间。理解这种短激发下的物理过程需要对电子-电子相互作用进行恰当处理。

Method: 本研究通过时间分辨模拟（time-resolved simulations）分析马赫-曾德尔干涉仪（Mach-Zehnder interferometer），在时间依赖平均场水平（time-dependent mean-field level）处理相互作用。

Result: 研究发现相互作用的主要效应是脉冲速度的重整化（renormalization of the pulse velocity）。至关重要的是，干涉效应在相互作用存在下表现出稳健性（robustness）。

Conclusion: 电子-电子相互作用主要影响脉冲传播速度而非破坏干涉特性，这为基于电子干涉仪的量子比特实现提供了重要物理基础，表明相互作用不会显著损害量子干涉效应。

Abstract: Electronic interferometers have been identified as possible candidates for building electronic flying qubits. Such a regime requires ultrafast voltage pulses whose duration is shorter than the time of flight through the device. Understanding the corresponding physics in the presence of such short excitations requires a proper treatment of electron-electron interactions. In this article, we take a step in this direction by performing time-resolved simulations of a Mach-Zehnder interferometer treating the interactions at the time-dependent mean-field level. We find that the main effect of the interaction is the renormalization of the pulse velocity. Very importantly, the interference effects appear to be robust to the presence of interactions.

</details>


### [108] [Nanoelectronics with Two Dimensional Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24046)
*Bing Zhao,Roselle Ngaloy,Lalit Pandey,Himanshu Bangar,Divya P. Dubey,Saroj P. Dash*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

Motivation: 二维磁体为自旋基纳米电子学提供了有前景的平台，能够在原子尺度上控制磁序、界面、量子几何和对称性。文章旨在总结该领域的最新进展，展示二维磁体如何实现可调谐、高效能的集成自旋电子技术。

Method: 文章采用综述分析方法，重点讨论了二维铁磁体、反铁磁体、交变磁体及相关磁性相的最新进展。分析了基于二维异质结构的垂直磁隧道结和横向自旋阀中的自旋相关输运，以及二维磁性异质结构中无外场高效自旋轨道矩磁化翻转机制。

Result: 研究表明，增强的居里温度、垂直磁各向异性和非常规磁序能够转化为器件相关的功能。原子级尖锐界面实现了高度可调的自旋注入、传播和检测，而非常规自旋电流源于相邻低对称性自旋轨道层。文章还讨论了涉及对称性破缺、贝里曲率和轨道角动量输运的微观机制。

Conclusion: 二维磁体有望成为可调谐、高效能集成自旋电子技术的有力候选者，能够在纳米尺度上利用交织的自旋、电荷、轨道和拓扑自由度。文章还概述了针对神经形态计算、混合量子自旋电子学和多功能架构的材料与器件设计策略。

Abstract: Two dimensional (2D) magnets have emerged as a compelling platform for spin based nanoelectronics, enabling atomic scale control of magnetic order, interfaces, quantum geometry, and symmetry. Here, we highlight recent advances in 2D ferromagnets, antiferromagnets, altermagnets, and related magnetic phases, emphasizing how enhanced Curie temperatures, perpendicular magnetic anisotropy, and unconventional magnetic orders translate into device relevant functionality. Spin dependent transport in vertical magnetic tunnel junctions and lateral spin valves based on 2D heterostructures are discussed, where atomically sharp interfaces enable highly tunable spin injection, propagation, and detection. We further focused on field free energy efficient spin orbit torque magnetization switching in 2D magnetic heterostructures, in which unconventional spin currents originate from an adjacent low symmetry spin orbit layer. Microscopic mechanisms involving symmetry breaking, Berry curvature, and orbital angular momentum transport are discussed, along with key challenges, including switching determinism and torque efficiency. Materials and device design strategies targeting neuromorphic, hybrid quantum spintronic, and multifunctional architectures are outlined. Collectively, these developments position 2D magnets as a promising candidate for tunable, energy efficient integrated spintronic technologies that can harness intertwined spin, charge, orbital, and topological degrees of freedom at the nanoscale.

### [109] [Integrated nanophotonic platform for on-chip quantum emitter interactions and entanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24090)
*Yinhui Kan,Shailesh Kumar,Xujing Liu,Antonio I. Fernández-Domínguez,Sergey I. Bozhevolnyi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种前向设计平台，利用工程化表面等离子体激元干涉实现固态量子发射器间的长程相互作用增强与抑制，为片上纠缠工程提供了紧凑可扩展的框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态量子发射器（quantum emitters）间的纠缠是光子量子技术的关键资源，但实现这种纠缠需要强且可控的长程相互作用。目前工程化这种耦合仍然具有挑战性，特别是对于片上远距离固态量子发射器。

Method: 引入前向设计（forward-designed）平台，通过工程化表面等离子体激元（surface plasmon polariton）干涉实现超紧凑纳米光子架构，以介导增强的长程量子发射器-量子发射器相互作用。具体实现了两种配置：用于能量汇聚的相位共轭椭圆设计，以及用于抑制能量转移的共辐射双曲设计。

Result: 实验证明了与裸基底相比，能量转移速率的大幅增强和抑制。预测了空间分离量子发射器间的瞬态纠缠，并发度（concurrence）峰值达到0.493，接近瞬态区域的理论界限。扩展到多量子发射器情况，观察到增强的能量汇聚，并预测了三量子发射器配置中的纠缠。

Conclusion: 这些结果为集成量子纳米光子系统中的片上纠缠工程建立了一个紧凑且可扩展的框架，为实现固态量子发射器间的可控长程相互作用提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Entanglement between solid-state quantum emitters (QEs) is a key resource for photonic quantum technologies. Achieving such entanglement requires strong and controllable long-range interactions between QEs. However, engineering such coupling remains challenging, particularly for on-chip distant solid-state QEs. Here, we introduce a forward-designed platform that enables ultracompact nanophotonic architectures to mediate enhanced long-range QE-QE interactions via engineered surface plasmon polariton interference. Using this strategy, we realize two distinct configurations: a phase-conjugated elliptic design for energy funneling, and a co-radiating hyperbolic design for its suppression. We experimentally demonstrate large enhancement and suppression of energy transfer rates compared to bare substrates. Furthermore, we predict transient entanglement between spatially separated QEs with concurrence peaking at 0.493, approaching the theoretical bound in the transient regime. Extending to the multi-QE case, we observe enhanced energy funneling and predict QE-QE entanglement in three-QE configurations. These results establish a compact and scalable framework for on-chip entanglement engineering in integrated quantum nanophotonic systems.

### [110] [Microwave response of fractional quantum Hall droplets with quasiparticle tunneling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24116)

TL;DR: 该研究理论分析了量子点接触中准粒子隧穿对分数量子霍尔液滴微波吸收光谱的影响，开发了非微扰路径积分蒙特卡洛方法，发现隧穿导致共振峰的可测量位移和展宽，为介观量子霍尔结构中准粒子动力学提供了定量探测手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过无接触的微波吸收光谱探测分数量子霍尔液滴的集体边缘动力学，超越传统输运测量的局限，探索准粒子隧穿对集体激发的影响。

Method: 开发了非微扰路径积分蒙特卡洛方法（nonperturbative path-integral Monte Carlo approach），能够在有限温度和任意液滴几何形状下计算频率依赖响应，并在弱隧穿区域与解析结果进行基准测试。

Result: 隧穿导致共振峰产生可测量的位移和展宽，这些效应系统地依赖于隧穿强度和器件几何形状，在直接对响应函数进行微扰处理时无法获得，只有在正确纳入相互作用核效应时才显现。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明微波光谱学可作为介观量子霍尔结构中准粒子动力学的定量探测手段，揭示了边缘模式干涉和隧穿诱导的集体激发重整化的实验可观测特征。

Abstract: We theoretically study microwave absorption spectroscopy of fractional quantum Hall droplets in the presence of quasiparticle tunneling across a quantum point contact. This contact-free probe provides access to collective edge dynamics beyond conventional transport measurements. We develop a nonperturbative path-integral Monte Carlo approach that enables computation of the frequency-dependent response at finite temperature and for arbitrary droplet geometries, and benchmark the method against analytical results in the weak-tunneling regime. We find that tunneling produces measurable shifts and broadening of resonance peaks, with systematic dependence on tunneling strength and device geometry. Such shifts and broadenings are not obtained in perturbative treatments acting directly on the response function, but emerge when interaction-kernel effects are properly incorporated. Our results indicate experimentally accessible signatures of edge-mode interference and tunneling-induced renormalization of collective excitations, and support the use of microwave spectroscopy as a quantitative probe of quasiparticle dynamics in mesoscopic quantum Hall structures.

### [111] [Thermal Casimir Force Imaging of Nonequilibrium Hot Electrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24157)
*Weikang Lu,Ziyi Xu,Hewan Zhang,Svend Age Biehs,Achim Kittel,Ludi Qin,Xue Gong,Huanyi Xue,Yanru Song,Zhengyang Zhong,Shiyou Chen,Kun Ding,Wei Lu,Zhenghua An*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究首次基于热卡西米尔效应（thermal Casimir effect）实现了非接触式热电子力测量，通过双共振原子力显微镜探针在5纳米间距下检测到约3巴的热卡西米尔压力，为纳米尺度热电子检测提供了新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热卡西米尔效应源于热激发电荷的电磁场涨落，能够产生热敏感力，为检测现代微型晶体管中普遍存在但难以探测的纳米尺度热电子（hot electrons）提供了新途径。然而，由于静电力和量子卡西米尔力等背景力的干扰，在纳米尺度检测热卡西米尔力仍极具挑战性。

Method: 研究采用配备双共振探针（dual-resonant tip）的原子力显微镜（AFM），实现了对非平衡热电子的热敏感力检测。该方法能有效抑制背景热不敏感力，从而将热电子与冷电子（cold electrons）区分开来。

Result: 在硅纳米收缩器件（silicon nanoconstriction devices）中，当电子温度约为10^3 K、间距为5纳米时，测得的热卡西米尔压力达到约3巴（bar）。该测量首次基于热卡西米尔效应实现了热电子的非接触力测量。

Conclusion: 该工作为热电子纳米测温学（hot electron nanothermometry）引入了新方法学，并为后摩尔纳米电子学（post-Moore nanoelectronics）的热机械特性提供了关键见解。

Abstract: The thermal Casimir effect, arising from fluctuating electromagnetic fields of thermally agitated charges, induces thermosensitive forces and presents a novel approach to detecting nanoscale hot electrons, elusive yet ubiquitous in modern miniaturized transistors. However, detecting thermal Casimir forces at the nanoscale remains extremely challenging due to background forces such as electrostatic force and quantum Casimir force. In this study, we present the first non-contact force measurement of hot electrons based on the thermal Casimir effect. Using an atomic force microscope (AFM) with a dual-resonant tip, we achieve thermosensitive force detection of nonequilibrium hot electrons while effectively suppressing background thermo-insensitive forces, thereby distinguishing them from cold electrons. In silicon nanoconstriction devices, the measured thermal Casimir pressure reaches approximately 3 bar at a separation of 5 nm at an electron temperature of about 10^3 K. Our work introduces a novel methodology for hot electron nanothermometry and provides critical insights into the thermo-mechanical properties of post-Moore nanoelectronics.

</details>


### [112] [Tuning the memristive response of TaO$_x$-based devices with Ag Nanoparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24168)
*R. Leal Martir,A. J. T. van der Ree,M. H. Aguirre,G. Palasantzas,D. Rubi,M. J. Sánchez*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过在Pt/Ta2O5/TaO2/Pt忆阻器顶部电极中嵌入银纳米颗粒（AgNPs），实现了对电阻开关行为的调控，选择性抑制了双回滞开关环中的一个，显著提高了高阻态的循环稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺陷工程是调控氧化物基忆阻器件中电阻开关（resistive switching, RS）的关键策略，其中氧空位（oxygen vacancy, OV）动力学控制着导电细丝的形成与断裂。本研究旨在探索银纳米颗粒嵌入对多界面忆阻器开关行为的影响。

Method: 研究采用Pt/Ta2O5/TaO2/Pt忆阻器结构，在顶部电极中嵌入银纳米颗粒（AgNPs），分析其电阻开关行为和统计稳定性。通过氧空位电阻网络（Oxygen Vacancy Resistive Network, OVRN）模型进行数值模拟，复现实验观察到的开关环和统计趋势。

Result: 无AgNPs的器件表现出两个手性相反的磁滞开关环（hysteresis switching loops, HSLs），分别源于Pt/Ta2O5顶部界面和Ta2O5/TaO2底部界面的参与。嵌入AgNPs降低了整体器件电阻，选择性抑制了一个开关环，产生单一明确的开关模式。AgNPs器件的高阻态循环间变异性显著降低，Weibull分析证实了改善的耐久性和开关重现性。

Conclusion: 在细丝型电阻开关框架下，AgNPs通过局部金属化顶部界面，部分抑制氧空位传输，将开关动力学限制在底部界面。通过金属纳米颗粒进行靶向界面金属化，为控制多界面电阻开关动力学和改善开关稳定性提供了有效途径，无需修改氧化物结构。

Abstract: Defect engineering is a key strategy to control resistive switching (RS) in oxide-based memristive devices, where oxygen vacancy (OV) dynamics governs filament formation and rupture. We investigate the effect of Ag nanoparticles (AgNPs) embedded in the top electrode of Pt/Ta2O5/TaO2/Pt memristors and analyze their RS behavior and statistical stability. Devices without AgNPs exhibit two hysteresis switching loops (HSLs) with opposite chiralities, originating from the participation of the Pt/Ta2O5 top interface and the Ta2O5/TaO2 bottom interface. Incorporating AgNPs reduces the overall device resistance and selectively suppresses one loop, yielding a single, well-defined switching mode. Moreover, devices incorporating Ag-NPs show markedly reduced cycle-to-cycle variability of the high-resistance state, as confirmed by Weibull analysis, indicating improved endurance and switching reproducibility. Within a filamentary RS framework, we attribute this behavior to local metallization of the top interface by AgNPs, which partially inhibit OV transport and confines the RS dynamics to the bottom interface. Numerical simulations with the Oxygen Vacancy Resistive Network (OVRN) model succesfully reproduce the experimental HSLs, statistical trends, and tunable ON/OFF ratios with AgNPs coverage. These findings demonstrate that targeted interface metallization via metallic nanoparticles provides an effective route to control multi-interface RS dynamics and improve switching stability in without modifying the oxide architecture.

### [113] [A Unified Origin of Primordial Black Hole Dark Matter and Nanohertz Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24061)
*Guillem Domènech,Shi Pi,Ao Wang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文提出一个统一框架，将Subaru-HSC观测到的超短时标微引力透镜事件与脉冲星计时阵列探测到的纳赫兹随机引力波背景联系起来，认为它们都源自振幅约10⁻²的平坦曲率功率谱增强，从而支持行星质量原初黑洞构成全部暗物质的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期Subaru-HSC的高频观测发现了一批超短时标（ultrashort-timescale）微引力透镜事件，为行星质量原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）构成全部暗物质提供了有力证据。同时，脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing arrays, PTAs）报告了纳赫兹随机引力波背景，需要统一解释这两个观测现象。

Method: 作者提出一个统一框架，假设存在一个宽泛、近乎平坦的曲率功率谱（curvature power spectrum）增强，其振幅约为O(10⁻²)。这种原初起源能够同时产生行星质量到太阳质量范围的原初黑洞质量函数（PBH mass function）。

Result: 该模型产生的原初黑洞质量函数覆盖行星质量到太阳质量范围，且与当前所有观测约束保持一致。这一统一框架将微引力透镜事件与随机引力波背景自然联系起来，为原初黑洞构成暗物质提供了自洽解释。

Conclusion: 这一统一原初黑洞-诱导引力波框架提出了具体的多信使（multi-messenger）预测，可通过未来的微引力透镜巡天、下一代脉冲星计时阵列、空间干涉仪、精密天体测量和激光测距实验进行决定性检验。

Abstract: Recent high-cadence observations by Subaru-HSC have identified a population of ultrashort-timescale microlensing events, providing a compelling window for planet-mass primordial black holes (PBHs) to constitute the entirety of dark matter. In this Letter, we demonstrate that this PBH population and the nanohertz stochastic gravitational-wave (GW) background reported by pulsar timing arrays (PTAs) can be naturally unified by a single primordial origin: a broad, nearly-flat enhancement of the curvature power spectrum with an amplitude of $O(10^{-2})$. The resulting PBH mass function spans the planet-to-solar mass range, while remaining consistent with all current observational constraints. This unified PBH--induced-GW framework makes concrete multi-messenger predictions, which can be decisively scrutinized by forthcoming microlensing surveys, next-generation PTAs, space-borne interferometers, precision astrometry, and laser ranging experiments.

### [115] [Controlled release from polyurethane films: drug release mechanisms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23386)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在分析聚氨酯薄膜负载双氯芬酸（diclofenac）的药物释放动力学和机制，通过模拟不同生理条件（静态与动态）来评估药物释放行为。

Method: 研究在静态和动态条件下进行实验，初始载药量分别为10%、20%和30%。动态条件模拟生物流动，流速设定为7.5 ml/s（正常状态）和23.5 ml/s（运动状态）。实验数据采用Higuchi、Korsmeyer-Peppas、一级动力学、零级动力学和Peppas-Sahlin模型进行分析。

Result: 实验结果显示，增加流速和初始载药量会增强药物释放。静态条件下释放速率更受药物剂量影响。分析表明扩散、突释和渗透压是主要释放机制，菲克型扩散（Fickian type）在整个释放过程中占主导地位。Peppas-Sahlin模型显示扩散机制贡献随流速和初始剂量增加而减少。

Conclusion: 药物释放动力学在静态条件下比动态条件下更受药物剂量影响。不同药物剂量测试表明，药物释放曲线的阶段数与流速和药物百分比无关，扩散机制在整个释放过程中保持主导地位。

Abstract: In this study, polyurethane-films loaded diclofenac were used to analyze the drug release kinetics and mechanisms. For this purpose, the experimental procedures were developed under static and dynamic conditions with different initial drug loads of 10, 20, and 30%. In the dynamic condition, to better simulate the biological flow, drug release measurements were investigated at flow rates of 7.5 and 23.5 ml/s. These values indicate the flow rate of the internal carotid artery (ICA) for a normal state of a body and for a person during the exercise, respectively. The experimental data were analyzed and adjusted by Higuchi, Korsmeyer-Peppas, First-order, zero-order, and Peppas-Sahlin models in order to understand the mechanisms contributed. Finally, Drug release mechanisms were specified by investigating the model correlation coefficients. Experimental results showed that increasing the flow rate and initial drug loads enhance drug liberation. In addition, the rate of release is more influenced by the drug dosage in the static state. The analysis revealed that diffusion, burst, and osmotic pressure are the principal mechanisms contributed. Moreover, Fickian type was the dominant mechanism at all duration of release. However, it was discovered using Peppas-Sahlin model that the contribution of the diffusion mechanism decreases with increasing flow rate and initial dosage. Furthermore, the tests at different drug dosages showed that the number of stages in medication release profile is independent of the flow rate and the medicine percentage. One can conclude that the drug release kinetic in static state is more influenced by drug dosage compare to dynamic state.

</details>

### [116] [Photoluminescence Line Shapes of Nanocrystals: Contributions from First- and Second-Order Vibronic Couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23604)
*Kaiyue Peng,Bokang Hou,Kailai Lin,Caroline Chen,Hendrik Utzat,Eran Rabani*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于计算单个半导体纳米晶体光致发光光谱的微观、无参数方法，该方法直接从半经验赝势框架推导激子-声子耦合，并系统纳入对角和非对角相互作用，成功应用于CdSe/CdS核壳纳米晶体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要开发一种微观、无参数的方法来准确计算单个半导体纳米晶体（semiconductor nanocrystals）的光致发光光谱（photoluminescence spectra），以深入理解激子-声子耦合（exciton-phonon coupling）对光谱特性的影响。

Method: 方法基于半经验赝势（semi-empirical pseudopotential）框架直接推导激子-声子耦合，系统纳入对角（diagonal）和非对角（off-diagonal）相互作用，并扩展至声子模式的二阶项；采用久保-丰泽（Kubo-Toyozawa）形式中的戴森展开（Dyson expansion）计算偶极-偶极相关函数（dipole-dipole correlation function）。

Result: 应用于CdSe/CdS核壳纳米晶体（core-shell nanocrystals）时，该方法在宽温度范围内定量重现了实验光致发光光谱，揭示二次声子耦合（quadratic phonon couplings）在100-150K以上贡献了近一半的均匀线宽（homogeneous linewidth），而非对角耦合导致的激子热化（exciton thermalization）作用较小且仅在接近300K时显现。

Conclusion: 该微观、无参数方法能够准确描述半导体纳米晶体的光致发光光谱，证实二次声子耦合对高温下线宽的主要贡献，而非对角耦合作用有限，为理解激子-声子相互作用机制提供了重要理论工具。

Abstract: We present a microscopic, parameter-free approach for computing the photoluminescence spectra of a single semiconductor nanocrystal. The method derives exciton-phonon coupling directly from the semi-empirical pseudopotential framework and systematically incorporates both diagonal and off-diagonal interactions, expanded to second-order in the phonon modes. The dipole-dipole correlation function was calculated using a Dyson expansion within the Kubo-Toyozawa formalism, enabling a consistent description of the role of pure dephasing and population-transfer on the photoluminescence spectral features. Applied to CdSe/CdS core-shell nanocrystals, the approach quantitatively reproduces experimental photoluminescence spectra over a wide temperature range, revealing that quadratic phonon couplings account for nearly half of the homogeneous linewidth above 100-150 K, while off-diagonal couplings leading to exciton thermalization play only a minor role and only as T approaches 300K.

</details>


### [117] [Molecular Electron Transfer in Optical Cavities: From Excitonic to Vibronic Polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23748)
*Takumi Hidaka,Tomohiro Fukushima,Nguyen Thanh Phuc*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究使用精确的层次运动方程方法，揭示了强耦合腔中电子转移动力学的非微扰和非马尔可夫特征，发现电子转移速率在强耦合区趋于饱和，并识别了由振动-光子耦合引起的三体相互作用导致的非单调振荡行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子激发与光学腔中量子化电磁场的强耦合为调控分子系统的物理化学性质提供了有效手段。研究旨在深入理解腔耦合分子中的电子转移动力学，超越传统微扰理论的局限。

Method: 采用数值精确的层次运动方程方法，该方法能够捕捉非微扰和非马尔可夫效应。进一步扩展了腔修饰电子转移模型，引入了分子电偶极矩的核坐标依赖性。

Result: 识别了与极化激元形成相关的显著共振和集体效应，发现电子转移速率在强耦合区趋于饱和。引入核坐标依赖性后，产生了涉及分子电子、振动自由度和腔光子的三体相互作用，导致电子转移速率对光-物质耦合强度和腔频率呈现非单调振荡依赖关系。

Conclusion: 腔修饰电子转移是一个多通道量子过程，由电子、振动和光子自由度之间的相互作用共同调控。这些发现揭示了量子干涉在多个转移路径中的关键作用。

Abstract: Strong coupling between molecular excitations and quantized electromagnetic fields in optical cavities provides a powerful means to control the physical and chemical properties of molecular systems. Here, we study electron transfer (ET) dynamics in cavity-coupled molecules using the numerically exact hierarchical equations of motion (HEOM) method, which captures nonperturbative and non-Markovian effects beyond standard perturbative theories. We identify distinct resonance and collective effects associated with polariton formation and show that the ET rate saturates in the strong-coupling regime, a feature not captured by perturbative approaches. We further extend the cavity-modified ET model by incorporating the nuclear-coordinate dependence of molecular electric dipole moments, which gives rise to a three-body interaction involving molecular electronic and vibrational degrees of freedom and cavity photons. This vibronic polariton formation leads to non-monotonic, oscillatory dependencies of the ET rate on the light-matter coupling strength and cavity frequency, which we attribute to quantum interference among multiple transfer pathways. These findings establish cavity-modified electron transfer as a multichannel quantum process governed by the interplay of electronic, vibrational, and photonic degrees of freedom.

### [118] [Relativistic Tidal Dissipation and the Gravitational-wave Signal of a White Dwarf Orbiting an Intermediate-Mass Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22688)
*Yang Yang,Leif Lui,Alejandro Torres-Orjuela,Xian Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究开发了白矮星-中等质量黑洞双星系统的完全相对论性潮汐响应模型，发现当黑洞质量超过10^5太阳质量时，潮汐相互作用呈现相对论效应且对黑洞自旋敏感，轨道平均潮汐耗散率可比牛顿预测降低约50%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找中等质量黑洞（IMBHs）并测量其质量和自旋对于理解大质量黑洞形成至关重要。白矮星-中等质量黑洞双星系统同时发射电磁辐射和引力波，提供了独特的多信使探测机会，但现有模型无法捕捉其在强引力场中的相对论动力学。

Method: 开发了白矮星接近中等质量黑洞时的完全相对论性潮汐响应模型，用于研究长期轨道演化及引力波信号。模型特别关注相对论框架旋转对潮汐耗散的影响。

Result: 对于质量超过10^5太阳质量的中等质量黑洞，潮汐相互作用呈现相对论效应且对黑洞自旋敏感。由于相对论框架旋转降低了近心点通道的相位相干性，轨道平均潮汐耗散率可比牛顿预测降低约50%。潮汐耗散导致轨道偏心率更快衰减，近心点距离可能随时间增加，这有助于解释准周期爆发和长期轨道周期增长。

Conclusion: 相对论性潮汐耗散在动力学上具有重要意义，对于可靠预测白矮星-中等质量黑洞系统的多信使信号至关重要。在典型空间观测中，引力波波形失配可在6个月内达到约0.1量级，表明这些效应具有可观测性。

Abstract: Finding intermediate-mass black holes (IMBHs) and measuring their masses and spins are key to understanding massive black hole formation. White dwarf (WD)-IMBH binaries provide a unique probe because they emit both electromagnetic radiation and gravitational waves (GWs), thereby conveying richer information. However, such multi-messenger sources often enter the regime of strong gravity, where existing models fail to capture their relativistic dynamics. Here, we develop a fully relativistic model for the tidal response of a WD close to an IMBH and use it to study the secular orbital evolution as well as the GW signal. We find that for IMBHs more massive than 10^5 solar masses, tidal interaction becomes relativistic and sensitive to IMBH spin. The interaction generally dissipates binary orbital energy and angular momentum, but due to relativistic frame rotation, which reduces phase coherence across pericenter passages, the orbit-averaged tidal dissipation rate can be suppressed by up to about 50% relative to Newtonian predictions. Including tidal dissipation leads to more rapid damping of the orbital eccentricity, to the extent that the pericenter distance may even increase over time, potentially explaining quasi-periodic eruptions and secular orbital period growth. Such tidal effects accumulate into measurable phase and amplitude deviations in the GW signal. For typical space-based observations, the GW waveform mismatch can reach values of order 0.1 within 6 months. Our results indicate that relativistic tidal dissipation is both dynamically important and observationally essential for reliably predicting the multi-messenger signals of WD-IMBH systems.

</details>


### [119] [Realistic Equations of State Informing Neutron Star Post-Merger Gravitational-Wave Frequencies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23646)
*Spencer J. Magnall,Nilaksha Barman,Debarati Chatterjee,Paul D. Lasky,Simon Goode*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究使用相对论平均场模型构建具有一致热效应处理的现实状态方程，计算双中子星并合后残余天体引力波峰值频率分布，发现频率范围约2.5-4 kHz，表明需要kHz敏感度的宽带观测台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双中子星并合产生的高温快速旋转中子星质量远超托尔曼-奥本海默-沃尔科夫质量极限，其引力波辐射为测量地面实验无法达到的密度和温度下的核物质状态方程提供了独特机会。

Method: 采用基于相对论平均场模型（relativistic mean field model）构建的现实状态方程，并保持热效应处理的一致性，计算预期峰值引力波频率分布，同时对状态方程和前身中子星质量进行边缘化处理。

Result: 峰值引力波频率分布范围约为2.5-4 kHz，该分布的宽度表明需要具有kHz敏感度的宽带观测台，并对某些所谓的"并合后优化配置"提出了质疑。研究表明KAGRA高频设计相比宽带设计更适合测量并合后残余天体。

Conclusion: 双中子星并合后残余天体的引力波峰值频率分布支持需要kHz敏感度的宽带引力波观测台，KAGRA高频设计在此类测量中表现出优越性，为未来探测器设计提供了重要参考。

Abstract: Binary neutron star mergers are thought to produce hot, rapidly rotating neutron stars with masses that can far exceed their Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff mass. The gravitational-wave emission from such remnants provides a unique opportunity to measure the nuclear equation of state at densities and temperatures not available to terrestrial experiments. Current detector design is informed by gravitational-wave signals from general relativistic hydrodynamics simulations of neutron star mergers, typically with hybrid thermal treatments for the equation of state, where a cold equation of state is modified by adding a thermal component. We use realistic equations of state based on the relativistic mean field model with consistent treatment of thermal effects to compute the distribution of expected peak gravitational-wave frequencies. Marginalising over equation of state and progenitor neutron star masses, we show the peak frequency of emission ranges from $\sim2.5$ to 4 kHz. The width of this distribution suggests the need for broadband observatories with kHz sensitivity, and calls into question some of the so-called post-merger optimised configurations. We show the proposed KAGRA high-frequency design is well-suited to measuring post-merger remnants when compared to the KAGRA broadband design.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Large liquid argon time projection chambers (LArTPCs) require stable and well-characterized delivery of ultraviolet (UV) light for in situ calibration of photosensors at cryogenic temperatures. Light loss in several fiber types and SMA connectors was measured across wavelengths from \qtyrange{275}{970}{nm}. In addition, light-loss measurements of the tested fibers after several liquid-nitrogen thermal cycles showed no statistically significant degradation relative to baseline measurements, and high-rate pulsed exposure (30-90 million pulses from a \qty{275}{nm} LED) likewise showed no measurable aging in jacketed fibers. A compact, palm-sized, 3D-printed PEEK diffuser housing with stacked UV-grade fused-silica diffusers yields Lambertian emission and the most uniform angular distribution. Optical components exhibiting improved UV transmission were deployed successfully in multiple DUNE small- and large-scale prototypes, demonstrating reliable operation of UV light calibration systems. These findings inform component selection and calibration procedures for achieving reliable, uniform UV light delivery in large-scale cryogenic detectors such as DUNE.

### [122] [A 200 dB Dynamic Range Radiation-Hard Delta-Sigma Current Digitizer for Beam Loss Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24140)
*Luca Giangrande*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种采用标准130纳米CMOS工艺制造的辐射加固电流模式Δ-Σ ADC，该转换器针对高能物理中的束流损失监测应用设计，能够在高达100 Mrad的总电离剂量下工作，并处理跨越九个数量级的输入电流范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在开发适用于高能物理束流损失监测（beam loss monitoring）的辐射加固模数转换器，需要同时满足极端环境下的辐射耐受性、宽动态范围电流测量以及快速响应时间等相互冲突的要求。

Method: 采用电流模式Δ-Σ（delta-sigma）架构，利用分辨率与采集时间之间的固有权衡关系：20 MHz采样的一阶调制器在关键10 μs窗口内为毫安级电流范围提供11位有效分辨率。通过延长积分时间至100秒实现亚皮安级分辨率，并集成了三重冗余数字逻辑和SEU容忍比较器组等辐射加固技术。

Result: 芯片集成了两个独立通道，在1.2 V电源下功耗为25 mW，工作动态范围超过200 dB。100 Mrad辐照后测量显示无性能退化，在1 mA至5 μA范围内未校准积分非线性度保持在满量程的[+0.2%, -0.3%]以内。

Conclusion: 该转换器的灵活性和辐射耐受性使其不仅适用于HL-LHC束流损失监测升级，也适用于其他恶劣环境下的精密电流测量应用，成功解决了高能物理实验中宽动态范围电流监测与快速机器保护的冲突需求。

Abstract: This paper presents a radiation-hardened current-mode delta-sigma ADC fabricated in a standard 130~nm CMOS technology and qualified for total ionizing doses up to 100~Mrad. The converter is designed for beam loss monitoring applications in high-energy physics, where it must handle input currents spanning nine decades, from 1~mA down to 1~pA, while providing a fast 10~\textmu s response time for machine protection. To meet these conflicting requirements, the architecture exploits the inherent trade-off between resolution and acquisition time: a first-order modulator sampled at 20~MHz delivers 11-bit effective resolution within the critical 10~\textmu s window for the mA current range. Extended integration times of up to 100~s enable the sub-picoampere resolution required for beam alignment and background monitoring and provides an operational dynamic range exceeding 200~dB. The chip integrates two independent channels, consumes 25~mW from a 1.2~V supply, and includes radiation-hardening techniques such as triple-redundant digital logic and SEU-tolerant comparator banks. Post-irradiation measurements up to 100~Mrad show no performance degradation, and the uncalibrated integral nonlinearity remains within [+0.2\%, --0.3\%] of full scale over the 1~mA to 5~\textmu A range. The converter's flexibility and radiation tolerance make it suitable not only for the HL-LHC beam loss monitoring upgrade but also for other precision current measurement applications in harsh environments.

</details>

### [123] [Diode Effect May Assist Finding Proper Superconductivity Mechanism in Copper Oxides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23552)
*Armen Gulian,Serafim Teknowijoyo,Vahan Nikoghosyan*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究在零磁场条件下于铜氧化物高温超导体中观测到超导二极管效应，表明时间反演对称性破缺可能是铜酸盐超导态的本征特性，对依赖时间反演对称机制的高温超导理论模型构成重要约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索铜氧化物高温超导体在无外加磁场条件下是否表现出时间反演对称性破缺，这关系到对高温超导机制本质的理解。

Method: 使用Tl₂Ba₂CaCu₂O₈微桥结构，在严格零场条件下于100K温度下测量超导二极管效应，并在高达±100 Oe的磁场范围内验证响应的稳定性。

Result: 在零磁场条件下观测到显著的超导二极管效应，该非互易响应在±100 Oe磁场范围内保持不变，与Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊δ中的零场二极管行为一致。

Conclusion: 时间反演对称性破缺可能是铜酸盐超导态的本征特性，这一发现对依赖时间反演对称机制的高温超导理论模型构成了显著约束。

Abstract: We present measurements demonstrating that copper-oxide high-temperature superconductors can exhibit broken time-reversal symmetry in the absence of external magnetic fields. Using $Tl_{2}Ba_{2}CaCu_{2}O_{8}$ microbridges, we observe a pronounced superconducting diode effect at 100 K under strictly zero-field conditions. This nonreciprocal response remains unchanged in magnetic fields up to $\pm 100 Oe$. Our results are consistent with recent reports of zero-field diode behavior in $Bi_{2}Sr_{2}CaCu_{2}O_{8+δ }$ and together indicate that time-reversal symmetry breaking may be an intrinsic property of the cuprate superconducting state. These findings significantly constrain theoretical models of high-temperature superconductivity that rely on time-reversal-symmetric mechanisms.

</details>


### [124] [High-pressure stabilization of Mg2IrH7: Structural proximity to high-Tc superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23675)
*Shubham Sinha,Wencheng Lu,Mads F. Hansen,Michael J. Hutcheon,Trevor W. Bontke,Lewis J. Conway,Kapildeb Dolui,Chris J. Pickard,Christoph Heil,Piotr A. Guńka,Stella Chariton,Vitali Prakapenka,Liangzi Deng,Ching-Wu Chu,Matthew N. Julian,Rohit P. Prasankumar,Timothy A. Strobel*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: Mg₂IrH₆是一种亚稳态复合金属氢化物，在常压下预测的超导转变温度高达170 K。高压实验发现立方相Mg₂IrH₇在约40 GPa以上稳定存在，该相为绝缘体，并在减压至约20 GPa时回复为立方相Mg₂IrH₅。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Mg₂IrH₆体系的动机在于其作为亚稳态复合金属氢化物，在常压下预测具有高达170 K的超导转变温度。在低压合成同构绝缘体Mg₂IrH₅后，需要通过高压研究探索该体系的相行为和化合物形成。

Method: 采用高压实验方法，包括X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）和拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopic）测量来确定相行为。通过电输运测量（electrical transport measurements）研究材料的电学性质，并与从头计算（ab initio predictions）结果进行对比验证。

Result: 实验结果表明立方相Mg₂IrH₇在约40 GPa以上稳定存在，并与可能成分为Mg₂IrH₅的六方氢化物共存。立方相Mg₂IrH₇为绝缘体，与从头计算结果一致，在室温减压至约20 GPa时回复为立方相Mg₂IrH₅。

Conclusion: 实验结果证实了Mg-Ir-H体系基态结构预测的正确性。两种成分相近的相（Mg₂IrH₇和Mg₂IrH₅）的形成，为通过非平衡处理途径获得超导Mg₂IrH₆开辟了新的机会。

Abstract: Mg$_2$IrH$_6$ is a metastable complex metal hydride with a predicted superconducting transition temperature as high as 170 K at ambient pressure. Following the synthesis of isomorphic, insulating Mg$_2$IrH$_5$ at low pressure, higher-pressure studies were conducted to investigate the phase behavior and compound formation in this system. X-ray diffraction and Raman spectroscopic measurements indicate that cubic Mg$_2$IrH$_7$ is stabilized above ca. 40 GPa and coexists with a related hexagonal hydride with likely composition near Mg$_2$IrH$_5$. Electrical transport measurements show that the cubic Mg$_2$IrH$_7$ is insulating, in agreement with ab initio predictions, and persists during room-temperature decompression until $\sim$20 GPa before reverting back to the cubic Mg$_2$IrH$_5$. The experimental results confirm ground-state structure predictions in the Mg-Ir-H system, and the formation of two nearly identical phases with surrounding compositions opens new opportunities to access superconducting Mg$_2$IrH$_6$ through non-equilibrium processing pathways.

### [125] [Intrinsic translational symmetry-breaking charge stripes in underdoped iron pnictides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23680)
*Qiang-Jun Cheng,Cong-Cong Lou,Yong-Wei Wang,Ze-Xian Deng,Xu-Cun Ma,Qi-Kun Xue,Can-Li Song*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 在铁基超导体Ca(Fe1-xCox)2As2薄膜中首次观测到单向电荷条纹序（charge-stripe order），该相介于向列相（nematic phase）与最佳掺杂超导相之间，其局域和全局抑制均能增强超导性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管电荷序在铜氧化物超导体中已得到充分确认，但在铁基超导体中尚未明确识别出本征的平移对称性破缺电荷序。本研究旨在探索铁基超导体中是否存在类似的电荷有序相及其与超导性的关系。

Method: 采用光谱成像扫描隧道显微镜（spectroscopic-imaging scanning tunneling microscopy）技术，对外延生长的Ca(Fe1-xCox)2As2（x = 0 ~ 0.055）薄膜进行观测，研究欠掺杂区域中的电荷有序现象。

Result: 在欠掺杂区域观测到单向的、近公度的电荷条纹序，沿反铁磁Fe-Fe键方向排列。该电荷序伴随着费米能级附近的范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularity），源于反铁磁和向列关联共同驱动的费米面重构。电荷条纹不稳定的局域和全局抑制均可增强超导性，可通过外延应变和Co掺杂进行调控。

Conclusion: 研究确立了电荷条纹序作为铁基超导体中的中间电子相，揭示了从向列性（nematicity）到超导性的相干路径。这些发现强调了电荷有序是不同高温超导体家族中的统一要素。

Abstract: Despite being well established in cuprates, an intrinsic translational symmetry-breaking charge order has not been clearly identified in iron-based superconductors. Using spectroscopic-imaging scanning tunneling microscopy on epitaxial Ca(Fe1-xCox)2As2 (x = 0 ~ 0.055) thin films, we observe smectic, near-commensurate charge-stripe order in the underdoped regime that intervenes between the nematic parent phase and optimally doped superconductivity. Distinct from the bidirectional checkerboard-like order in cuprates, these charge stripes are unidirectional along the antiferromagnetic Fe-Fe bond direction and are accompanied by a van Hove singularity near the Fermi level, inherited from the Fermi surface reconstruction driven by intertwined antiferromagnetic and nematic correlations. Both local and global suppression of the charge-stripe instability enhance superconductivity, tunable via epitaxial strain and Co doping. These results establish charge-stripe order as an intermediate electronic phase in iron pnictides and reveal a coherent pathway from nematicity to superconductivity. Our findings highlight charge ordering as a unifying element across different families of high-temperature superconductors.

</details>


### [126] [Inverse Isotope Effect in the Ternary Perovskite Hydride SrPdH/D$_{2.9}$: A Signature of Quantum Zero-Point Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23691)
*Wencheng Lu,Mihir Sahoo,Roman Lucrezi,Michael J. Hutcheon,Shubham Sinha,Pedro N. Ferreira,Chris J. Pickard,Qiang Zhang,Matthew N. Julian,Rohit P. Prasankumar,Christoph Heil,Timothy A. Strobel*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 基于第一性原理计算指导，在低压条件下合成了三元钙钛矿氢化物SrPdH₃₋ₓ并发现其超导性。中子衍射结构表征显示近化学计量比组成SrPdD₂.₉(₂)，超导转变温度分别为T_c = 2.1 K（H）和T_c = 2.2 K（D），表现出反常同位素效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过理论指导发现新型低压氢化物超导体，扩展实验实现的三元氢化物超导体家族，并验证量子核运动对准确理论处理低压氢化物超导体的重要性。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）指导材料设计，在低压条件下合成三元钙钛矿氢化物SrPdH₃₋ₓ。通过中子衍射（neutron diffraction）进行结构表征，并结合输运测量（transport measurements）和磁化率测量（magnetic susceptibility measurements）研究超导性质。

Result: 实验证实SrPdH₃₋ₓ具有超导性，超导转变温度分别为T_c = 2.1 K（氢化物）和T_c = 2.2 K（氘化物），表现出反常同位素效应（inverse isotope effect）。第一性原理计算将这一效应主要归因于量子零点运动（quantum zero-point motion）。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了钙钛矿氢化物结构原型中的超导性，扩展了实验实现的三元氢化物超导体家族。理论与实验在热力学稳定性和超导性质方面的良好一致性，为理论指导的超导体发现提供了重要验证，并证明了量子核运动对准确理论处理低压氢化物超导体的重要性。

Abstract: Guided by first-principles calculations, we demonstrate superconductivity in the ternary perovskite hydride SrPdH$_{3-x}$, synthesized at low pressure. Structural characterization via neutron diffraction reveals the near-stoichiometric composition SrPdD$_{2.9(2)}$ with 96\% deuterium site occupancy. Subsequent transport and magnetic susceptibility measurements establish onset superconducting transitions at $T_\text{c} = \SI{2.1}{K} $ (H) and $T_\text{c} = \SI{2.2}{K} $ (D), exhibiting an inverse isotope effect that our first-principles calculations attribute predominantly to quantum zero-point motion. The excellent agreement between theory and experiment with respect to thermodynamic stability and superconducting properties provides important validation for theory-guided superconductor discovery. This work establishes superconductivity in the perovskite hydride structural prototype -- expanding the limited family of experimentally realized ternary hydride superconductors -- and demonstrates the importance of quantum nuclear motion on the accurate theoretical treatment of low-pressure hydride superconductors.

</details>


### [127] [Unveiling the superconducting scenario in multiphase superconductor CeRh$_2$As$_2$ from space-group symmetry analysis and DFT calculations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23726)
*V. G. Yarzhemsky,E. A. Teplyakov,S. V. Eremeev,E. V. Chulkov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了CeRh₂As₂超导体中磁场诱导的奇偶性转变机制，提出在保持三重态（triplet）自旋多重性的前提下，通过对称性变化实现从低场偶宇称态到高场奇宇称态的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CeRh₂As₂超导体因在磁场下存在两个超导相（其中一个超过泡利-克洛格斯顿极限）而备受关注。传统理论将这种场诱导转变描述为单重态-三重态转变，但同一化合物同时展现两种自旋配对态并不常见。本文旨在探索在不改变自旋多重性的情况下，超导态对称性变化的可能性。

Method: 基于安德森配对函数（Anderson pair functions）构建超导序参量，考虑点群D₄h和磁群4/mm'm'对称性下的相位缠绕。分析了非简单空间群结构导致的非平凡库珀配对，特别是在费米面与布里渊区边界相交的情况。通过精确的密度泛函理论计算研究了能带结构。

Result: 发现具有E₁u'⁺对称性的两个三重态（反自旋配对和等自旋配对态）是无节点的，但具有不同的内部结构，可能分别对应低场和高场相。在X点处，三重态对是偶宇称的，而单重态对可以是偶宇称或奇宇称的。此外，在X点处，通过晶格平移连接的原子中心处相位改变π的配对密度波也是可能的。

Conclusion: 密度泛函理论计算揭示了Ce 4f电子对费米能级态的贡献，表明奇偶性转变可以在布里渊区对称点处的三重态场景中发生，即无需改变自旋多重性即可实现对称性转变。

Abstract: Despite of the low transition temperature, the recently identified superconductor CeRh$_2$As$_2$ has garnered significant interest due to its unique symmetry and magnetic characteristics, particularly the existence of two superconducting (SC) phases under a magnetic field, one of which exceeds the Pauli-Clogston limit. The field-induced transition from a low-field even-parity state to a high-field odd-parity state is usually described as a singlet-triplet transition. However, it is uncommon for a single compound to exhibit both triplet and singlet SC scenarios. The aim of this paper is to investigate the possibilities of symmetry changes in the SC state without a change of spin multiplicity. To this end, we construct the SC order parameter based on Anderson pair functions, considering the phase winding within the symmetry of the point group $D_{4h}$ and the magnetic group $4/mm^{\prime }m^{\prime}$. It was found that two triplets with opposite-spin and equal-spin pairing states of symmetry $E_{1u}^{\prime +}$, are nodeless but exhibit distinct internal structures and may be associated with low-and high-field phases. Additionally, nontrivial Cooper pairing resulting from the non-symmorphic structure of the space group was examined, particularly in the case where the Fermi surface intersects with the boundaries of a Brillouin zone (BZ). It was determined that at the X point, triplet pairs are even, while singlet pairs can be either even or odd. Furthermore, at the X point, pair density waves that alter phase by $π$ at the atomic centers linked by lattice translations are also feasible. To explore the possibility of such scenarios, precise DFT calculations of the band structure were performed, revealing the contribution of Ce $4f$ electrons to the states at the Fermi level. Thus, the even-odd transition can take place in a triplet scenario at symmetry points of a BZ.

</details>


### [128] [Reply to "Threefold error in the reported zero-field cooled magnetic moment of single crystal $La_2SmNi_2O_7$ (arXiv: 2602.23240)"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23842)
*Feiyu Li,Zhenfang Xing,Di Peng,Jie Dou,Ning Guo,Liang Ma,Yulin Zhang,Lingzhen Wang,Jun Luo,Jie Yang,Jian Zhang,Tieyan Chang,Yu-Sheng Chen,Weizhao Cai,Jinguang Cheng,Yuzhu Wang,Yuxin Liu,Tao Luo,Naohisa Hirao,Takahiro Matsuoka,Hirokazu Kadobayashi,Zhidan Zeng,Qiang Zheng,Rui Zhou,Qiaoshi Zeng,Xutang Tao,Junjie Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文回应了Korolev和Talantsev对Li等人Nature论文中超导相分数（superconducting phase fraction）计算的批评，通过三个主要论点反驳其质疑，并确认原始研究的计算方法是有效的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在回应Korolev和Talantsev对Li等人在Nature 649, 871-878 (2026)中报道的超导相分数（superconducting phase fraction）计算的批评，澄清相关争议并维护原始研究的有效性。

Method: 通过三个关键论据进行反驳：首先确认低温尾部微弱上升源于背景信号而非顺磁迈斯纳效应（paramagnetic Meissner effect）；其次指出退磁效应（demagnetization effect）应基于实际测量的磁矩作为相分数的函数计算；最后强调样品为高质量块状单晶（bulk single crystal），排除了多个离散超导区域存在的可能性。

Result: 分析表明Korolev和Talantsev将退磁场视为常数，导致其计算的超导相分数低估了约(1-Nχ_{meas})(1-N)倍（约1/3），这解释了其结果与原始研究相差近三倍的原因。原始研究的计算方法和结论未被质疑所动摇。

Conclusion: Li等人在Nature 649, 871-878 (2026)中报告的超导相分数计算并未被Korolev等人在arXiv:2602.23240 (2026)中提出的分析所否定，原始研究的方法和结论仍然有效。

Abstract: We respond to the critique by Aleksandr V. Korolev and Evgeny F. Talantsev on the superconducting phase fraction ($f$) calculations in Li et al. Nature 649, 871-878 (2026). First, the weak upturn in the low-temperature tail of our data has been confirmed to originate from the background, and the paramagnetic Meissner effect is absent in our case; thus, field-cooled (FC) data can be used for superconducting phase fraction calculations. Second, demagnetization effect must be calculated based on the actual measured moment as a function of $f$, which has been well-established and routinely employed in the superconductivity community. In contrast, Korolev and Talantsev treated the demagnetization field as a constant; thus, their calculation underestimates $f$ by a factor of $(1-Nχ_{meas})(1-N)$. This factor is close to 1/3, given $N$ = 0.849, $χ_{meas}$ = -1.313 in our study, which explains the origin of their deviated result (nearly three times smaller than our results). Third, our sample is a homogeneous high-quality bulk single crystal, evidenced by various techniques, making the existence of multiple discrete superconducting regions highly unlikely. We conclude that the superconducting phase fraction calculations reported in Li et al. Nature 649, 871-878 (2026) are not invalidated by the analyses presented in Korolev et al. arXiv: 2602.23240 (2026).

</details>


### [129] [Superconductivity in the A15-type V3(Os1-2xSixGex) medium-entropy alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24028)
*Yucheng Li,Kuan Li,Lingyong Zeng,Rui Chen,Jingjun Qin,Shuangyue Wang,Huixia Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究设计并合成了一系列新型A15型中/高熵合金超导体V3(Os1-2xSixGex)，通过电阻率、磁化率和比热测量证实其为II型体超导体，超导转变温度随Os浓度降低而升高，且V3(Os0.333Si0.333Ge0.333)的上临界场超过泡利极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 立方A15型超导合金在低温超导应用中占据主要市场并展现奇特物理性质，而中/高熵合金（MEAs-HEAs）因其高机械硬度和优异辐照耐受性可在极端条件下稳定使用。本研究旨在结合A15型超导体与中/高熵合金的特性，设计新型超导材料。

Method: 采用电弧熔炼（arc melting）方法合成了一系列先前未报道的A15型V3(Os1-2xSixGex)中/高熵合金超导体（x = 0.333, 0.375, 0.425）。通过电阻率（resistivity）、磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）和比热（specific heat）测量来表征其超导性质。

Result: 所有样品均为II型体超导体（type-II bulk superconductors）。超导转变温度（superconducting transition temperature, Tc）随Os浓度系统性降低而呈现上升趋势。V3(Os0.333Si0.333Ge0.333)样品的上临界场（upper critical field）超过泡利极限（Pauli limit），表明其可能因重Os原子诱导的自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）而具有强抗磁场能力。

Conclusion: 这些发现不仅推进了对熵稳定A15型合金中涌现现象的理解，还扩展了新型超导体的成员。该研究展示了结合A15型超导体与中/高熵合金特性的成功策略，为开发具有优异性能的超导材料提供了新途径。

Abstract: Cubic A15-type superconducting alloys continue to fascinate the academic and industrial fields because they mainly support the largest market for low-temperature superconducting applications and show exotic physical properties. Medium-/high-entropy alloys (MEAs-HEAs) can be employed stably under extreme conditions due to their high mechanical hardness and excellent irradiation tolerance. Combining with the features of the A15-type superconductor and MEAs-HEAs, we design a series of previously unreported A15-type V3(Os1-2xSixGex) (x = 0.333, 0.375, 0.425) MEA superconductors, which can be obtained by an arc melting method. Resistivity, magnetic susceptibility, and specific heat measurements indicate that all of them are type-II bulk superconductors. The superconducting transition temperature (Tc) exhibits an upward trend with the systematic reduction of Os concentration. Additionally, the upper critical field of the V3(Os0.333Si0.333Ge0.333) sample is larger than the Pauli limit, suggesting it may be robust against magnetic fields due to spin-orbit coupling induced by the heavy Os atoms. These findings not only advance our understanding of emergent phenomena in entropy-stabilized A15-type alloys but also expand the members of new superconductors.

</details>


### [130] [Highly-linear flux-to-voltage transducer based on superconducting quantum interference proximity transistors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24075)
*Angelo Greco,Giorgio De Simoni,Francesco Giazotto*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超导量子干涉器件（SQUIDs）因其固有的非线性周期传输函数而存在根本性限制，而磁通锁定环（FLL）配置虽能缓解此问题，却引入了电子复杂性和带宽约束，阻碍了量子电路的可扩展性。

Method: 研究团队开发了bi-SQUIPT（双环超导量子干涉晶体管），这是一种通过邻近效应超导弱连接调制态密度的磁通量传感器。该器件采用双环架构和差分读出，能够抵消单个元件典型的非线性特性。

Result: 实验测量显示电压摆幅约为120 μV，无杂散动态范围（SFDR）高达60 dB，与理论预测一致且与SQUID阵列相当，同时功耗保持在飞瓦量级。器件在高达600 mK温度下表现出卓越的操作稳定性。

Conclusion: bi-SQUIPT通过消除非线性限制同时保持低功耗和高稳定性，成为高密度低温量子电子学的使能技术，为量子电路的可扩展性提供了有前景的解决方案。

Abstract: Superconducting quantum interference devices (SQUIDs) are state-of-the-art in ultra-sensitive magnetometry; however, conventional SQUID devices are fundamentally limited by the inherently nonlinear and periodic nature of their transfer function. Although flux-locked loop (FLL) configurations can mitigate this issue, they introduce electronic complexity and bandwidth constraints that hinder scalability in quantum circuits. In this work, we present an experimental demonstration of the bi-SQUIPT, a flux transducer that modulates the density of states in a proximitized superconducting weak link. The device employs a dual-loop architecture with differential readout, which enables cancellation of non-linearities typical of individual elements, achieving a voltage swing of approximately 120 $μ$V. Measurements yield a spurious-free dynamic range (SFDR) of up to 60 dB, consistent with theoretical predictions and comparable to that of SQUID arrays, while maintaining power dissipation in the femtowatt range. The results further highlight a remarkable operational stability up to 600 mK, positioning the bi-SQUIPT as an enabling technology for high-density cryogenic quantum electronics.

### [131] [A Kapitza Pendulum Route to Supercurrent Tunnel Diodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24198)
*Yuriy Yerin,Stefan-Ludwig Drechsler,A. A. Varlamov,Francesco Giazotto,Jeroen van den Brink,Mario Cuoco*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于参数驱动的超导二极管新机制，通过频率调制的超流振幅在电流-相位关系中产生有效高阶非谐项，利用卡皮查摆的数学等价性动态打破互易性，实现了无需磁性或自旋轨道耦合的非互易超流传输。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导二极管作为支持非互易超流传输的非耗散电路元件具有吸引力，但传统约瑟夫森隧道结本质上是互易的。现有打破互易性的方法通常涉及磁性或自旋轨道耦合，这增加了器件复杂性并限制了可重复性。

Method: 通过施加频率调制的超流振幅，在电流-相位关系（current-phase relation）中产生有效高阶非谐项。利用与卡皮查摆（Kapitza pendulum）的数学等价性，这些项动态地打破互易性，建立了卡皮查超流二极管（Kapitza supercurrent diode）的概念。

Result: 证明了非互易超导传输可以通过非平衡驱动常规约瑟夫森隧道结来实现。提出了卡皮查超流二极管的两种实现方案：通过门控超导干涉仪或磁通驱动的双环SQUID，在实验可及频率ω/2π∼1-10 GHz范围内实现非互易超流传输。

Conclusion: 本文展示了一种基于参数驱动的超流非互易性替代动态路径，为超导电子学提供了一种不依赖磁性或自旋轨道耦合的非互易超导二极管新方案。

Abstract: Superconducting diodes that support nonreciprocal supercurrent flow in principle constitute attractive, non-dissipative, circuit elements for superconducting electronics. But their realization faces fundamental challenges, as conventional Josephson tunnel junctions are inherently reciprocal. Existing approaches to break reciprocity typically involve magnetism or spin-orbit coupling, which often increase device complexity and limit reproducibility. Here, we demonstrate an alternative dynamical route to supercurrent nonreciprocity based on parametric driving. By applying a frequency-modulated supercurrent amplitude we show that effective higher-order, nonharmonic terms are generated in the current-phase relation. Leveraging mathematical equivalences with the Kapitza pendulum, we show that these terms dynamically break reciprocity. This establishes the concept of a Kapitza supercurrent diode and demonstrates that nonreciprocal superconducting transport can be engineered by nonequilibrium driving conventional Josephson tunnel junctions. We propose two implementations of the Kapitza supercurrent diode - via gate-controlled superconducting interferometers or flux-driven double-loop SQUIDs - to achieve nonreciprocal supercurrent transport within experimentally accessible frequencies $ω/2π\sim 1$-$10\,\mathrm{GHz}$.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究通过理论分析探讨Aharonov-Bohm（AB）通量对磁性金刚石链（magnetic diamond chains）中交换耦合的影响，重点关注通量诱导的磁耦合放大效应及其与平带量子度规（quantum metric）的关联。

Result: 最显著的结果是AB通量诱导的短距离磁耦合显著放大，导致磁振子（magnons）热导率大幅增加。研究还表明，通量依赖的耦合衰减长度与平带的量子度规相关。

Conclusion: 这些结果对自旋电子器件中磁性的控制具有重要意义，并对量子技术中纳米尺度磁振子热输运具有相关性，为平带磁性系统中的新奇现象提供了理论见解。

Abstract: The physics in flat bands has emerged as an essential field in condensed matter physics where a plethora of phenomena can be unveiled, such as anomalous transport properties, superconductivity dominated by quantum geometry or exotic topological phases. Our goal here is to show that even in magnetic systems, the presence of flat bands can give rise to unexpected features. More precisely, we address the impact of an Aharonov-Bohm (AB) flux on the exchange couplings in magnetic diamond chains. The most remarkable result is the significant amplification of magnetic couplings at short distances induced by the AB flux, leading to a considerable increase in the thermal conductivity of the magnons. We have also shown that the flux-dependent decaying length of the couplings is connected to the quantum metric of the flat bands. Our results could be of interest for the control of magnetic properties in spintronic devices and relevant for the heat transport by magnons at the nanoscale in quantum technologies.

### [133] [Real-Time Formation of a Landau Polaron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24113)
*Priya Nagpal,Arnab Ghosh,Helene Seiler,Samuel Palato,Patanjali Kambhampati*

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个微观线形框架，将集体晶格极化的增长与相干多维光谱中反对角线宽度的演化联系起来，揭示了极化子形成的实时特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极化子（polarons）是电子激发与自洽晶格畸变耦合的准粒子，但其形成过程尚未在实时尺度上直接观测。研究旨在建立连接集体晶格极化增长与光谱线宽演化的理论框架。

Method: 开发了一个微观线形框架（microscopic lineshape framework），将集体晶格极化的增长与相干多维光谱（coherent multidimensional spectroscopy）中反对角线宽度（anti-diagonal linewidth）在布居时间（population-time）上的演化联系起来。该形式主义将反对角线宽度直接关联于晶格频率-频率相关性的衰减。

Result: 欠阻尼声子环境产生振荡性线宽调制，而过阻尼集体极化动力学则产生单调指数展宽。将该框架应用于钙钛矿量子点（perovskite quantum dots）的多维测量，观察到约150飞秒的指数性反对角展宽，反映了集体极化序参数的衰减。

Conclusion: 反对角线宽动力学可作为朗道极化子（Landau polaron）形成的直接实时特征。该研究建立了连接光谱线宽演化与极化子形成动力学的微观框架，为实时观测集体晶格极化过程提供了新方法。

Abstract: Polarons are electronic excitations dressed by a self-consistent lattice distortion, yet their formation has not been directly resolved in real time. We develop a microscopic lineshape framework that connects the growth of a collective lattice polarization to the population-time evolution of the anti-diagonal linewidth in coherent multidimensional spectroscopy. Within this formalism, the anti-diagonal linewidth directly tracks the decay of lattice frequency-frequency correlations. Underdamped phonon environments produce oscillatory linewidth modulation, whereas overdamped collective polarization dynamics generate monotonic exponential broadening. Applying this framework to multidimensional measurements on perovskite quantum dots, we show that the observed approximately 150 femtosecond exponential anti-diagonal broadening reflects the decay of a collective polarization order parameter. These results establish anti-diagonal linewidth dynamics as a direct real-time signature of Landau polaron formation.

### [134] [An exactly solvable evaporation-deposition PCA with long-distance interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.23837)
*Arvind Ayyer,Moumanti Podder*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维周期性边界条件下具有蒸发-沉积机制的随机元胞自动机（PCA），建立了马尔可夫链的遍历性，给出了极限分布、配分函数和密度的显式公式，并提出了可逆性的充要条件。对于m=2的特殊情况，提供了模型的自由能解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究一维周期性边界条件下具有特定蒸发-沉积机制的随机元胞自动机（probabilistic cellular automaton, PCA）模型。该模型涉及两种类型的概率性状态转换，关注其马尔可夫链的遍历性、极限分布和可逆性条件。

Method: 研究采用随机元胞自动机（PCA）框架，在一维周期性边界条件的格点上定义具有两种概率性转换规则的离散时间马尔可夫链。方法包括分析马尔可夫链的遍历性、推导极限分布和配分函数的显式公式，以及建立可逆性的充要条件。

Result: 证明了所得离散时间马尔可夫链是遍历的（ergodic），并给出了其极限分布、配分函数（partition function）和密度的显式公式。提出了马尔可夫链可逆性的必要充分条件。特别地，对于m=2的情况，提供了该模型自由能（free energy）的完全解析表达式。

Conclusion: 该研究成功分析了一维蒸发-沉积随机元胞自动机模型的动力学特性，建立了完整的数学框架来描述其统计力学性质，包括遍历性、极限分布和可逆性条件，为m=2情况提供了精确的解析解。

Abstract: We consider a probabilistic cellular automaton (PCA) of evaporation-deposition on the one-dimensional lattice having $n$ sites with periodic boundary conditions, in which each site, during each epoch, can be in one of two states: $0$ and $1$. Fix a positive integer $m\geqslant 2$. There are two types of transitions at each discrete time, which are as follows: (i) the first site in every contiguous block of $m$ $0$s becomes a $1$ with probability $p_1$, and (ii) the first site in every contiguous block of $(m-1)$ $0$s followed immediately by a $1$ also becomes a $1$ with probability $(1-p_2)$. As in a PCA, all of these transitions occur simultaneously. We show that the resulting discrete-time Markov chain is ergodic, and we give an explicit formula for its limiting distribution, the partition function and the density. We also propose necessary and sufficient conditions for this Markov chain to be reversible. For $m=2$, we provide a fully analytical expression for the free energy of this model.

*Sunil Chhita,Duncan Dauvergne,Thomas Finn*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 证明高度函数在边界处收敛于Airy表面（Airy surface）与独立同分布噪声场（i.i.d. noise field）的独立和，其波动由全平面光滑相（full-plane smooth phase）控制；同时证明Temperleyan骨干路径族收敛于Airy线系综（Airy line ensemble）。

Conclusion: 该研究首次实现了无向路径族向Airy线系综的收敛，并在噪声边界处获得了Airy收敛结果，为理解随机铺砌模型的边界行为提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We study the rough-smooth boundary in the two-periodic Aztec diamond, a random domino tiling model exhibiting three types of macroscopic regions. We show that the height function at this boundary converges to an independent sum of an Airy surface and an i.i.d. noise field with fluctuations governed by the full-plane smooth phase. Going further, we prove convergence of a family of Temperleyan backbone paths to the Airy line ensemble. This gives the first convergence result for a family of undirected paths converging to the Airy line ensemble, as well as Airy convergence at a noisy boundary.

### [136] [Fulde-Ferrell superfluids in an asymmetric three-component Fermi Gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24006)
*Yuhan Lu,Lihong Zhou,Yongping Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过系统分析非对称三组分费米气体中的热力学势全局极小值，揭示了一类新型复合Fulde-Ferrell超流体，其关键特征在于强自旋轨道耦合在动量空间下带中产生双阱结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非对称三组分费米气体同时引入了自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和粒子数不平衡（population imbalance）两种机制，已知这两种机制能够稳定Fulde-Ferrell超流体。研究旨在系统探索此类系统中的超流体特性。

Method: 通过寻找热力学势（thermodynamic potential）的全局极小值，系统研究非对称三组分费米气体中的Fulde-Ferrell超流体。该系统在第一和第二组分间存在拉曼诱导的自旋轨道耦合，而仅在第一和第三组分间存在接触相互作用。

Result: 当强自旋轨道耦合在动量空间的下自旋轨道耦合带（lower spin-orbit-coupled band）中产生双阱结构（double-well structure）时，揭示了一类新型复合Fulde-Ferrell超流体（composite Fulde-Ferrell superfluids），并识别了这些复合超流体的关键特征。

Conclusion: 研究发现了在特定条件下（强自旋轨道耦合导致动量空间双阱结构）出现的新型复合Fulde-Ferrell超流体，扩展了对多组分费米系统中超流体相的理解。

Abstract: An asymmetric three-component Fermi gas, featuring Raman-induced spin-orbit coupling between the first and second components and contact interaction only between the first and third components, introduces both spin-orbit coupling and population imbalance-two mechanisms known to stabilize the Fulde-Ferrell superfluids.We systematically study Fulde-Ferrell superfluids in an asymmetric three-component Fermi gas by finding the global minima of the thermodynamic potential. We reveal a new class of composite Fulde-Ferrell superfluids that emerges when strong spin-orbit coupling generates a double-well structure in momentum space within the lower spin-orbit-coupled band. The key features of these composite superfluids are identified.

### [137] [Effective Three-Boson Interactions using a Separable Potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.24226)
*Corinne Beckers,Jacques Tempere,Jeff Maki,Denise Ahmed-Braun*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究推导并求解了可分离势（separable potentials）下的三体散射振幅积分方程，在强相互作用区域获得了非弹性散射的已知解析形式，并提出了弹性三体散射的新标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）通常使用零程接触势描述两体相互作用，但在扩展到三体过程时，由于缺乏内禀长度尺度会导致发散。虽然可以通过引入零程三体相互作用并重整化来解决，但当两体势具有有限范围（如可分离势）时，则无需此类重整化。

Method: 本研究推导了可分离势（separable potentials）下的三体散射振幅积分方程，并在强相互作用区域（strongly-interacting regime）求解该方程。

Result: 通过该模型，研究恢复了非弹性散射过程（inelastic scattering processes）散射振幅的已知解析形式，并提出了弹性三体散射过程（elastic three-body scattering processes）的新标度律（new scaling law）。

Conclusion: 对于具有有限范围的两体势（如可分离势），无需引入零程三体相互作用进行重整化，即可直接处理三体散射问题，并在强相互作用区域获得解析结果和新标度关系。

Abstract: Effective field theories (EFTs) are widely used to study many-body systems by describing two-body interactions using zero-ranged contact potentials. However, when extended to three-body processes, these contact interactions lead to divergences due to the absence of an intrinsic length scale. In EFT, this is typically resolved by introducing a zero-ranged three-body interaction, which can be renormalized to make the low-energy physics independent of the short-distance physics. However, when the two-body potential has a finite range, such as in separable potentials, there is no need for such renormalization. In this work, we derive the integral equation for the three-body scattering amplitude for separable potentials, and solve it in the strongly-interacting regime. With our model, we retrieve the known analytic form of the scattering amplitude for inelastic scattering processes and formulate a new scaling law for elastic three-body scattering processes.

</details>
